      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā abbhañjanadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Abbhañjanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ 
  
     Supaṭadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Divāvihārā nikkhanto vipassi lokanāyako 
 Lahuṃ supaṭakaṃ  katvā kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe supaṭakaṃ adāsahaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi supaṭassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
   Padhānaṃ payitantaṃ ta machasaṃ 
   Isiṃ syā 
   Supaṭikaṃ syā suppaṭaṃ     
  
                   
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā supaṭadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Supaṭadāyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ 
  
     Daṇḍadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Kānanaṃ vananemāgayha veḷuṃ chetvānahaṃ tadā 
 Ālambanaṃ karitvāna saṅghassa adadiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Tena cittappasādena subbate abhivādiya 
 Ālambadaṇḍaṃ datvāna pakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho 
  
      Catunavute                   ito kappe yaṃ daṇḍa madadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi daṇḍadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā daṇḍadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Daṇḍadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ 
  
     Girinelapūjakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Migaluddo pure āsiṃ vipine vicaraṃ ahaṃ 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddha sabbadhammānapāraguṃ 
  
      Tasmiṃ mahākāruṇike sabbasathite rate 
 Pasannacitto sumano nelapupphamapūjayiṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā girinela pūjako thero imā gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Girinesapūjakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ 
  
     Bodhisammajjakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Ahaṃ pure bodhipattaṃ ujjhitaṃ vetiyaṅgaṇe 
 Taṃ gahetvāna chaḍḍesiṃ alabhiṃ vīsati guṇe 
  
      Tassa kammassa tejena saṃsaranto bhavābhave 
 Duve bhave saṃsarāmi devatte cāpi mānuse 
  
      Devalokā cavitvāna āgantvā mānusaṃ bhavaṃ 
 Duve kule pajāyāmi khattiye cāpi mānuse 
  
      Aṅgapaccaṅgasampanno ārohapariṇahavā 
 Abhirūpo suci homi sampuṇṇaṅgo anūnako 
      Devaloke manusse vā jāto vā yattha katthaci 
 Bhave suvaṇṇavaṇṇova uttattakanakūpamo 
  
      Mudukā                   maddavā saniddhā  sukhumā sukumārikā 
 Chavi me sabbadā hoti bodhipatte suchaḍḍite 
      Yato kutoci gatisu sarīre samudāgate 
 Na limpati rajojallaṃ vipāko pattachaḍḍane   
  
      Uṇhe vātātape tassa aggitāpena vā puna  
 Gatte sedā na muccanti vipāko pattachaḍḍane 
  
      Kuṭṭhaṃ gaṇḍo kilāso ca tilakā piḷakā tathā 
 Na honti kāye daddū ca vipāko pattachaḍḍane 
  
   Mudumaddavā siniddhā syā 
   Pattachaḍḍhite  sabbattha  machasaṃ 
   Pana machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Aparampi guṇaṃ tassa nibbattati bhavābhave 
 Rogā na honti kāyasmiṃ vipāko pattachaḍḍane 
  
      Aparampi guṇaṃ tassa nibbattati bhavābhave 
 Na hoti cittajā pīḷā vipāko pattachaḍḍane 
  
      Aparampi guṇaṃ tassa nibbattati bhavābhave 
 Amittā na bhavantassa vipāko pattachaḍḍane 
  
      Aparampi guṇaṃ tassa nibbattati bhavābhave 
 Anūnabhogo bhavati vipāko pattachaḍḍane 
  
      Aparampi guṇaṃ tassa nibbattati bhavābhave 
 Aggirājuhi corehi na hoti udake bhayaṃ 
  
      Aparampi guṇaṃ tassa nibbattati bhavābhave 
 Dāsidāsā anuvarā honti cittānuvattakā 
  
      Yamhi āyuppamāṇamhi jāyate mānuse bhave 
 Tato na hāyate āyu tiṭṭhate yāvatāyukaṃ 
  
      Abbhantarā bāhirā ca  negamā ca saraṭṭhakā 
 Anuyuttā  honti sabbe vuddhikāmā sukhicchakā 
  
      Bhogavā yasavā homi sirimā ñātipakkhavā 
 Apetabhayasantāso bhavehaṃ sabbato bhave 
  
      Devā manussā asurā gandhabbā yakkharakkhasā 
 Sabbe te parirakkhanti bhave saṃsarato sadā 
  
      Devaloke manusse ca anubhotvā ubho yase 
 Avasānena ca nibbānaṃ sivaṃ patto anuttaraṃ 
  
      Sambuddhamuddisitvāna bodhiṃ vā tassa satthuno 
 Yo puññaṃ pasave poso tassa kiṃ nāma dullabhaṃ 
  
      Magge phale āgame ca jhānābhiññāguṇesu ca 
 Aññosaṃ adhiko hutvā nibbāyāmi anāsavo 
  
   Abbhantarā ca bāhirā machasaṃ 
   Nuyuttā machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Purehaṃ bodhiyā pattaṃ chaḍḍetvā haṭṭhamānaso 
 Imehi vīsataṅgehi samaṅgi homi sabbadā 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bodhisammajjako thero imā gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Bodhisammajjakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ 
  
     Āmaṇḍaphaladāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragū 
 Vuṭṭhahitvā samādhimhā caṅkami lokanāyako 
  
      Khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna āharanto phalaṃ tadā 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ caṅkamantaṃ mahāmuniṃ 
  
      Pasannacitto sumano sire katvāna añjaliṃ 
 Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā āmaṇḍamadadiṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi āmaṇḍassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā āmaṇḍaphaladāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Āmaṇḍaphaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Sugandhatthorāpadānaṃ 
  
      Imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma gottena  uppajji vadataṃvaro 
  
      Anuvyañjanasampanno  battisaṃvaralakkhaṇo 
 Byāmappabhāparivuto raṃsujālasamosaṭo  
  
      Assāsetā yathā cando suriyova pabhaṅkaro 
 Nibbāpetā yathā megho sāgarova guṇākaro 
  
      Dharaṇiriva                   sīlena himavāva samādhinā 
 Ākāso viya paññāya asaṅgo anīlo yathā 
  
      Sa kadāci mahāvīro parisāsu visārado 
 Saccāni sampakāsesi uddharanto mahājanaṃ 
  
      Tadāhi bāraṇasiyaṃ seṭṭhiputto mahāyaso 
 Āsahaṃ dhanadhaññassa pahutassa pabhu tadā  
  
      Jaṅghāvihāraṃ vicaraṃ migadāyamupeccahaṃ 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ desentaṃ amataṃ padaṃ 
  
      Vissaṭṭhakantavacanaṃ  karavīkasamassaraṃ 
 Haṃsarudābhinigghosaṃ  viññāpentaṃ mahājanaṃ 
  
      Disvā devātidevaṃ taṃ sutvā ca  madhuraṃ giraṃ 
 Pahāyānappake  bhoge pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Evaṃ pabbajito cāhaṃ na cirena bahussuto 
 Ahosiṃ dhammakathiko vicittapaṭibhāṇavā 
  
      Mahāparisamajjhehaṃ haṭṭhacitto punappunaṃ 
 Vaṇṇayiṃ hemavaṇṇassa vaṇṇaṃ vaṇṇavisārado 
  
      Esa khiṇāsavo buddho anīgho chinnasaṃsayo 
 Sabbakammakkhayaṃ patto vimuttopadhisaṃkhaye 
  
      Esa so bhagavā buddho esa sīho anuttare 
 Sadevakassa lokassa brahmacakkappavattako 
  
   Nāmena sīmu 
   Anubyañjanasampanno machasaṃ 
   Raṃsijālasamotthaṭo machasaṃ 
   Bahūtadā machasaṃ 
   Visaṭṭhakantavacanaṃ machasaṃ 
   Haṃsarutehi nigghosaṃ machasaṃ 
 Haṃsadundubhinigghosaṃ syā     
   Sutthāva machasaṃ 
   Pahāyanappake machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Danto dametā santo ca sametā nibbuto isi 
 Nibbāpetā ca assattho assāsetā mahājanaṃ 
  
      Vīro suro ca dhīro ca  pañño kāruṇiko vasī 
 Vijitāvī ca sa jino appagabbho anālayo 
  
      Anejo acalo dhīmā amoho asamo muni 
 Dhorayho usabho usabho nāgo sīho sakko garūsupi 
  
      Virāgo vimalo brahmā vādasūro raṇanañjaho 
 Akhilo ca visallo ca asamo saṃyuto  suci 
  
      Brāhmaṇo                   samaṇo nātho bhisakko sallakattako 
 Yodho buddho suto suto  acalo muditodito   
  
      Dhātā dhatā ca hantā ca  kattā tetā pakāsitā 
 Sampahaṃsitā bhettā ca chettā sotā pasaṃsitā 
  
      Akhilo ca visallo ca anīgho akathaṅkathi 
 Anejo virajo khantā  gantā  vattā pakāsitā  
  
      Tāretā atthakāretā kāretā sampadālitā  
 Pāpetā sahitā kantā hantā ātā pī tāpaso   
  
   Vikanto machasaṃ 
   Vusabho syā payato     
   Sutāsuto machasaṃ 
   Sito machasaṃ 
   Santi ca machasaṃ 
   Kattā machasaṃ 
   Gandhā machasaṃ 
   Pasaṃsitā machasaṃ 
   Samapadāritā machasaṃ 
    Tāpitā ca visositā syā 
  
                   
  
      Samacitto  samasamo asahāyo dayāsayo   
 Accherasatto  akuho katāvī isisattamo 
  
      Nittiṇṇakaṅkho nimmāno appameyyo anūpamo 
 Sabbavākyapathānīto saccañeyyantagū  jino 
  
      Sattasāravare  tasmiṃ pasādo amatāvaho 
 Tasmā buddhe ca dhamme ca saṃghe saddhā mahiddhikā   
  
      Guṇehi evamādīhi tilokasaraṇuttamaṃ 
 Vaṇṇento parisāmajjhe akaṃ  dhammakathaṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Tato cutohaṃ  tuyite anubhetvā mahāsukhaṃ 
 Tato cuto manussesu jāto bhomi sugandhiko 
      Nissāso mukhagandho ca dehagandho tatheva me 
 Sedagandho ca satataṃ sabbagandhetisetime   
  
      Mukhagandho sadā mayhaṃ padumuppalacampake   
 Ādisanto   sadā vāti sarīro ca tatheva me 
  
      Guṇaṃ                   buddhassa vatvāna hitāya janasandhisu   
 Sukhito   homi sabbattha saradvadhanisamāyuto   
  
      Yasassī sukhito kanto jutimā piyadassano 
 Vattā aparibhuto ca niddoso paññavā tathā 
  
      Khīṇe āyusi   nibbānaṃ sulabhaṃ buddhabhattino 
 Tesaṃ hetuṃ pavakkhāmi taṃ suṇātha yathātathaṃ 
  
      Santaṃ yasaṃ bhagavato vidhinā abhivādayaṃ 
 Yattha tatthupapannopi yasassī tena homahaṃ 
  
   Saccaṭṭhito syā 
   Dayālayo machasaṃ 
   Accheramanto syā 
   Sabbaneyyantiko syā 
   Sataraṃsīvare syā 
   Mahatthikā machasaṃ 
   Kathiṃ syā 
   Cutāhaṃ machasaṃ 
   Sabbagandhova hoti me machasaṃ 
    Padūmuppalavampako machasaṃ 
    Parisanto machasaṃ atikanto syā Atīsanto     
    Phalantaṃ syā 
    Bhāsitassa syā 
    Hitāya ca nasadisaṃ machasaṃ 
    Sucitto syā 
    Saṅghebirasamāyuto machasaṃ 
    Pāvusi syā 
  
                   
  
      Dukkhassantakaraṃ buddhaṃ dhammaṃ santamasaṅkhataṃ 
 Vaṇṇayaṃ sukhado āsiṃ sattānaṃ sukhito tato 
  
      Guṇaṃ vadanto buddhassa buddhapītisamāyuto 
 Sakantiṃ parakantiñca janayiṃ tena kantimā 
  
      Janoghe  titthakākiṇṇe  abhibhuyya kutitthiye 
 Guṇaṃ vadanto jotesiṃ nāyakaṃ jutimā tato 
  
      Piyakārī janassāpi sambuddhassa guṇaṃ vadaṃ 
 Saradova sasaṅkohaṃ tenāsiṃ  piyadassano 
  
      Yathāsattivasenāhaṃ sabbavācāhi santhaviṃ 
 Sugataṃ tena vāgīso vicittapaṭibhāṇavā 
  
      Ye bālā vimatippattā paribhonti mahāmuni 
 Niggahiṃ te sadhammena paribhūto na tenahaṃ  
  
      Buddhavaṇṇena  sattānaṃ kilese apanesahaṃ 
 Nikkilesamano homi tassa kammassa vāhasā 
  
      Sotunaṃ                   buddhimajaniṃ  buddhānussatidesako 
 Tenāhamāsiṃ  sappañño nipuṇatthavipassako 
  
      Sabbāsavariparikkhiṇo tiṇṇasaṃsārasāgaro 
 Sikhīva anupādāno pāpuṇissāmi nibbutiṃ 
  
      Imasmiṃ yeva kappasmiṃ yamahaṃ santhaviṃ jinaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhavaṇṇassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sugandho thero imā gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Sugandhattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ 
  
   Jino te machasaṃ 
   Titthikākiṇṇe machasaṃ 
   Thomesīṃ syā 
   Paribhutena tenahaṃ syā 
   Buddhavaṇṇehi sīmu 
   Vuṇḍimajaniṃ machasaṃ 
   Tenāpi cāsiṃ syā 
  
                   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
  
 Tiṇado mañcado ceva saraṇabbhañjanappado 
 Supaṭo daṇḍadāyī ca nelapūji tatheva ca 
 Bodhisammajjakāmeṇḍo  sugandho dasamo dijo   
 Gāthāsataṃ satevītaṃ cettha sabbaso 
  
 Tiṇadāyakavaggo tepaññāsamo 
  
     Mahākaccānattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino anejo ajitañjayo 
 Satasahasse kappānaṃ ito uppajji nāyako 
  
      Vīro kamalapattakkho sasaṅkavimalānano 
 Kanakāvalasaṅkāso  ravidittiyasamappabho 
  
      Sattanettamanohārī varalakkhaṇabhusito 
 Sabbavākyapathātīto manujāmarasakkato 
  
      Sambuddho bodhayaṃ satte vāgīso madhurassaro 
 Karuṇānibaddha  santāno parisāsu visārado 
  
      Deseti                   madhuraṃ dhammaṃ catusaccupasaṃhitaṃ 
 Nimugge mohapaṅkamhi samuddharati pāṇino 
  
      Tadā ekacaro hutvā tāpaso himavālayo 
 Nabhasā mānusaṃ lokaṃ gacchanto jinamaddasaṃ 
  
      Upecca santikaṃ tassa assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ 
 Vaṇṇayantassa vīrassa sāvakassa mahāguṇaṃ 
  
      Saṃkhittena mayā vuttaṃ vitthārena pakāsayaṃ 
 Parisaṃ mañca toseti yathā kaccāyano ayaṃ 
  
      Nāhaṃ evaṃ vidhaṃ kañci  aññaṃ passāmi sāvakaṃ 
 Tasmātadagge  esaggo evaṃ dhāretha bhikkhavo 
  
      Tadāhaṃ vimhito hutvā sutvā vākyaṃ manoramā 
 Himavantaṃ gamitvāna āhatvā  pupphasañcayaṃ 
  
      Pūjetvā lokasaraṇaṃ taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃ 
 Tadā mamāsayaṃ ñatvā vyākāsi saraṇañjaho 
  
   Bodhisammajjako maṇḍo machasaṃ 
   Ti ca machasaṃ 
   Kañcanakavasaṅkalāso syā 
   Nibandha sabbattha 
   Nāśaṃ evaṃmidhekakaccaṃ machasaṃ 
   Tasematadagge sīmu Tasmātadagge ṭhapemi theragāthaṭṭhakathā 
   Āhitvā 
  
                   
  
       Passathetaṃ isivaraṃ niddhantakanakattacaṃ 
 Uddhaggalomaṃ pīṇaṃsaṃ acalaṃ pañjaliṃ ṭhitaṃ 
  
      Hāsassupuṇṇanayanaṃ  buddhavaṇṇagatāsayaṃ 
 Dhammaṃva viggahavaraṃ  amatāsittasantibhaṃ 
  
      Kaccānassa guṇaṃ sutvā taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayaṃ ṭhito 
 Anāgatamhi addhāne gotamassa mahāmune 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Kaccāno nāma nāmena hessi satthusāvako 
  
      Bahussuto mahāñāṇi adhippāyavidū mune 
 Pāpuṇissati taṃ ṭhānaṃ yathāyaṃ vyākato mayā 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Duve bhave saṃsarāmi devatte atha mānuse 
 Aññaṃ gatiṃ na gacchāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Duve kule pajāyāmi khattiye atha brāhmaṇe 
 Nīce kule na jāyāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Pacchime                   va  bhave dāni jāto ujjeniyā pure   
 Pajjotassa ca caṇḍassa purohitadijātino   
  
      Putto tiraṭavacchassa  nipuṇo vedapāragū 
 Mātā ca candimā nāma kaccānohaṃ varattavo 
  
      Vīmaṃsatthaṃ buddhassa bhumipālena pesito 
 Disvā mokkhapuradvāraṃ nāyakaṃ guṇasañcayaṃ 
  
      Sutvā ca vimalaṃ vākyaṃ gatipaṅkavisosanaṃ 
 Pāpuṇiṃ amataṃ santaṃ sosehi saha sattahi   
  
      Adhippāyavidū jāto sugatassa mahāmune   
 Ṭhapito etadagge ca susamiddhamanoratho 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
   Bhāsaṃsapuṇṇanayanaṃ machasaṃ 
   Dhammajaṃuggahadayaṃ machasaṃ Dhammapaṭiggabhavaraṃ syā 
   Pacchime ca machasaṃ 
   Ujjeniyaṃ pure machasaṃ 
   Purohitadijādhino machasaṃ 
   Nidīvacchassa theragāthaṭṭhakathā Tiriṭivacchassa machasaṃ 
   Sesebhi saha pañcahi sīmu theragāthaṭṭhakathā  Sesehi saha sattahi  iti manorathapūraṇi ādiaṭṭhakathāhi saddhiṃ sameti 
   Mahāmate machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Ittha sudaṃ āyasmā mahākaccāno thero imā gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Mahākaccānattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ 
  
     Vakkalittherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
 Anomanāmo amito nāmena padumuttaro 
  
      Padumākāravadano padumāmalasucchavī 
 Lokenānupalittova teyena padumaṃ yathā 
  
      Vīro padumapattakkho santo ca padumaṃ yathā 
 Padumuttaragandho ca  tasmā so padumuttaro 
  
      Lokajeṭṭho ca nimmāno andhānaṃ nayanūpamo 
 Santaveso guṇanidhi karuṇāmatisāgaro 
  
      Sakadāci mahāvīro brahmāsurasuraccito 
 Sadevamanujākiṇṇo  janamajjhe anuttamo   
  
      Vadanena sugandhena madhurena rutena ca 
 Rañjayaṃ parisaṃ sabbaṃ santhavī sāvakaṃ sakaṃ 
  
       Saddhādhimutto                   sumatī mama dassanalālaso   
 Natthi etādiso añño yathāyaṃ bhikkhu vakkali  
  
      Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ nagare brāhmaṇatrajo 
 Hutvā sutvā ca taṃ vākyaṃ taṃ ṭhānamabhirocayiṃ 
  
      Sasāvakaṃ taṃ vimalaṃ nimantetvā tathāgataṃ 
 Sattāhaṃ bhojayitvāna dussegacchādayiṃ tadā 
  
      Nipacca sirasā tassa anantaguṇasāgare 
 Nimuggo pītisampuṇṇo idaṃ pacanamabraviṃ 
  
   Padumuttaragandhova machasaṃ 
   Sadevamanujākiṇṇe machasaṃ 
   Jinuttamo machasaṃ 
   Dassanasālayo syā 
  
                   
  
       Yo so tayā santhavito ito sattamakehani   
 Bhikkhu saddhāvataṃ aggo tādiso homahaṃ mune   
  
      Evaṃ vutte mahāvīro anāvaraṇadassano 
 Imaṃ vākyaṃ udīresi parisāyaṃ  mahāmuni 
  
       Passathetaṃ māṇavakaṃ pītamaṭṭhanivāsanaṃ 
 Hemayaññopavītaṅgaṃ  jananettamanoharaṃ 
  
      Eso anāgataddhāne gotamassa mahesino 
 Aggo saddhādhimuttānaṃ sāvakoyaṃ bhavissati 
  
      Devabhūto manusso vā sabbasantāpavajjito 
 Sabbabhogaparibbūḷho sukhito saṃsarissati 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakusalasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena  satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Vakkalī nāma nāmena hessati satthūsāvako 
  
      Tena kammavisesena cetanāpaṇīdhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Sabbattha sukhito hutvā saṃsaranto bhavābhave 
 Sāvatthiyaṃ pure jāto kule aññatare ahaṃ 
  
      Nonītasukhumālaṃ maṃ jātapallavakomalaṃ 
 Mandaṃ uttānasayanaṃ pisācībhayatajjitā   
  
      Pādamūle mahesissa sāyesuṃ dīnamānasā 
 Imaṃ dadāma te nātha saraṇaṃ hohi nāyaka  
  
      Tadā                   paṭiggahi so maṃ bhītānaṃ saraṇo muni 
 Jālitā saṅkhalaṅkena  mudukomalapāṇinā 
  
      Tadāppabhūti tenāhaṃ arakkheyyena rakkhito 
 Sabbaveravinimmutto  sukhena parivaḍḍhito 
  
      Sugatena vinābhūto ukkaṇṭhāmi muhuttakaṃ 
 Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
   Ito sattamake muni machasaṃ Ito saddhādhimutto iti syā 
   Parisāya machasaṃ 
   Hemayaññopacitaṅgaṃ machasaṃ 
   Gottena machasaṃ 
   Pisācabhayatajjitā sīmu Machasaṃ 
   Jālinācakkakitena machasaṃ 
   Sabbāpadāvinimmutto theragāthaṭṭhakathā sabbabyādhivinimmutto syā sabbupadhivinimmutto     
  
      Sabbapāmisambhūtaṃ lakkhīnilayanaṃ paraṃ   
 Rūpaṃ sabbasubhākiṇṇaṃ atitto pihayāmahaṃ  
  
      Buddharūparataṃ  ñatvā tadā ovadi maṃ jino 
  Alaṃ vakkali kiṃ rūpe ramase bālanandite 
  
      Yo hi passati saddhammaṃ so maṃ passati paṇḍito 
 Apassamāno saddhammaṃ maṃ passampi na passati 
  
      Anattādīnavo kāyo visarukkhasamūpamo 
 Āvāso sabbarogānaṃ puñjo dukkhassa kevalo 
  
      Tibbandiya tato rūpe khandhānaṃ uyadabbayaṃ 
 Passa sabbakilesānaṃ sukhenantaṃ gamisassi   
  
      Evaṃ tenānusiṭṭhohaṃ nāyakena hitesinā 
 Gijjhakūṭaṃ samāruyha jhāyāmi girikandare 
  
      Ṭhito pabbatapādamhi mamāha so mahāmuni   
 Vakkalīti jino vācaṃ taṃ sutvā mudito ahaṃ 
  
      Pakkhandiṃ selapabbhāre anekasataporise 
 Tadā buddhānubhāvena sukhenava mahiṃ gato 
  
      Punopi  dhammaṃ desesi  khandhānaṃ udayabbayaṃ 
 Tamhaṃ dhammamaññāya arahattamāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Sumahāparisāmajjhe  tadā maṃ maraṇantago  
 Aggaṃ saddhādhimuttānaṃ paññapesi mahāmati 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhajūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā                   jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgo va bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassaṃ sāsanaṃ 
  
   Nīlakkhitayanaṃ varaṃ machasaṃ 
   Vibharāmahaṃ machasaṃ 
   Buddho rūparataṃ sīmu buddharūparatiṃ machasaṃ 
   Assāsayi mahāmuni machasaṃ 
   Punāpi sīmu Syā 
   Deseti machasaṃ 
   Sumahāparisamajjhe machasaṃ 
   Caraṇantago machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vakkalitthero imaṃ gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Vakkalittherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ 
  
     Mahākappinattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragu 
 Udito jagadākāse  ravīva saradambare 
  
      Vacanābhāya bodheti veneyyapadumāni so 
 Kilesapaṅkaṃ soseti matiraṃsīhi nāyako 
  
      Titthiyānaṃ yaso hanti khajjotābhā yathā ravi 
 Saccatthābhaṃ pakāseti ratanaṃva divākaro 
  
      Guṇānaṃ āyatibhūto ratanānaṃva sāgaro 
 Pajjunnoriva bhūtāni dhammameghena vassati 
  
      Akkhadasso tadā āsiṃ nagare haṃsasavhaye 
 Upecca dhammamassosiṃ jalajuttaranāmino 
  
      Ovādakassa bikkhūnaṃ sāvakassa katāvino 
 Guṇaṃ pakāsayantassa tosayantassa  me manaṃ 
  
      Sutvā patīto sumano nimantetvāna taṃ ṭhānambhipatthayiṃ 
 Sasissaṃ bhojayitvāna taṃ ṭhānambhipatthayiṃ 
  
      Tadābhāsi mahābhāgo  haṃsadundubhisussaro   
 Passathetaṃ mahāmattaṃ vinicchayavisāradaṃ 
  
      Maṃpādamūle patītaṃ  samuggatatanūruhaṃ 
 Jimutavaṇṇaṃ pīṇaṃsaṃ pasannanayanānanaṃ 
  
      Parivārena mahatā rañjayaṃ taṃ  mahāyasaṃ 
 Eso katāvino ṭhānaṃ pattheti muditāsayo 
  
      Iminā                   piṇḍapātena  cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca   
 Kappasatasahassāni nūpapajjati duggatiṃ 
  
      Devesu devasobhaggaṃ manussesu mahantataṃ 
 Anubhotvāvasesena  nibbānaṃ pāpuṇissati 
  
   Ajaṭākāse machasaṃ Jaladākāse     
   Tappayantassa machasaṃ 
   Tadā haṃsasambhāgo machasaṃ 
   Haṃsadundubhinissaro theragāthaṭṭhakathā haṃsadundubhinissano machasaṃ 
   Patitaṃ pādamūle me machasaṃ 
   Rañjayannaṃ sīmu rājayuttaṃ machasaṃ   Paṇipātenaṃ machasaṃ 
   Cāgena paṇidhīhi ca machasaṃ 
   Anubhotvāna sesena machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottana satthā loke bhavissati 
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Kappino nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvako 
  
      Tatohaṃ sukataṃ kāraṃ katvāna jinasāsane 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tusitaṃ agamāsahaṃ 
      Devanamānusarajjāni sataso anusāsiya 
 Bārāṇasīsamāsanne jāto keniyajātiyaṃ 
  
      Sahassaparivārena  sapajāpatiko ahaṃ 
 Pañca paccekabuddhānaṃ satāni samupaṭṭhahiṃ 
  
      Temāsaṃ bhojayitvāna pacchādambha ticīvaraṃ 
 Tato cutā mayaṃ sabbe ahumbha tidasūpagā 
  
      Puto sabbe manussattaṃ āgamimbha  tato cutā 
 Kukkuṭambhi pure jātā himavantassa passato 
  
      Kappino nāmahaṃ āsiṃ rājaputto mahāyaso 
 Sesāmaccakule jātā mameva parivārayuṃ 
  
      Mahārajjasukhaṃ patto sabbakāmasamiddhimā 
 Vāṇijehi samakkhātaṃ buddhappādamahaṃ suṇiṃ 
  
       Buddho loke samuppanno asamo ekapuggalo 
 So pakāseti saddhammaṃ amataṃ sukhamuttamaṃ 
  
      Suyuttā tassa sissā ca sumuttā ca anāsavā   
 Sutvā tesaṃ suvacanaṃ sakkaritvāna vāṇije 
  
      Pahāya rajjaṃ sāmacco nikkhamaṃ buddhamāmako 
 Nadiṃ disvā mahācandā pūritaṃ samatittikaṃ 
  
      Appatiṭṭhaṃ anālambaṃ duttaraṃ sīghavāhiniṃ 
 Guṇaṃ saritvā buddhassa sotthinā samatikkamiṃ 
  
      Bhavasotaṃ sace buddho tiṇṇo lokantagū vidu 
 Etena saccavajjena gamanaṃ me samijjhatu 
  
   Satasahasseparivāro syā 
   Agamimha machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Yadi                   santigamo maggo mokkho vaccantikaṃ  sukhaṃ 
 Etena saccavajjena gamanaṃ me samijjhatu 
  
      Saṅgho ce tiṇṇakantāro puññakkhetto anuttaro 
 Etena saccavajjena gamanaṃ me samijjhatu 
  
      Saha kate saccavare maggā apagataṃ jalaṃ 
 Tato sukhena uttiṇṇo nadītīre manorame 
  
      Nisisannaṃ addasaṃ buddhaṃ udentaṃva pabhaṅkaraṃ 
 Jalantaṃ hemaselaṃva dīparukkhaṃva jotitaṃ 
  
      Sasī va  tārāsabhitaṃ sāvakehi purakkhataṃ vāsavaṃ viya vassantaṃ desanājaladaṃ tadā  
  
      Vanditvāna sahāmacco ekamantaṃ upāvisiṃ  
 Tato no āsayaṃ  ñatvā buddho dhammamadesayī 
  
      Sutvāna dhammaṃ vimalaṃ avocumha mayaṃ jinaṃ 
 Pabbājehi mahāvīra nibbittamha  mayaṃ bhave 
  
      Savākkhāto  bhikkhave dhammo dukkhantakaraṇāya vo 
 Caratha brahmacariyaṃ iccāha muni sattamo 
  
      Saha vācāya sabbepi bhikkhuvesadharā mayaṃ 
 Ahumbha upasampannā sotāpannā ca sāsane 
  
      Tato jetavanaṃ gavatvā anusāsi vināyako 
 Anusiṭṭho jinenāhaṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Tato bhikkhusahassaṃ  taṃ anāsāsiṃ ahaṃ tadā 
 Mamānusāsanakarā tepi āsuṃ anāsavā 
  
      Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
 Bhikkhu ovādakānaggo kappinoti mahājane 
  
      Satasahasse kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha 
 Sumutto saravevegova kilese jhāpayi  mama 
  
   Mokkhadaṃ santikaṃ syā 
   Sasiṃva machasaṃ 
   Desanājaladantaraṃ machasaṃ Devenajaladantaraṃ syā     
   Ekamantamupācisaṃ machasaṃ   Tatosajjhāsayaṃ syā 
   Nibbinnāmha machasaṃ 
   Svakkhāto machasaṃ 
   Tatobhikkhusahassāni machasaṃ 
   Jhāpayiṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgo va bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassaṃ sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahākappino thero imaṃ gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Mahākappinattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ 
  
     Dabbattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro                   nāma jino sabbalokavidū muni 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji cakkhumā 
  
      Ovādako viññāpako tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ 
 Desanākusalo buddho tāresi ranataṃ bahuṃ 
  
      Anukampako kāruṇiko hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ 
 Sampatte titthiye sabbe pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi  
  
      Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi suññataṃ  titthiyehi ca 
 Vicittaṃ arahantehi vasībhūtehi tādihi 
  
      Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsa  uggato so mahāmuni 
 Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso battiṃsavaralakkhaṇo 
  
      Vassasatasahassāni āyu vijjati tāvade 
 Tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ 
  
      Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyā seṭṭhiputto mahāyaso 
 Upetvā lokapajjotaṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ 
  
      Senāsanāni bhikkhūnaṃ paññāpentaṃ sasāvakaṃ 
 Kittayantassa vacanaṃ suṇitvā mudito ahaṃ 
  
      Adhikāraṃ sasaṅghassa katvā tassa mahesino 
 Nipacca sirasā pāde taṃ ṭhānambhipatthayiṃ 
  
   Patiṭṭhahi syā 
   Suññakaṃ syā 
   Paññāsaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Tadā bhāsi  mahāvīro mama kammaṃ pakittayaṃ 
 Yo sasaṅghamabhojesi sattāhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Soyaṃ kamalapattakkho sīhaṃso kanakattavo 
 Mama pādamūle nipatī  patthayaṃ ṭhānamuttamaṃ 
  
      Sahasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena  satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Sāvako tassa buddhassa dabbo nāmena vissuto 
 Senāsanapaññāpako aggo hessatiyaṃ  tadā 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇīdhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñca devarajjamakārayiṃ 
 Satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñca cakkavatti ahosahaṃ 
  
      Padesarajjaṃ                   vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ 
 Sabbattha sukhito āsiṃ tassa kammassa vāhasā 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe vipassī nāma nāyako 
 Uppajji cārunayano  sabbadhammavipassako 
  
      Duṭṭhacitto upavadiṃ sāvakaṃ tassa tādino 
 Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇaṃ suddhoti ca vijāniya 
  
      Tasseva naravīrassa sāvakānaṃ mahesinaṃ 
 Salākaṃ paggahetvāna  khīrodanamadāsahaṃ 
  
      Imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma nāmena uppajji vadataṃ varo 
  
      Sāsanaṃ jotayitvā so abhibhuyya kutitthiye 
 Veneyye  vinayitvāna nibbuto so sasāvako 
  
      Sasisse nibbute nāthe atthamentamhi  sāsane 
 Devā kandiṃsu saṃviggā muttakesā rudammukhā 
  
   Tadāhāsa sīmu Machasaṃ 
   Patito     
   Gottena machasaṃ 
   Hessatayā sīmu 
   Cārudassano machasaṃ 
   Salākañcagahetvāna machasaṃ 
   Vineyya machasaṃ 
   Antappattambhi theragāthaṭṭhakathā 
  
                   
  
       Nibbāyissatī dhammakkho na passissāma subbate 
 Na suṇissāma saddhammaṃ aho no appapuññatā   
  
      Tadāyaṃ paṭhavī  sabbā acalā sācalācalī  
 Sāgaro ca sasokova vinadī karuṇaṃ giraṃ 
  
      Catuddisā dundubhiyo nādayiṃsu amānusā 
 Sammantato asaniyo phaliṃsu  ca bhayāvahā 
  
      Ukkā patiṃsu nabhasā dhūmaketu cadissatha   
 Sabbatthalajasattā ca  raviṃsu karuṇaṃ migā 
  
      Uppāte  dāruṇe disvā sāsanatthaṅgamasuvake 
 Saṃviggā bhikkhavo satta cintayimha mayaṃ tadā 
  
      Sāsanena vināmhākaṃ jīvitena alaṃ mayaṃ 
 Pavisitvā mahāraññaṃ yuñjāma jinasāsane  
  
      Addasumbha  tadāraññe ubbiddhaṃ selamuttamaṃ 
 Tissenaṇiyā tamāruyha tisseṇiṃ pātayimhase 
  
      Tadā                   ovadi no thero buddhuppādo sudullabho 
 Saddhā ca dullabhā  laddhā thokaṃ sesañca   sāsanaṃ 
  
      Nipatanti khaṇātītā anante dukkhasāgare 
 Tasmā payogo kattabbo yāva ṭhāti mune mataṃ    
  
      Arahā āsi so thero anāgāmī tadānugo 
 Susīlā itare yuttā devalokaṃ agamhase 
  
      Nibbuto tiṇṇasaṃsāro suddhāvāse ca ekako 
 Ahaṃ ca pukkusātī ca sabhiyo bāhiyo tathā 
  
      Kumārakassapo ceva tattha tatthūpagā mayaṃ 
 Saṃsārabandhanā muttā gotamenānukampitā 
  
      Mallesu kusinārāyaṃ jāto gabbheva me sato 
 Matā mātā citārūḷhā tato nippatito ahaṃ 
  
      Patito dabbapuñjamhi tato dabboti vissuto 
 Brahmacārībalenāhaṃ vimutto sattavassiko 
  
   Pathavi machasaṃ 
   Calācalā machasaṃ Pulāpūlī syā 
   Patiṃsu sīmu 
   Dissati machasaṃ 
   Sadhūmā jālavaṭṭā ca machasaṃ 
   Uppāde machasaṃ 
   Sāsanaṃ machasaṃ 
   Addasamha machasaṃ Sīmu 
   Saddhātidullabhā machasaṃ 
    Thokasesañca sīmu 
    Yāva tiṭṭhati sāsanaṃ syā Theragāthaṭṭhakathā 
    Pakkusāti ca machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Khīrodanaphalenāhaṃ pañcahaṅgehupāgato 
 Khīṇāsavopavādena pāpehi bahucotito 
  
      Ubho puññaṃ ca pāpañca vītivattomhi dānahaṃ   
 Patvāna paramaṃ santiṃ viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Senāsanaṃ paññāpayiṃ bhāsayitvāna subbate 
 Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho etadaggo phapesi maṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgo va bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassaṃ sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dabbo mallaputto thero imaṃ gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Dabbo mallaputtattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ 
  
     Kumārakassapattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
 Sabbalokahito vīro padumuttaranāmako 
  
      Tadāhaṃ brāhmaṇo hutvā vissuto vedapāragū 
 Divāvihāraṃ vivaraṃ addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Catusaccaṃ                   pakāsentaṃ bodhayantaṃ sadevakaṃ 
 Vicittakathikānaggaṃ vaṇṇayantaṃ mahājane 
  
      Tadā muditacittohaṃ nimantetvā tathāgataṃ 
 Nānārattehi vatthehi alaṅkatvāna maṇḍapaṃ 
  
      Nānāratanapajjotaṃ sasaṅghaṃ bhojayiṃ tahiṃ 
 Bhojayitvāna sattāhaṃ nānaggarasabhojanaṃ 
  
      Nānāvaṇṇehi  pupphehi pūjayitvā sasāvakaṃ 
 Nipajja pādamūlamhi taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
   Dānihaṃ machasaṃ 
   Nānācittehi machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Tadā munivaro āha kāruṇekarasāsayo   
 Passathetaṃ dijavaraṃ padumānalovanaṃ 
  
      Pītipāmojjabahulaṃ samuggatatanūruhaṃ 
 Bhāsāhitavisālakkhaṃ  mama sāsanalālasaṃ 
  
      Mama pādamūle patitaṃ  ekāvatta sumānasaṃ 
 Esa pattheti taṃ ṭhānaṃ vicittakathikattanaṃ  
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Kumārakassapo nāma hessati satthusāvako 
  
      Vicittapupphadussānaṃ ratanānaṃ ca vāhasā 
 Vicittakaṭhikānaṃ so aggataṃ pāpuṇissati 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇīdhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Parimbhamaṃ bhavākāse  raṅgamajjhenaṭo yathā   
 Sākhāmigatrajo hutvā migiyā kuccimokkamiṃ 
  
      Tadā mayi kucchigate majjhavāro upaṭṭhito 
 Sākhena vattā me mātā nigrodhaṃ saraṇaṃ gatā 
  
      Tena sā migarājena maraṇaṃ parimocitā 
 Pariccajitvā saṃ pāṇaṃ  mamevaṃ ovadī tadā 
  
      Nigrodhameva seveyya na sākhamupasaṃvase 
 Nigrodhasmiṃ mataṃ seyyo yaṃ ce sākhamhi  jīvitaṃ 
  
      Tenānusiṭṭho  migayuthapena ahaṃ ca mātā ca tathetare ca 
 Āgamma                   rammaṃ tusitādhivāsaṃ gatā pavāsaṃ sagharaṃ yatheva 
  
      Puno kassapavīrassa atthamentamhi sāsane 
 Āruyha selasikharaṃ yuñjitvā jinasāsanaṃ 
  
   Karuṇokaruṇālayo syā Karuṇākarasāsayo theragāthāṭṭhakathā 
   Hāsamhitavisālakkhaṃ machasaṃ Sīmu Hāsādhikaṃ theragāthaṭṭhakathā 
   Patitaṃ pādamūle me machasaṃ 
   Vicittakathikatthadaṃ sīmu 
   Bhavābhave machasaṃ 
   Raṅgamajjhe yathā naṭo theragāthaṭṭhakathā raṅgamajjhanaṭo yathā sīmu Machasaṃ   Sapāṇaṃ machasaṃ 
   Sākhasmi machasaṃ 
   Tenānusiṭṭhā machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Idānahaṃ  rājagahe jāto seṭṭhikule ahu   
 Āpannasattā  me mātā pabbaji anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Sagambhaṃ taṃ viditvāna devadattamupānayuṃ 
 So avoca vināsetha pāpikaṃ bhikkhunīṃ imaṃ 
  
      Idānipi munindena jinena anukampitā 
 Sukhīni ajanī mayhaṃ mātā bhikkhunupassaye 
  
      Taṃ viditvā mahīpālo kosalo maṃ aposayi 
 Kumāraparihārena nāmenāhañca kassapo 
  
      Mahākassapamāgamma ahaṃ kumārakassapo 
 Vammikasadisaṃ kāyaṃ sutvā buddhena desitaṃ 
  
      Tato cittaṃ vimucci me anupādāya sabbaso 
 Pāyāyiṃ damayitvāhaṃ etadaggaṃ apāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgo va bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassaṃ sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kumārakassapo thero imaṃ gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Kumārakassapattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ 
  
 Catuvīsatimaṃ bhāṇāvāraṃ 
  
     Bāhiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
 Mahappabho tilokaggo nāmena padumuttaro 
  
      Khippābhiññassa bhikkhuno guṇaṃ kittayato mune 
 Sutvā udaggacittohaṃ kāraṃ katvā mahesino  
  
   Idānāhaṃ machasaṃ 
   Ahuṃ machasaṃ 
   Āpannagambhā sīmu 
  
                   
  
      Datvā sattāhikaṃ dānaṃ sasissassa mune ahaṃ 
 Abhivādiya sambuddhaṃ taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayiṃ tadā 
  
      Tato maṃ vyākarī  buddho etaṃ passatha brāhmaṇaṃ 
 Patitaṃ pādamūle me pasannanayanānanaṃ  
  
      Hemayaññopavitaṅgaṃ                   avadātananuttavaṃ 
 Palambibimbatamboṭṭhaṃ sitatiṇhasamaṃ dvījaṃ  
  
      Guṇatthāmabahutaraṃ  samuggatatanūruhaṃ 
 Guṇoghāyatanībhūtaṃ pītisamphullitānanaṃ 
  
      Eso patthayate ṭhānaṃ khippābhiññassa bhikkhuno 
 Anāgate mahāvīro gotamo nāma hessati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Bāhiyo nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvako 
  
      Tadātituṭṭho  vuṭṭhāya yāvajīvaṃ mahāmune 
 Kāraṃ katvā cuto saggaṃ agaṃ sabhavanaṃ yathā 
  
      Devabhūto manusso vā sukhito tassa kammuno 
 Vāhasā saṃsaritvāna sampattiṃ anubhosahaṃ  
  
      Puno  kassapavīrassa atthamentamhi sāsane 
 Āruyha selasikharaṃ yuñjitvā jinasāsanaṃ 
  
      Visuddhasīlā sappaññā jinasāsanakārakā 
 Tato cutā pañcajanā devalokaṃ agamhase 
  
      Tatohaṃ bāhiyo jāto bhārukacche puruttame 
 Tato nāvāya pakkhanto  sāgaraṃ appasiddhiyaṃ   
  
      Tato nāvā abhijjittha gantvāna katipāhakaṃ 
 Tadā bhiṃsanake   ghore patito makarākare 
  
      Tadāhaṃ vāyamitvāna santaritvā mahodadhiṃ 
 Suppāra   paṭṭanavaraṃ sampatto mandamedhiko    
  
      Dārucīraṃ nivāsetvā gāmaṃ piṇḍāya pāvisiṃ 
 Tadāha so jano tuṭṭho arahāyamidhāgato 
  
   Byākari machasaṃ 
   Cariyaṃ paccavekkhaṇaṃ machasaṃ 
   Setatiṇahasmiṃ dijaṃ machasaṃ 
   Guṇathāmbahutaraṃ machasaṃ 
   Tadāhituṭṭho machasaṃ 
   Anubhomahaṃ machasaṃ 
   Puna machasaṃ 
   Pakkhando machasaṃ Pakkanto     
   Appasiddhikaṃ sīmu 
    Bhiṃsasanake machasaṃ 
    Suppāda machasaṃ 
    Mandamedhito machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Imaṃ annena pānena vatthena sayanena ca 
 Bhesajjena ca sakkaccā hessāma sukhitā mayaṃ 
  
      Paccayānaṃ tadā lābhī tehi sakkatapūjito 
 Arahāhanti saṃkappaṃ uppādesiṃ ayoniso 
  
      Tato                   me cittamaññāya codayī pubbadevatā 
 Na tvaṃ upāyamaggaññū kuto tvaṃ arahaṃ bhave 
  
      Codito tāya saṃviggo tadāhaṃ paripucchisaṃ 
 Ke vā ete kuhiṃ loke arahanto naruttamā 
  
      Sāvatthiyaṃ kosalamandire jino pahūtapañño varabhurimedhaso 
 So sakyaputto arahā anāsavo deseti dhammaṃ arahattapattiyā 
  
      Tadassa sutvā vacanaṃ supīṇito 
 Tidhiṃva laddhā kapaṇotivimhito 
 Udaggacitto arahattamuttamaṃ  
 Sudussanaṃ daṭṭhumanantagocaraṃ 
  
      Tadā tato nikkhamitūna satvaraṃ  
 Kadā jinaṃ passāmi vimālananaṃ 
 Upecca rammaṃ vijitavhayaṃ vanaṃ 
 Dije apucchiṃ kuhiṃ lokanandano 
  
      Tato avocuṃ naradevavandito 
 Puraṃ paviṭṭho asanesanāsayo  
 Sace hi  khippaṃ munidassanussuko 
 Upecca vandāhi tamaggapuggalaṃ 
  
      Tatohaṃ tuvaṭṭaṃ gantvā sāvatthipuramuttamaṃ 
 Vicarantaṃ tamaddakkhiṃ piṇḍatthamapihāgidhaṃ  
  
      Pattapāṇiṃ alolakkhaṃ bhājayantaṃ viyāmataṃ  
 Sirīnilayasaṅkāsaṃ ravidittiharānanaṃ 
  
      Pāṇasantāraṇatthāya                   piṇḍāya vicarāmahaṃ 
 Na te dhammakathākālo iccāha munisattamo 
  
   Arahattamuttamaṃ machasaṃ 
   Nikkhamitvāna satthuno machasaṃ 
   Asanesanāya so machasaṃ 
   Sasova machasaṃ paccehi syā 
   Piṇḍatthaṃ apihāgidhaṃ machasaṃ jotayantaṃ idhāmataṃ syā 
   Pācayantaṃ pītākaraṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Tadā punappunaṃ buddhaṃ āyāciṃ dhammalālaso 
 So me dhammadesesi gambhīraṃ suññataṃ padaṃ 
  
      Tassa dhammaṃ suṇitvāna pāpuṇiṃ āsavakkhayaṃ 
 Parikkhīṇāyuko santo aho satthānukampako 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgo va bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassaṃ sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Evaṃ thero viyākāsi bāhiyo dārucīriyo 
 Saṅkārakūṭe patito bhūtāviṭṭhāya gāviyā 
  
      Attano pubbacaritaṃ  kittayitvā mahāmati 
 Parinibbāyī so vīro  sāvatthiyaṃ puruttame 
  
      Nagarā nikkhamanto taṃ disvāna isisattamo 
 Dārucīradharaṃ dhīraṃ bāhiyaṃ bāyināgamaṃ 
  
      Bhūmiyaṃ patitaṃ dantaṃ indaketuṃva  pātitaṃ 
 Gatāyusaṃ gatakelasaṃ  jinasāsanakārakaṃ 
  
      Tato āmantayī satthā sāvake sāsane rate 
  Gaṇhatha netvā  jhāpetha tanuṃ sabrahmacārino 
  
      Thūpaṃ karotha pūjetha nibbuto so mahāmati 
 Khippābhiññānamesaggo sāvako me vacokaro 
  
      Sahassampi ce gāthā anatthapadasaṃhitā 
 Ekaṃ kāthāpadaṃ seyyo sutvā upasammati 
  
      Yattha āpo ca paṭhavī  tejo vāyo na gādhati 
 Na tattha sukkā jotanti ādicco nappakāsati 
 Na tattha candimā bhāti tamo tattha na vijjati 
  
   Pubbacariyaṃ machasaṃ 
   Thero machasaṃ Dhīro syā 
   Indaketuva machasaṃ 
   Gatāyuṃ sukkhakilesaṃ machasaṃ 
   Hutvā syā     
   Pathavī machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Yādā ca attanā vedi muni monena brāhmaṇo 
 Atha rūpā arūpā ca sukhadukkhā vimuccati 
 Iccovaṃ abhaṇī nātho tilokasaraṇo muni 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bāhiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Bāhiyattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ 
  
     Koṭṭhitattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro                   nāma jino sabbalokavidu muni 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji cakkhumā 
  
      Ovādako viññāpako tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ 
 Desanākusalo buddho tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ 
  
      Anukampako kāruṇiko hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ 
 Sampatte titthiye sabbe pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi   
  
      Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi suññakaṃ titthiyehi ca 
 Vicittaṃ arahantehi vasībhūtehi tādihi 
  
      Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ uggato so mahāmuni 
 Kañca nagghiyasaṅkāso battiṃsavaralakkhaṇo 
  
      Vassasatasahassāni āyu vijjati tāvade 
 Tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ 
  
      Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ brāhmaṇo vedapāragu 
 Upetvā sattasāraggaṃ  assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ 
  
      Tadā so sāvakaṃ vīro pabhinnamatigocaraṃ 
 Atthe dhamme ca nerutte  paṭibhāne ca kovidaṃ 
  
      Ṭhapesi etadaggamhi taṃ sutvā mudito ahaṃ 
 Sasāvakaṃ jinavaraṃ sattāhaṃ bhojayiṃ tadā 
  
      Dussehakacchādayitvāna sasissaṃ buddhisāgaraṃ 
 Nipacca pādamūlamhi taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Tato avoca lokaggo passathetaṃ dijuttamaṃ 
 Vinataṃ pādamūle me kamalodarasappabhaṃ 
  
   Patiṭṭhayī theragāthaṭṭhakathā 
   Upeccasabbalokaggaṃ machasaṃ 
   Atthe dhamme nirutte ca machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Buddhaseṭṭhassa bhikkhussa  ṭhānaṃ patthayate ayaṃ 
 Tāya saddhāya cāgena dhammassa savaṇena  ca 
  
      Sabbattha sukhito hutvā saṃsaritvā bhavābhave 
 Anāgatamhi addhāne ladacchate taṃ manorathaṃ 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena  satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa                   dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Koṭṭhito nāma nāmena hessati satthu sāvake 
  
      Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ 
 Mettacitto paricariṃ sato paññāsamāhito 
  
      Tena kammavipākena cetanāpaṇīdhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Sataṃ tīṇikkhattuñca devarajjamakārayiṃ 
 Satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñca cakkavattī ahosahaṃ 
  
      Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ 
 Sabbattha sukhito āsiṃ tassa kammassa vāhasā 
  
      Duve bhave saṃsarāmi devatte atha mānuse 
 Aññaṃ gatiṃ na gacchāmi suciṇṇassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Duve kule pajāyāmi khattiye atha brāhmaṇe 
 Nīce kule na jāyāmi suciṇṇassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Pacchimbhave  sampatte brahmabandhu ahosahaṃ 
 Sāvatthiyaṃ vippakule paccājāto mahaddhane 
  
      Mātā candavatī nāma pitā me assalāyano 
 Yadā me pitaraṃ buddho vinayī sabbasuddhiyā 
  
      Tadā pasanno sugate pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Moggallāno ācariyo upajjho  sārisambhavo 
  
   Seṭṭhaṃ buddhassa bhikkhussa syā 
   Tena dhammassavanena sīmu Saddhammassavanena machasaṃ 
   Gontena machasaṃ 
   Pacchime bhave machasaṃ 
   Upajjhā machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Kesesu chijjamānesu diṭṭhi chinnā samūlikā 
 Nivāsento  ca kāsāmaṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Atthadhammaniruttīsu paṭibhāne ca me mati 
 Pahinnā tena lokaggo etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
      Asandiddhaṃ vīyākāsiṃ upatissena pucchito 
 Paṭisambhidāsu tenāhaṃ aggo sambuddhasāsane 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgo va bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassaṃ sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahākoṭṭhito thero imaṃ gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Mahākoṭṭhitattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ 
  
     Uruvelakassapattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro                   nāma jino sabbalokavidu muni 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji cakkhumā 
  
      Ovādako viññāpako tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ 
 Desanākusalo buddho tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ 
  
      Anukampako kāruṇiko hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ 
 Sampatte titthiye sabbe pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi   
  
      Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi puññakaṃ titthiyehi ca 
 Vicittaṃ arahantehi vasībhutehi tādihi 
  
      Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ uggato so mahāmuni 
 Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso battiṃsavaralakkhaṇo 
  
   Nivāsanto sīmu 
   Patiṭṭhayī sīmu Theragāthaṭṭhakathā 
  
                   
  
      Vassasatasahassāni āyu vijjati tāvade 
 Tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ 
  
      Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ brāhmaṇo sādhusammato 
 Upecca lokapajjotaṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ 
  
      Tadā mahāparisatiṃ mahāpurisasāvakaṃ 
 Ṭhapentaṃ etadaggamhi sutvāna mudito ahaṃ 
  
      Mahatā parivārena nimannetvā mahājinaṃ 
 Brāhmaṇānaṃ sahassena saha dānamadāsahaṃ 
  
      Mahādānaṃ daditvāna abhivādiya nāyakaṃ 
 Ekamante  ṭhito haṭṭho saha dānamadāsahaṃ 
  
      Tayi saddhāya me vīra adhikaraguṇena ca 
 Parisā mahatī hotu nibbattassa tahiṃ tahiṃ 
  
      Tadā avoca parisaṃ gajagajjitasussaro 
 Karavīkaruto satthā etaṃ passatha brāhmaṇaṃ 
  
      Hemavaṇṇaṃ mahābāhuṃ kamalānanalovanaṃ 
 Uddhaggatanujaṃ  haṭṭhaṃ saddhāvantaṃ  guṇe mama 
  
      Esa patthayate ṭhānaṃ  sīhaghosassa bhikkhuno 
 Anāgatamhi addhāne lacchite taṃ manorathaṃ 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loka bhavissati 
  
      Tassa                   dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Kassapo nāma nāmena  hessati satthu sāvako 
  
      Ite dvenavute kappe ahu satthā anuttaro 
 Anūpamo asadiso phusso lokagganāyako 
  
      So ca sabbaṃ namaṃ hantvā vijaṭetvā mahājaṭaṃ 
 Vassate amataṃ vuṭṭhiṃ tappayanto sadevakaṃ 
  
      Tadāhi hi bārāṇasiyaṃ rājāpaccā ahumhase 
 Bhātaromha tayo sabbe saṃvissatthā ca  rājino 
  
   Ekamantaṃ machasaṃ 
   Udaggatanujaṃ machasaṃ 
   Saddhavatta machasaṃ 
   Patthayi taṃ ṭhānaṃ syā 
   Gottena machasaṃ 
   Saṃvisaṭṭhāva machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Vīraṅgarūpā balino saṅgāme aparājitā 
 Tadā kupitapaccanto amhe āha mahipati 
  
      Etha gantvāna paccantaṃ sodhetvā aṭavībalaṃ 
 Khemaṃ mevijitaṃ katvā punarethā ti  bhāsatha 
  
      Tato mayaṃ avocumha yadi deyyāsi nāyakaṃ 
 Upaṭṭhānāya amhākaṃ sādhayissāma vo tato 
  
      Tato mayaṃ laddhavarā bhūmipālena pesitā 
 Nikkhittasatthaṃ paccantaṃ katvā punarupecca taṃ 
  
      Yācitvā satthupaṭṭhānaṃ rājānaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Munivīraṃ labhitvāna yāvajīvaṃ yajimha taṃ 
  
      Mahagghāni ca vatthāni paṇītāni rasāni ca senāsanāni rammāni bhesajjāni hitāni ca 
  
      Datvā sasaṃghassa mune  dhammenuppāditāni no 
 Sīlavanto kāruṇikā bhāvatāyuttamānasā 
  
      Sadā  paricaritvāna mettacittena nāyakaṃ 
 Nibbute tamhi lokagge pūjaṃ katvā yathābalaṃ 
  
      Tato cutā santusitaṃ gatā tattha mahāsukhaṃ 
 Anubhūtā mayaṃ sabbe buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Māyākāro                   yathā raṅge  dasseti vikatī bahu   
 Tathā bhave bhamantohaṃ videhādhipatī ahuṃ 
  
      Guṇāvelassa vākyena micchādiṭṭhīgatāsayo 
 Narakammaggamārūḷho rujāya  mama dhītuyā 
  
      Ovādaṃ nādiyitvāna brahmunā nāradenahaṃ 
 Bahudhā sāsito  santo diṭṭhaṃ hitvāna pāpikaṃ 
  
      Pūrayitvā visesena dasakammapathānahaṃ 
 Hitvāna dehamagamiṃ saggaṃ sabhavanaṃ yathā 
  
      Pacchimbhave sampatte  brahmabandhu ahosahaṃ 
 Bārāṇasiyaṃ phitāyaṃ jāto vippamahākule 
  
      Maccuvyādhijarābhīto jahitvāna mahādhanaṃ   
 Nibbānaṃ padamesanto jaṭilesu paribbajiṃ 
  
   Punadethāti machasaṃ 
   Sasaṅghamunino machasaṃ 
   Saddhā machasaṃ 
   Laddho syā     
   Vikatiṃ bahuṃ machasaṃ 
   Rucāya machasaṃ Rūpāsa theragāthaṭṭhakathā 
   Saṃsito machasaṃ 
   Pacchime bhave sampatte machasaṃ 
   Ogāhetvā mahāvanaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Tadā dve bhātaro mayhaṃ pabbajiṃsu mayā saha 
 Uruvelāyaṃ māpetvā assamaṃ nivasiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Kassapo nāma gottena uruvelanivāsiko  
 Tato me āsi paññatti uruvelakassapo iti 
  
      Nādīsakāse bhātā me nādīkassapaavhayo 
 Āsī samīpassanāmena yagāya gayakassapo   
  
      Dve satāni kaniṭṭhassa tīṇi majjhassa bhātuno 
 Mama pañcasatānūnā sissā sabbe mamānugā 
  
      Tadā pecca maṃ buddho katvā nānāvidhani me   
 Pāṭihīrāni lokaggo vinesi narasārathi 
  
      Sahassaparivārena ahosiṃ ehibhikkhuko 
 Teheva saha sabbehi arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Te                   cevaññe ca bahavo sissā maṃ parivārayuṃ 
 Sāsituṃ va samatthohaṃ tato maṃ isisattamo 
  
      Mahāparisabhāvasmiṃ etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
 Aho buddhe kataṃ kāraṃ saphalaṃ me ajāyatha 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgo va bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassaṃ sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā uruvelakassapo thero imaṃ gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Uruvelakassapattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ 
  
     Rādhattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbalokavidu muni 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji cakkhumā 
  
      Ovādako viññāpako tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ 
 Desanākusalo buddho tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ 
  
   Uruvelāya nivasiṃ syā 
   Gayāyaṃ gayākassapo machasaṃ 
   Katvāna vividhāni me machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Anukampako kāruṇiko hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ 
 Sampatte titthiye sabbe pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi 
  
      Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi suññakaṃ  titthiyehi ca 
 Vicittaṃ arahantehi vasībhūtehi tādihi 
  
      Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ uggato so mahāmuni 
 Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso battiṃsavaralakkhaṇo 
  
      Vassasatasahassāni āyu vijjati tāvade 
 Tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ 
  
      Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ brāhmaṇo mantapāragū 
 Upecca taṃ naravaraṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ 
  
      Paññāpentaṃ mahāvīraṃ parisāsu visāradaṃ 
 Paṭibhāṇeyyakaṃ bhikkhuṃ etadagge vināyakaṃ 
  
      Tadāhaṃ kāraṃ katvāna sasaṅghe lokanāyake 
 Nipacca sirasā pāde taṃ ṭhānambhipatthayiṃ 
  
      Tato maṃ bhagavā āha siṅgīnikkhasamappabho 
 Sarena rajanīyena kilesamalahārinā 
  
       Sukhī bhavassu dighāyu sijjhataṃ  paṇidhi tava 
 Sasaṅghe me kataṃ kāra anīva vipulaṃ tayā 
  
      Satasahasse                   ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loka bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Rādhoti nāmadheyyena hessati satthusāvako 
  
      Sa te hetuguṇe tuṭṭho sakyaputto narāsabho 
 Paṭibhāṇeyyakānaggaṃ paññāpessati nāyako   
  
      Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ 
 Mettacitto paricariṃ sato paññāsamāhito 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
   Suññataṃ machasaṃ 
   Sijjhatu machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuṃ ca devarajjamakārayiṃ 
 Satānaṃ pañcakkhattuṃ ca cakkavattī ahosahaṃ 
  
      Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ 
 Sabbattha sukhito āsiṃ tassa kammassa vāhasā 
  
      Pacchimbhave sampatte giribbapuruttame 
 Jāto vippakuleniddhe vikalacchādanāsate 
  
      Kaṭacchubhikkhā pādāsiṃ sāriputtassa tādino 
 Yadā jiṇṇo ca vuddho ca tadā rāmamupāgamiṃ 
      Pabbājenti na maṃ kekaci  jiṇṇaṃ dubbalathāmakaṃ 
 Tena dīno vivaṇṇaṅgo sokī  cāsiṃ tadā ahaṃ 
  
      Disvā mahākāruṇiko mamāha so mahāmuni  
 Kimatthā putta sokaṭṭo brūhi te cittajaṃ rujaṃ 
      Pabbajjaṃ na labhe vīra svākkhāte tava sāsane 
 Tena sokena dīnosmi saraṇaṃ hohi nāyaka 
  
      Tadā bhikkhu samānetvā āpucchi muni sattamo 
 Imassa adhikāraṃ ye saranti vyāvarantu te 
  
      Sāriputto tadāvoca kāramassa sarāmahaṃ 
 Kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ dāpesi piṇḍāya cārato mama 
  
      Sādhu sādhu kataññusi sāriputta imaṃ tuvaṃ 
 Pabbājehi dijaṃ vuddhaṃ hessatājāniyo ahaṃ 
  
      Tato                   alatthaṃ pabbajjaṃ kammavācepasampadaṃ 
 Na cireneva kālena pāpuṇiṃ āsavakkhayaṃ 
  
      Sakkaccaṃ munino vākyaṃ suṇomi mudito yato 
 Paṭibhāneyyakānaggaṃ tato maṃ ṭhapayī jino 
  
   Pabbajati na maṃ koci machasaṃ 
   Soko machasaṃ 
   Mamamāha mahāmunī machasaṃ 
                   
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgo va bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassaṃ sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā rādho thero imaṃ gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Rādhattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ 
  
     Mogharājattherāpadānaṃ  
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbalokavidū muni 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji cakkhumā 
  
      Ovādako viññāpako tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ 
 Desanākusalo buddho tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ 
  
      Anukampako kāruṇiko hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ 
 Sampatte titthiye sabbe pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi 
  
      Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi suññakaṃ titthiyehi ca 
 Vicittaṃ arahantehi vasībhūtehi tādihi 
  
      Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ uggato so mahāmuni 
 Kañcanagghiye saṅkāso battiṃsavaralakkhaṇo   
  
      Vassasatasahassāni āyu vijjati tāvade 
 Tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ 
  
      Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ kule aññatare ahuṃ 
 Parakammāyane yutto natthi me kiñci saṃdhanaṃ 
  
      Paṭikkamanasālāyaṃ vasanto katabhumiyaṃ 
 Aggimujjālayiṃ natthi daḷhaṃ kaṇhāsi sā  mahi 
  
      Tadā parisatiṃ nātho catusaccappakāsako 
 Sāvakā sampakittesi lukkhacivaradhārakaṃ 
  
   Catutthavagge aññaṃ mogharājāpadānaṃ vijjati Theragāthaṭṭhakathāyaṃ tameva uddharitvā dassitaṃ 
  
   Bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo machasaṃ 
   Daḷhaṃ kaṇhāsiyā sīmu Daḷhakaṇhā sisā syā 
  
                   
  
      Tassa tamhi guṇe tuṭṭho paṇipacca  tathāgataṃ 
 Lukhacīvaradhāggaṃ patthayiṃ ṭhānamuttamaṃ 
  
      Tadā avoca bhagavā sāvake padumuttaro 
 Passathetaṃ purikasaṃ kucelaṃ tanudehakaṃ 
  
      Pītippasannavadanaṃ                   saddhādhanasamanvitaṃ 
 Uddhaggatanujaṃ haṭṭhaṃ acalaṃ sālapiṇḍikaṃ  
  
      Eso pattheti taṃ ṭhānaṃ saccasenassa bhikkhuno 
 Lukhacīvaradhārissa tassa vaṇṇagatāsayo   
  
      Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā nipacca sirasā jinaṃ 
 Yāvajīvaṃ subhaṃ kammaṃ karitvā jinasāsane 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇīdhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsupago ahaṃ 
  
      Paṭikkamanasālāyaṃ bhūmidāhakakammunā 
 Samasahassaṃ niraye adayhaṃ vedanaṭṭito 
  
      Tena kammāvasesena pañcajātisatānabhaṃ 
 Manusso kulajo hutvā jātiyā lakkhaṇaṅkito 
  
      Pañcajātisatāneva kuṭṭharogasamappito 
 Mahādukkhaṃ anubhaviṃ tassa kammassa vāhasā 
  
      Imasmiṃ bhaddake kappe upariṭṭhaṃ yasassinaṃ 
 Piṇḍapātena tappesiṃ pasannamānaso ahaṃ 
  
      Tena kammavisesena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Macchimabhave sampatte ajāyiṃ khattiye kule 
 Pituno accayenāhaṃ mahārajjasamappito 
  
      Kuṭṭharogābhibhutohaṃ na ratiṃ na sukhaṃ labhe 
 Moghaṃ rajjasukhaṃ  yasmā mogharājā tato amaṃ 
  
      Kāyassa dosaṃ disvāna pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Bāvarissa dijaggassa sissattaṃ ajjhupāgamiṃ 
  
      Mahatā parivārena upecca naranāyakaṃ 
 Apucchiṃ nipuṇaṃ pañhaṃ taṃ vīraṃ vādisūdanaṃ 
  
   Patipajja syā 
   Sālapiṇḍitaṃ machasaṃ 
   Vaṇṇasitāsayo machasaṃ 
   Rajjaṃ sukhaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Ayaṃ loko paro loko brahmaloko sadevako 
 Diṭṭhiṃ  te nābhijānāti  gotamassa yasassino 
  
      Evābhikkantadassāviṃ                   atthi pañhena āgamaṃ 
 Kathaṃ lokaṃ avekkhantaṃ maccurājā na passati 
  
      Suññato lokaṃ avekkhassu mogharāja sadā sato 
 Attānudiṭṭhiṃ ūhacca evaṃ maccutaro siyā 
  
      Evaṃ lokaṃ avekkhantaṃ maccurājā na passati 
 Iti maṃ abhaṇi buddho sabbarogatikicchako 
  
      Saha gāthāvasānena kesamassuvivajjito 
 Kāsāvavatthavasano āsiṃ bhikkhu tathārahā 
  
      Saṃghikesu vihāresu na vasiṃ rogapiḷito 
 Mā vihāro padussīti vātarogehi piḷito   
  
      Saṃsārakūṭā āhitvā  susānā rathākāhi ca 
 Tato saṃghāṭikaṃ katvā dhārayiṃ lukhacīvaraṃ 
  
      Mahābhisakko tasmiṃ me guṇe tuṭṭho vināyako 
 Lukhacīvaradhārīnaṃ etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
      Puññapāpaparikkhīṇo sabbarogavivajjito 
 Sikhīva anupādāno nibabāyissamanāsavo 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgo va bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassaṃ sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mogharājatthero imaṃ gāthāyo abhisitthāti 
  
 Mogharājattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ 
  
 Kaccānavaggo catupaññāsamo 
  
   Diṭṭhiṃ no machasaṃ Diṭṭhaṃ no     Sīmu 
   Nābhijānāmi sīmu Machasaṃ Syā 
   Vācāyābhisupīḷito syā     
   Āhatvā sīmu 
  
                   
  
 Uddānaṃ   
  
 Kaccāno vakkalī thero mahākappinasavhayo 
 Dabbo kumāranāmo ca bāhiyo koṭṭhito vasī 
 Uruvelakassapo rādho mogharājā ca paṇḍito 
 Tīṇi gāthāsatānettha dvāsaṭṭhi ceva piṇḍitā 
  
     Lakuṇaṭakabhaddiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro                   nāma jino sabbadhammesu cakkhumā 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
  
      Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ seṭṭhiputto mahādhano 
 Jaṅghāvihāraṃ vicaraṃ saṃghārāmamagacchahaṃ  
  
      Tadā so lokapajjoto dhammaṃ desesi nāyako 
 Mañjussarānaṃ pavaraṃ sāvakaṃ abhikittayī 
  
      Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā kāraṃ katvā mahesino 
 Vanditvā satthuno pāde taṃ ṭhānambhipatthayiṃ 
  
      Tadā buddho viyākāsi saṃghamajjhe vināyako 
 Anāgatamhi addhāne lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ 
  
      Satasahasse ito  kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Bhaddiyo nāma nāmena hessati satthu sāvako 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇīdhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Dvānavute  ito kappe phusso uppajji nāyako 
 Durāsade duppasaho sabbalokuttamo jino 
  
      Caraṇena ca sampanno brahā uju patāpavā 
 Hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ  bahuṃ  mocesi bandhanā 
  
   Saṅghārāmaṃ agacchahaṃ machasaṃ 
   Satasahassito machasaṃ 
   Devanavute machasaṃ 
   Sabbasattānaṃ machasaṃ 
   Bahu machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Nandarāmavane tassa ahosiṃ phussakokilo   
 Gandhakuṭisamāsante ambarukkhe vasāmahaṃ 
  
      Tadā piṇḍāya gacchantaṃ dakkhiṇeyyaṃ jinuttamaṃ 
 Disvā cittaṃ pasādetvā mañjunādena kūjahaṃ   
  
      Rājuyyānaṃ tadā gantvā supakkaṃ kanakattacaṃ 
 Ambapiṇḍiṃ  gahetvāna sambuddhassopanāmayiṃ 
  
      Tadā me cittamaññāya mahākāruṇiko jino 
 Upaṭṭhākassa hatthano pattā paggaṇhi nāyako 
  
      Adāsiṃ                   tuṭṭhacittohaṃ  ambapiṇḍiṃ mahāmune 
 Patte pakkhippa pakkhehañjaliṃ katvāna mañjunā 
  
      Sarena rajanīyena sacaṇīyena vaggunā 
 Vassanto buddhajūjatthaṃ niḷaṃ  gantvā nipajjahaṃ 
  
      Tadā muditacittaṃ maṃ buddhapemagatāsayaṃ 
 Sakuṇagghiṃ upāgantvā ghātayī duṭṭhamānaso 
  
      Tato cutohaṃ tusite anubhotvā mahāsukhaṃ 
 Manussayonimāgacchiṃ tassa kammassa vāhasā 
  
      Imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma gottena uppajji vadataṃvaro 
  
      Sāsanaṃ jotayitvā so abhibhuyya kutitthiye 
 Vinayitvāna veneyye nibbuto so sasāvako 
  
      Nibbute tamhi lokagge pasannā janatā bahu 
 Pūjanatthāya buddhassa thūpā kubbanti satthuno 
  
      Sattayojanikaṃ thūpaṃ sattaratanabhūsitaṃ 
 Karissāma mahesissa iccevaṃ mantayanti te 
  
      Kikito kāsirājassa tadā senāya nāyako 
 Hutvāhaṃ appamāṇassa pamāṇaṃ cetiye vadiṃ 
  
      Tadā te mama vākyena cetiyaṃ yojanuggataṃ 
 Akaṃsu naravīrassa nānāratanabhūsitaṃ 
  
      Tena kammena saketena cetanāpaṇīdhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
   Pussakokilo syā 
   Mañjunābhinikujahaṃ machasaṃ 
   Ambapiṇḍaṃ machasaṃ 
   Haṭṭhacittohaṃ machasaṃ 
   Niḍḍaṃ syā     
  
                   
  
      Pacchime ca bhavedāni jāto seṭṭhikule ahaṃ 
 Sāvatthiyaṃ puravare phīte mahaddhane 
  
      Purappavese sugataṃ disvā vimhitamānaso 
 Pabbatvājāna na ciraṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Cetiyassa pamāṇaṃ yaṃ akariṃ tena kammutā 
 Lakuṇṭakasarīrohaṃ jāto paribhavāraho 
  
      Sarena madhurenāhaṃ pūjetvā isisattamaṃ 
 Mañjussarānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ aggattamanupāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Phaladānena                   buddhassa guṇānussaraṇena ca 
 Sāmaññaphalasampanno viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā lakuṇaṭakabhaddiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Lakuṇaṭakabhaddiyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ 
  
     Kaṅkhārevatattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro                   nāma jino sabbadhammesu cakkhumā 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
  
      Sīhahanu brahmagiro haṃsadundūbhinissaro  
 Nāgavikkantagamano candasurādhikappabho  
  
      Mahāmati mahāvīro mahājhāyī bahābalo   
 Mahākāruṇiko nātho mahātamapanūdano  
  
   Haṃsadundunissano machasaṃ   nisāvano syā   Nissavano     
   Candasurādikappabho machasaṃ 
   Mahāgati syā Mahābhito     
   Mahātamavidhaṃsato syā mahātamanisudano     
                   
  
      Sakadāci tilokaggo veneyye vinayaṃ bahu   
 Dhamma desesi sambuddho sattāsayavidū muni 
  
      Jhāyi jhānarataṃ vīraṃ upasantaṃ anāvilaṃ 
 Vaṇṇayanto parisatiṃ tosesi  janatā jino 
  
      Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ brāhmaṇo vedapāragu 
 Dhammaṃ sutvāna mudito taṃ ṭhānambhipatthayiṃ 
  
      Tadā jino viyākāsi saṅghamajjhe vināyako 
 Mudito hehi tvaṃ brahme lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena hessasi  satthusāvako 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Revato nāma nāmena hessasi  satthusāvako 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehi tāvatisamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Pacchime ca bhave dāni jātohaṃ koliye pure 
 Khattiye kulasampanne iddhe phīte mahaddhane 
  
      Yadā                   kapilavatthusmiṃ buddho dhammamadesayi 
 Tadā pasanno sugate pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Kaṅkhā me bahulā āsi kappākappe tahiṃ tahiṃ 
 Sabbaṃ taṃ vinayī buddho desetvā dhammamuttamaṃ 
  
      Tatohaṃ tiṇṇasaṃsāro sadā jhānasukhe rato 
 Viharāmi tadā buddho maṃ disvā etadabravi 
  
      Yaṃ kāci kaṅkhā idha vā huraṃ vā 
 Sakavediyā vā paravediyā vā 
 Ye jhāyino tā pajahanti sabbā 
 Ātāpino brahmacariyaṃ carantā 
  
   Bahuṃ machasaṃ 
   Toseti syā     
   Hessati machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Satasahasse kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha 
 Sumutto saravegova kilese jhāpayī  mama 
  
      Tato jhānarataṃ disvā buddho lokantagū muni 
 Jhāyīnaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ aggo paññāpesi  mahāmati 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā khaṅkhārevato thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Kaṅkhārevatattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ 
  
     Sīvalittherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammesu cakkhumā 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
  
      Sīlaṃ tassa asaṅkheyyaṃ samādhi vajirūpamo 
 Asaṅkheyyaṃ ñāṇavaraṃ vimutti ca anūpamā 
  
      Manujāmaranāgānaṃ brahmānaṃ ca samāgame samaṇabrāhmaṇākiṇṇe dhammaṃ desesi nāyako 
  
      Sasāvakaṃ mahālābhiṃ puññavantaṃ jutindharaṃ 
 Ṭhapesi etadaggamhi parisāsu visārado 
  
      Tadāhaṃ khattiyo āsiṃ nagare haṃsasavhaye 
 Sutvā jinassa taṃ vākyaṃ sāvakassa guṇaṃ bahuṃ 
  
      Nimantayitvā                   sattāhaṃ bhojayitvā sasāvakaṃ 
 Mahādānaṃ daditvāna taṃ ṭhānambhipatthayiṃ 
  
      Tadā maṃ cittaṃ pāde disvāna purisāsabho 
 Sussarena mahāvīro idaṃ vacanamabravī 
  
   Jhāpayiṃ machasaṃ 
   Paññāpeti machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Tato jinassa vacanaṃ sotukāmā mahājanā 
 Devadānavagandhabbā brahmāno ca mahiddhikā 
  
      Samaṇabrāhmaṇā ceva namassiṃsu katañjalī 
 Namo te purisājaññā namo te purisuttama 
  
      Khattiyena mahādānaṃ dinnaṃ sattāhikaṃ yi vo   
 Sotukāmā phalaṃ tassa vyākarohi mahāmune 
  
      Tato avoca bhagavā suṇātha mama bhāsitaṃ 
 Appameyyamhi buddhamhi saṅghamhi suppatiṭṭhitā   
  
      Dakkhiṇā tāya ko vattā appameyyaphalā hi sā 
 Apivesa mahābhogo ṭhānaṃ pattheti uttamaṃ 
  
      Lābhī vipullābhānaṃ yathā bhikkhu sudassano 
 Tathāhampi bhaveyyanti lacchatetaṃ anāgate 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Sīvali nāma nāmesa hessati satthusāvako 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsūpago ahaṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe vipassī lokanāyako 
 Uppajji cārunayano  sabbadhammavipassako 
  
      Tadāhaṃ bandhumatiyaṃ kulassaññatarassa ca 
 Dayito patthito ceva  āsiṃ kammantavyāvaṭo  
  
      Tadā aññataro pūgo vipassissa mahesino 
 Parivesaṃ akāresi  mahantamativissutaṃ 
  
      Tiṭṭhite                   ca mahādāne dadaṃ  khajjakasaṃhitaṃ  
 Navaṃ dadhiṃ madhuṃ ceva vicinaṃ neva addasa  
  
      Tadāhaṃ taṃ gahetvāna navaṃ dadhiṃ madhumpi ca 
 Kammassāmigharaṃ gacchiṃ tamesantā mamaddasuṃ 
  
   Sattabhikādhikaṃ syā sattāhikampi co machasaṃ 
   Patiṭṭhitā machasaṃ 
   Cārudassano machasaṃ 
   Passito ceva machasaṃ 
   Vāvaṭo machasaṃ 
   Akāreyi 
   Daduṃ machasaṃ 
   Khajjakasañhitaṃ machasaṃ 
   Addasuṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Sahassampi datvāna nālahiṃsu ca taṃ dvayaṃ 
 Tatohaṃ evaṃ cintesiṃ netaṃ hessati orakaṃ 
  
      Yathā ime janā sabbe sakkaronti tathāgataṃ 
 Ahampi kāraṃ kassāmi sasaṅghe lokanāyake 
  
      Tadāhamevaṃ cintetvā dadhiṃ madhuñca ekato 
 Madditvā lokanāthassa sasaṅghassa adāsahaṃ 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇīdhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
      Punāhaṃ bārāṇasiyaṃ rājā hutvā mahāyaso 
 Sattukassa tadā ruṭṭho  dvārarodhaṃ akārayiṃ 
  
      Tadā sapattino  ruddhā sattāhaṃ  rakkhitā ahuṃ 
 Tato tassa vipākena papatiṃ  nirayaṃ bhūsaṃ 
  
      Pacchime ca bhave dāni jātohaṃ koliye pure 
 Suppavāyā ca me mātā mahālilicchavī pitā 
  
      Khattiye puññakammena dvārarodhassa vāhasā 
 Sattavassāni nivasiṃ mātukucchimhi dukkhito 
  
      Sattāhaṃ dvāramūḷhohaṃ mahādukkhasamappito 
 Mātā me chandadānena evamāsi sudukkhitā 
  
      Svatthitohaṃ nikkhanto buddhena anukampito 
 Nikkhantadivaseyeva pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Upajjhā  sāriputto me moggallāno mahiddhiko 
 Kese oropayanto me anusāsi mahāmati 
  
      Kesesu                   chijjamānesu arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
 Devā nāgā manussā ca paccaye upanenti me 
  
      Padumuttaranāthañca vipassiñca vināyakaṃ 
 Yaṃ pūjayiṃ pamudito paccayehi visesato 
  
   Duṭṭho machasaṃ 
   Tapassito machasaṃ 
   Ekāhaṃ sabbattha 
   Pāpatiṃ machasaṃ Pāpiṭṭhaṃ syā 
   Upajjho sīmu 
  
                   
  
      Tato tesaṃ visesena  kammānaṃ vipuluttamaṃ 
 Lābhaṃ labhāmi sabbattha vane gāme jale thale 
  
      Revataṃ dassanatthāya yadā yāti vināyako 
 Tiṃsabhikkhusahassehi saha lokagganāyako 
  
      Tadā devopanītehi mamatthāya mahāmati 
 Paccayehi mahāvīro sasaṅgho lokanāyako 
  
      Upaṭṭhito mayā buddho gantvā revatamaddasa 
 Tato jetavanaṃ gantvā etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
      Lābhīnaṃ sivalī aggo mama sissesu bhikkhavo 
 Sabbalokahito satthā kittayī parisāsu maṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sīvalī thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Sīvalittherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ 
  
     Vaṅgīsattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammesu cakkhumā 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
  
      Yathāpi sāgare ūmi gagane viya tārakā 
 Evaṃ pāvacanaṃ tassa arahantehi cittitaṃ 
  
      Sa devāsuranāgehi manujehi purakkhato 
 Samaṇabrāhmaṇākiṇṇe janamajjhe januttamo 
  
      Pabhābhi anurañjento  lokaṃ  lokantagū jino 
 Vacanena vibodhento veneyyapadumāni so 
  
   Vipākena sīmu 
   Anurañjananto machasaṃ 
   Loke machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Vesārajjehi sampanno catūhi purisuttamo 
 Pahīnabhayasārajjo khemappatto visārado 
  
      Āsahaṃ                   pavaraṃ ṭhānaṃ buddhabhūmiṃ ca kevalaṃ 
 Paṭijānāti lokaggo natthi sañcodako kvaci 
  
      Sīhanādamasambhītaṃ nadato tassa tādino 
 Devo naro vā brammā vā paṭivattā na vijjati 
  
      Desento pavaraṃ dhammaṃ santārento sadevakaṃ 
 Dhammacakkaṃ pavatteti parisāsu visārado 
  
      Paṭibhānavataṃ aggaṃ sāvakaṃ sādhusammataṃ 
 Guṇaṃ bahuṃ pakittetvā etadagge ṭhapesi taṃ 
  
      Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ brāhmaṇo sādhusammato 
 Sabbavedavidu jāto vaṅgīso  vādisudano 
  
      Upecca taṃ mahāvīraṃ sutvā taṃ dhammadesanaṃ 
 Pītivaraṃ paṭilabhiṃ sāvakassa guṇe rato 
  
      Nimattayitvā  sugataṃ sasaṅghaṃ lokanandanaṃ 
 Sattāhaṃ bhojayitvāhaṃ dussehacchādayiṃ tadā 
  
      Nipacca sirasā pāde katokāso katañjalī 
 Ekamantaṃ ṭhito haṭṭho santhaviṃ jinamuttamaṃ 
  
       Namo te vādisaddūla  namo te purisuttama   
 Namo te sabbalokagga namo te abhayaṅkara 
  
      Namo te māramathana namo te diṭṭhisudana 
 Namo te santisukhada namo te saraṇaṅkara 
  
      Anāthānaṃ bhavaṃ nātho bhītānaṃ abhayappado 
 Vissāmabhūmi  sattānaṃ saraṇaṃ saraṇesitaṃ 
  
   Vāgīso sīmu 
   Nimantetvāva machasaṃ 
   Vādimaddana machasaṃ 
   Isisattama machasaṃ 
   Vissāsaṃ bhūmi syā Vissāsabhūmi     
  
                   
  
      Evamādīhi sambuddhaṃ santhavitvā mahāguṇaṃ 
 Avocaṃ vādisūrassa  gatiṃ pappomi bhikkhūno 
  
      Tadā avoca bhagavā anantapaṭibhānavā 
 Yo so buddhaṃ abhojesi sattāhaṃ saha sāvakaṃ 
  
      Guṇaṃ ca me pakittesi pasanto sehi pāṇihi 
 Eso patthayate ṭhānaṃ vādisūrassa bhikkhuno 
  
      Anāgatamhi                   addhāne lacchate taṃ manorathaṃ 
 Devamānusasampattiṃ anubhotvā anappakaṃ 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Vaṅgīso nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvako 
  
      Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ 
 Paccayehi upaṭṭhāsi mettacitto tathāgataṃ 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tusitaṃ  agamāsahaṃ 
  
      Pacchime ca bhavedāni paribbājakule  ahaṃ 
 Paccājāto yadā āsiṃ jātiyā sattavassiko 
  
      Sabbavedavidū jāto vādasatthavisārado 
 Vādissaro cittakathi paravādappamaddano 
  
      Vaṅge jātoti vaṅgiso vacane issaroti vā 
 Vaṅgīso iti me nāmaṃ abhavī lokasammataṃ 
  
      Yadāhaṃ viññutaṃ patto ṭhito paṭhamayobbane 
 Tadā rājagahe ramme sāriputtamathaddasaṃ  
  
 Pañcavisatimaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ 
  
      Piṇḍāya vicarantaṃ taṃ pattapāṇiṃ susaṃvutaṃ 
 Alolakkhiṃ mitabhāṇiṃ yugamattanirikkhakaṃ   
  
   Vādisudassa machasaṃ 
   Tāvatiṃsaṃ syā 
   Jāto vippakule machasaṃ 
   Sāriputtamabhaddasaṃ machasaṃ Ca addasaṃ syā 
   Nidakkhitaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Taṃ disvā vimhito hutvā avocaṃ mananucchavaṃ  
 Khaṇikaṃ ṭhānaracitaṃ  cittaṃ gāthāpadaṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Ācikkhi so me satthāraṃ sambuddhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Tadā so paṇḍito vīro uttaraṃ  samavoca me 
  
      Virāgasaṃhitaṃ vākyaṃ katvā duddasamuttamaṃ 
 Vicittapaṭibhānehi tosito tena tādinā 
 Nipacca sirasā pāde pabbājehīti maṃ braviṃ 
  
      Tato maṃ sa mahāpañño buddhaseṭṭhamupānayi 
 Nipacca sirasā pāde nisīdiṃ satthu sattike 
  
      Mamāha vadanaṃ seṭṭho kacci vaṅgīsa jānasi   
 Kiñci sippanti tassāhaṃ jānāmi ti ca abraviṃ   
  
      Matasīsaṃ                   vanacchaddhaṃ api bārasavassikaṃ 
 Tava vijjāvisesena sace sakkosi bhāsaya   
  
      Āmāti me paṭiññāte tīṇi sīsāni dassayī 
 Niraya nara devesu upapanne avācayiṃ 
  
      Tadā paccekabuddhassa  siraṃ dassesi nāyako 
 Tatohaṃ vihatārambho pabbajjaṃ samayācisaṃ 
  
      Pabbajitvāna sugataṃ santhavāmi tahiṃ tahiṃ 
 Tato maṃ kabbavīttoti  ujjhāyantiha bhikkhavo 
  
      Tato vimaṃsanatthaṃ me āha buddho vināyako 
 Takkitā panimā gāthā ṭhānaso paṭibhanti vā 
  
      Na kabbavittohaṃ vīra ṭhānaso paṭibhanti maṃ   
 Tena hi dāni vaṅgīsa ṭhānaso santhavāhi maṃ 
  
   Mamanucchaṃ machasaṃ 
   Kaṇikāraṃvanicitaṃ machasaṃ 
   Uttariṃ machasaṃ 
   Saccaṃ vaṅgīsa kaccino syā 
   Braciṃ machasaṃ 
   Vācāya machasaṃ 
   Khīṇasavasseva machasaṃ 
   Kavicittoti syā     
   Taṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Tadāhaṃ santhaviṃ vīraṃ gāthāhi isisattamaṃ 
 Ṭhānāso me tadā tuṭṭho jino agge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
      Paṭibhānena cittena aññe samatimaññahaṃ 
 Pesale tena saṃviggo arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Paṭibhānavataṃ aggo añño koci na vijjati 
 Yathāyaṃ bhikkhu vaṅgīso evaṃ dhāretha bhikkhavo 
  
      Satasahasse kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha 
 Sumutto saravegova kilese jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ  
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vaṅgīso thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Vaṅgīsattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ 
  
     Nandakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro                   nāma jino sabbadhammesu cakkhumā 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
  
      Hitāya sabbasattānaṃ sukhāya vadataṃ varo 
 Atthāya purisājañño paṭipanno sadevake 
  
      Yasaggappatto sirimā kittivaṇṇabhato  jino 
 Pūjito sabbalokassa disāsabbāsu vissuto 
  
      Uttiṇṇavicikiccho so vītivattakathaṃkatho 
 Paripuṇṇamanasaṃkappo patto sambodhimuttamaṃ 
  
   Jhāpayiṃ mama sīmu 
   Kittivaṇṇabhaṭo syā 
  
                   
  
      Anuppannassa maggassa uppādetā naruttamo 
 Anakkhātañca akkhāsi asañjātaṃ ca sañjanī 
  
      Maggaññū so maggavidū  maggakkhāyī nārāsabho 
 Maggassa kusalo satthā sārathīnaṃ varuttamo 
  
      Tadā mahākāruṇiko dhammaṃ deseti  nāyako 
 Nimugge mohapaṅkamhi  samuddharati pāṇito  
  
      Bhikkhūnīnaṃ ovadane sāvakaṃ seṭṭhasammataṃ 
 Vaṇṇayaṃ etadaggamhi paññāpesi mahāmuni 
  
      Taṃ sutvāhaṃ pamudito nimantetvā tathāgataṃ 
 Bhojayitvā sasaṅghaṃ taṃ patthayiṃ ṭhānamuttamaṃ 
  
      Tadā pamudito nātho maṃ avoca mahāisi 
 Sukhī bhavassu dighāyu  lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Nandako nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvako 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsupago ahaṃ 
  
      Pacchime ca bhavedāni jāto seṭṭhikule ahaṃ 
 Sāvatthiyaṃ puravare  iddhe phīte mahaddhane 
  
      Purappavese sugataṃ disvā vimhitamānaso 
 Jetārāmapaṭiggāhe pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Na                   cireneva kālena arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
 Tatohi tiṇṇasaṃsāro sāsito sabbadassitā 
  
   Maggaññūmaggavidu ca machasaṃ 
   Desesī machasaṃ 
   Kāmapaṅkamhi machasaṃ 
   Pāṇine machasaṃ 
   Dighāvu machasaṃ 
   Pure vare machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Bhikkhūnīnaṃ dhammakathaṃ paṭipucchā kariṃ ahaṃ 
 Sāsitā tā mayā sabbā abhaviṃsu anāsavā 
  
      Satāni pañcanūnāni tadā tuṭṭho mahāhito 
 Bhikkhunīnaṃ ovadataṃ aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
      Satasahasse kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha 
 Sumutto saravegova kilese jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nandako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Nandakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ 
  
     Kāḷudāyittherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammesu cakkhumā 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
  
      Nāyakānaṃ varo satthā guṇāguṇavidu jino 
 Kataññu katavedi ca titthe yojeti pāṇino  
  
      Sabbaññutena ñāṇena tulayitvā dayāsayo 
 Deseti pavaraṃ dhammaṃ anantaguṇasañcayo 
  
      Sa kadāci mahāvīro anantajanasaṃsadi  
 Deseti madhuraṃ dhammaṃ catusaccupasaṃhitaṃ 
  
      Sutvāna taṃ dhammavaraṃ ādimajjhantasobhanaṃ 
 Pāṇasatasahassānaṃ dhammābhisamayo ahu 
  
   Jhāpayiṃ mama sīmu 
   Pāṇine machasaṃ 
   Anantajinasaṃsari machasaṃ Anantajanasaṃsudhi syā Anantajanataṃsari     
  
                   
  
      Ninnāditā tadā bhūmi gajjiṃsu ca payodharā 
 Sādhukāraṃ pavattesuṃ  devabrahmanarāsurā 
  
      Aho kāruṇiko satthā aho saddhammadesanā 
 Aho bhavasamuddamhi nimugge uddharī jino 
  
      Evaṃ pavedajātesu  satarāmarabrahmasu 
 Kulappasādakānaggaṃ sāvakaṃ vaṇṇayī jino 
  
      Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ jātomaccakule ahuṃ 
 Pasādiko dassanīyo pahūtadhanadhaññavā 
  
      Haṃsārāma                   mupeccāhaṃ vanditvā taṃ tathāgataṃ 
 Suṇitvā madhuraṃ dhammaṃ kāraṃ katvā ca tādino 
  
      Nipacca pādamūlehaṃ imaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
 Kulappasādakānaggo yo tayā santhūto  mune 
  
      Tādiso hemahaṃ vīra  buddhaseṭṭhassa sāsane 
 Tadā mahākāruṇiko siñcantovāmatena maṃ   
  
      Āha maṃ putta uttiṭṭha lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ 
 Kathaṃ nāma jine kāraṃ katvāna viphalo siyā 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Udāyi nāma nāmena hessati satthū sāvako 
  
      Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ 
 Mettacitto paricariṃ paccayehi vināyakaṃ 
  
      Tena kammavipākena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Pacchime ca bhavedāni ramme kāpilavatthave 
 Jāto mahāmaccakule suddhodanamahīpate 
  
      Yadā ajāyi siddhattho ramme lumbinikānate 
 Hitāya sabbalokassa sukhāya ca narāsabho 
  
   Pavantiṃsu machasaṃ 
   Saṃvegajātesu sīmu 
   Yo tava sāsane syā 
   Tādisohaṃ mahāvīra syā 
  
                   
  
      Tadaheva ahaṃ jāto saha teneva vaḍḍhito 
 Piyo sahāyo dayito viyatto tītikovido 
  
      Ekūnatiṃso vayasā nikkhanto pabbajittha so   
 Chabbassaṃ vītināmetvā buddho āsi vināyako 
  
      Jetvā sasenakaṃ māraṃ khepayitvā āsave 
 Bhavaṇṇavaṃ taritvāna āsi buddho sadevake   
  
      Isivhayaṃ gamitvāna  vinetvā pañcavaggiye 
 Tato vinesi bhagavā gantvā gantvā tahiṃ tahiṃ 
  
      Veneyye vinayanto so saṃgaṇahanto sadevakaṃ 
 Upecca māgadhagiriṃ  viharittha tadā jino 
  
      Tadā                   suddhodanenāhaṃ bhūmipālena pesito 
 Gantvā disvā dasabalaṃ pabbajitvārahā ahuṃ 
  
      Tadā mahesiṃ yācitvā pāpayiṃ kapilavhayaṃ 
 Tato purāhaṃ gantvāna pasādesiṃ mahākulaṃ 
  
      Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho maṃ mahāparisāya so   
 Kulappasādakānaggaṃ paññāpesi vināyako 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kāḷudāyi thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Kāḷudāyittherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ 
  
     Abhayattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammesu cakkhumā 
 Ito satasamassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
  
      Saraṇagamane kañci  niveseti tathāgato 
 Kañci sīle niveseti dasakammapathuttame 
  
   Nikkhamitvā agārato machasaṃ 
   Buddho āsi sadevake machasaṃ   Isivhayaṃ pattaṃ gantvā syā 
   Magadhe giriṃ machasaṃ Maṅgalāgiriṃ     
   Mamāha purisāsabho syā     
   Kiñci machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Deti kassavi so vīro sāmaññaphalamuttamaṃ 
 Samāpatti tathā aṭṭha tisso vijjā pavecchati   
  
      Chaḷabhiññāsu yojeti kañci sattaṃ naruttamo 
 Deti kassaci so nātho catasso paṭisambhidā 
  
      Bodhaneyyaṃ pajaṃ disvā asaṅkheyye pi yojane   
 Khaṇena upagantvāna vineti narasārathi 
  
      Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ ahosiṃ brāhmaṇatrajo 
 Pāragu sabbavedānaṃ veyyākaraṇasammato 
  
      Niruttiyā ca kusalo nighaṇṭumhi visārado 
 Padako keṭubhavidu chandovicitikovido 
  
      Jaṅghāvihāraṃ vivaraṃ haṃsārāmamupeccahaṃ 
 Addasaṃ vadataṃ seṭṭhaṃ  mahājanapurakkhataṃ 
  
      Desentaṃ virajaṃ dhammaṃ paccanīkamatī ahaṃ 
 Upetvā tassa vākyāti sutvāna vimalānahaṃ   
  
      Vyāhaṭaṃ                    punaruttaṃ vā apatthaṃ vā niratthakaṃ 
 Nāddasaṃ tassa munito tato pabbajito ahaṃ 
  
      Na cireneva kālena sabbasatthavisārado 
 Nipuṇo buddhavacane ahosiṃ gaṇisammato 
  
      Tadā catasso gāthāyo ganthayitvā suvyañjanā 
 Santhavitvā tilokaggaṃ desayissaṃ dine dine 
  
      Virattoyiṃ mahāvīra saṃsāre sabhaye vasaṃ 
 Karuṇāya na nibbāyi tato kāruṇiko muni 
  
      Puthujjanova yo santo na kilesavaso ahu 
 Sampajāno satiyutto tasmā eso acintiyo 
  
   Pavacchati machasaṃ 
   Asaṅkheyyampiyojanaṃ machasaṃ 
   Varadaṃ seṭṭhaṃ machasaṃ Pavaraṃ seṭṭhaṃ syā 
   Vākyānaṃ machasaṃ 
   Vyāhataṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Dubbalāni kilesāni yassāsayagatānime 
 Ñāṇaggiparidaḍḍhāni na khīyiṃsu tadabbhutaṃ  
  
      Yo sabbalokassa garu loko yassa tathā garu 
 Tthāpi lokācariyo loko tassānuvattako 
  
      Evamādīhi sambuddhaṃ kittayaṃ dhammadesanaṃ 
 Yāvajīvaṃ karitvāna gato saggaṃ tato cuto 
  
      Evamādīhi sambuddhaṃ kittayaṃ dhammadesanaṃ 
 Yāvajīvaṃ karitvāna gato saggaṃ tato cuto 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ buddhambhikittayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Devaloke mahārajjaṃ rajjā pādesikaṃ ca yaṃ   
 Cakkavattimahārajjaṃ bahusonubhaviṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Duve bhave pajāyāmi devatte atha mānuse 
 Aññaṃ gatiṃ na jānāmi kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Duve kule pajāyāmi khattiye atha brāhmaṇe
