 Nīce kule na jāyāmi kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Pacchime ca bhave dāni giribbajapuruttame 
 Raññohaṃ bimbisārassa putto nāmena cābhayo 
  
      Pāpamittavasaṃ gantvā nigaṇṭhena vimohito 
 Pesito nātaputtena  buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upeccahaṃ 
  
      Puccitvā                   nipuṇaṃ pañhaṃ sutvā vyākaraṇuttamaṃ 
 Pabbajitvāna naciraṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Kittayitvā jinavaraṃ kittito bhomi sabbadā 
 Sugandhadehavadano āsiṃ sukhasamappito 
  
      Tikkha hāsu lahupañño  mahāpañño tathevahaṃ 
 Vicittapaṭibhāno ca tassa kammassa vāhasā 
  
      Abhitthavitvā padumuttarābyaṃ  
 Pasannacitto asamaṃ sayambhuṃ 
 Na gacchi kappāni apāyabhūmiṃ 
 Sataṃ sahassāni phalena tassa 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
   Tambabhūtaṃ machasaṃ 
   Pādesiṃ kañcanagghiyaṃ machasaṃ   Nāṭaputtena sīmu 
   Tikkhabhāsalahupaññā machasaṃ 
   Padumuttarāhaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā abhayatthero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Abhayattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ 
  
     Lomasakaṅgiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma nāmena  uppajji vadanaṃ varo 
  
      Tadāhaṃ candano ceva pabbajitvāna sāsane 
 Āpāṇakoṭikaṃ dhammaṃ pūrayitvāna sāsane  
  
      Tato cutā santusitaṃ upapannā ubho mayaṃ Tattha dibbehi naccehi gītehi vāditehi ca  
  
      Rūpādidasahaṅgehi abhibhotvāna sesake 
 Yāvatāyuṃ vasitvāna anubhotvā mahāsukhaṃ  
  
      Tato cavitvā tidasaṃ candano upapajjatha 
 Ahaṃ kapilavatthusmiṃ ahosiṃ  sākiyatrajo 
  
      Yadā udāyitherena ajjhiṭṭho lokanāyako 
 Anukampiya sakyānaṃ upesi kapilavhayaṃ 
  
      Tadātimānino sakyā na buddhassa guṇaññuno 
 Panamanti na sambuddhaṃ jātitthaddhā anādarā 
  
      Tesaṃ                   saṅkappamaññāya ākāse caṅkamī jino 
 Pajjunno viya vassittha pajjalittha yathā sīkhi 
  
      Dassetvā rūpamatulaṃ puna antaradhāyatha 
 Ekopi hutvā bahudhā ahosi punarekako 
  
      Andhakāraṃ pakāsaṃ ca dassayitvā anekadhā 
 Pāṭihīraṃ  karitvāna vinayī ñātake muni 
  
   Gottena machasaṃ 
   Ajāyiṃ machasaṃ 
   Pāṭiheraṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Cātuddīpo mahāmegho tāvade sampavassatha   
 Tadā hi jātakaṃ buddho vessantaramadesayi 
  
      Tadā te khattiyā sabbe tihantvā jātijaṃ madaṃ 
 Upesuṃ saraṇaṃ buddhaṃ   āha suddhodano tadā 
  
      Idaṃ tatiyaṃ tava bhūripañña 
 Pādāni vandāmi samantacakkhu 
 Yadābhijāno paṭhaviṃ  pakampayi 
 Yadā ca taṃ tajjahi jambuchāyā 
  
      Tadā buddhānubhāvaṃ taṃ disvā vimhitamānaso 
 Pabbajitvāna tattheva nivasiṃ mātupūjako 
  
      Candano devaputto maṃ upagantvānapucchatha 
 Bhaddekarattassa tadā saṃkhepavitthāranayaṃ  
  
      Coditohaṃ tadā tena upecca naranāyakaṃ 
 Bhaddekarattaṃ sutvāna saṃviggo vanamāmako 
  
      Tadā mātaramāpucchiṃ  vane vacchāmi ekako 
 Sukhumāloti me mātā vārayi taṃ tadāvacaṃ 
  
      Dabbaṃ kusaṃ  poṭakilaṃ usīraṃ muñjababbajaṃ  
 Urasā panudissāmi vivekamanubrūhayaṃ 
  
      Tadā vanaṃ paviṭṭhohaṃ saritvā jinasāsanaṃ 
 Bhaddekarattaovādaṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Atitaṃ                   nanvāgameyya nappaṭikaṃkhe anāgataṃ 
 Yadititaṃ pahīnaṃ taṃ appattañca anāgataṃ 
  
      Paccuppannañca yo dhammaṃ tattha tattha vipassati 
 Asaṃhīraṃ asaṃkuppaṃ taṃ vidvā anubrūhaye 
  
   Tāvadeva pavassatha machasaṃ 
   Pathavī machasaṃ 
   Saṅkhepavitthāraṃ nayaṃ machasaṃ 
   Tadāmātaramapucchiṃ machasaṃ 
   Te machasaṃ 
   Muñjapabbajaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Ajjeva kiccaṃ ātappaṃ ko jaññā maraṇaṃ suve 
 Na hi no saṃgaraṃ tena mahāsenena maccunā 
      Evaṃ viharamātāpī  ahorattamatanditaṃ 
 Taṃ ve bhaddekarattoti santo ācikkhate muni 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā lomasakaṅgiyo  thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Lomasakaṅgiyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ 
  
     Vanavacchattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma nāmena  uppajji vadataṃvaro 
  
      Tadāhaṃ pabbajitvāna tassa buddhassa sāsane 
 Yāvajīvaṃ caritvāna brahmacariyaṃ tato cuto 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Tato cuto araññamhi kapoto āsahaṃ tahiṃ 
 Vasate guṇasampanno bhikkhu jhānarato sadā   
      Mettacitto kāruṇiko sadā pamuditānano 
 Upekkhako mahāvīro appamaññāsu kovido 
  
      Vinīvaraṇasaṅkappe sabbasattahitāsaye 
 Vissattho  nacirenāsiṃ tasmiṃ sugatasāvake 
  
      Upecca                   pādamūlamhi nisinnassa tadā sa me   
 Kadāci āmisaṃ deti dhammaṃ deseti cekadā 
  
   Vihāriṃ ātāpiṃ machasaṃ 
   Lomasaṃkhiyo syā 
   Gottena machasaṃ 
   Visaṭṭho machasaṃ 
   Tadāssame machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Tadā vipulapemeta upāsitvā jinatrajaṃ 
 Tato cuto gato saggaṃ pavāsā  sagharaṃ yathā 
  
      Saggā cuto manussesu nibbatto puññakammunā 
 Agāraṃ chaḍḍayitvāna pabbajiṃ lahuso ahaṃ 
  
      Samaṇo tāpaso vippo paribbājo tathevahaṃ 
 Hutvā vāsiṃ araññamhi anekasataso ahaṃ 
  
      Pacchime ca bhade dāni ramme kāpilavatthave  
 Vacchagotto dvijo  tassa jāyāya ahamokkamiṃ 
  
      Mātu me dohaḷo āsi tirokucchigatassa me 
 Jāyamānasamīpamhi vanavāsāya nicchayo 
  
      Tato me ajanī mātā ramanīye vanantare 
 Gabbhato nikkhamantaṃ maṃ kāsāyena paṭiggahuṃ 
  
      Tato kumāro siddhattho jāto sakyakuladdhajo 
 Tassa mitto piyo āsiṃ saṃvissattho sumāniyo 
  
      Sattasārehi nikkhante ohāya vipulaṃ yasaṃ 
 Ahampi pabbajitvāna himavantamupāgamiṃ 
  
      Vanālayaṃ bhāvanīyaṃ kassapaṃ dhūtavādakaṃ  
 Disvā sutvā jinuppādaṃ upesiṃ narasārathiṃ 
  
      So me dhammamadesesi sabbatthaṃ sampakāsayaṃ 
 Tatohaṃ pabbajitvāna vanameva punāgamiṃ  
  
      Tatthāppamatto  viharaṃ chalabhiññā aphassayiṃ  
 Aho suladdhalābhomhi sumittenānukampito 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vanavaccho thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Vanavacchattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ 
  
   Pavāso machasaṃ 
   Kapilavatthave machasaṃ   Dijo machasaṃ 
   Dhūtavādikaṃ machasaṃ 
   Pūnāgamaṃ machasaṃ 
   Tatthappamatto sīmu 
   Apassayiṃ syā 
  
                   
  
     Cūḷasugandhattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Imamhi                   bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma nāmena  uppajji vadataṃ varo 
  
      Anuvyañjanasampanno battiṃsavaralakkhaṇo  
 Byāmappabhāparivuto raṃsijālasamotthato  
  
      Assāsetā yathā cando suriyova pabhaṅkaro 
 Nibbāpetā yathā megho sāgarova guṇākaro 
  
      Dharaṇiriva sīlena himavāva samādhinā 
 Ākāso viya paññāya asaṅgo anilo yathā 
  
      Tadāhaṃ bārāṇasiyaṃ upapanno mahākule 
 Pahūtadhanadhaññasmiṃ nānāratanasañcaye 
  
      Mahatā parivārena nisinnaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Upecca dhammamassosiṃ amataṃva manoharaṃ 
  
      Khattiṃsalakkhaṇadharo  sanakkhattova candimā 
 Anuvyañjanasampanno sālarājāva phullito 
  
      Raṃsijālaparikkhitto dittova kanakācalo 
 Byāmappabhāparivuto sarasmīva divākaro 
  
      Soṇṇānano jinavaro samaṇīva  siluccayo 
 Karuṇāpuṇṇahadayo guṇena viya sāgaro 
  
      Lokavissutakitti ca sinerūva naguttamo 
 Yasasā vitthato vīro ākāsasadiso muni 
  
      Asaṅgacitto sabbattha anilo viya nāyako 
 Patiṭṭhā sabbabhūtānaṃ mahīva muni sattamo 
  
      Anupalitto lokena toyena padumaṃ yathā 
 Kuvādagacchadahano aggikkhandhova sobhati  
  
      Agado viya sabbattha kilesavisanāsako 
 Gandhamādanaselova guṇagandhavibhusito 
  
      Guṇānaṃ ākaro vīro ratanānaṃva sāgaro 
 Sindhūva vanarājinaṃ kilesamalahārako 
  
   Gottena machasaṃ 
   Bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo machasaṃ 
   Samotthaṭo machasaṃ 
   Davattiṃsalakkhaṇadharo machasaṃ 
   Ramaṇīva syā 
   Sobhasi machasaṃ Sovasi syā 
  
                   
  
      Vijayīva                   mahāyodho mārasenappamaddano  
 Cakkavattīva so rājā bojjhaṅgaratanissaro 
  
      Mahābhisakkasaṅkāso dosavyādhitikicchako 
 Sallakatto yathā seṭṭho  diṭṭhigaṇḍaviphālako 
  
      So tadā lokapajjoto sanarāmarasakkato 
 Parisāsu narādicco dhammaṃ desayate jino 
  
      Dānaṃ datvā mahābhogo sīlena sugatūpago 
 Bhāvanāya ca nibbāti iccevamanusāsatha 
  
      Desanaṃ taṃ mahassādaṃ ādimajjhantasobhanaṃ 
 Suṇanti parisā sabbā amataṃva mahārasaṃ 
  
      Sutvā sumadhuraṃ dhammaṃ pasanno jinasāsane 
 Sugataṃ saraṇaṃ gantvā yāvajīvaṃ namassahaṃ 
  
      Munino gandhakuṭiyā opuñchesiṃ  tadā mahiṃ 
 Catujjātena gandhena māse aṭṭhadinesvahaṃ 
  
      Paṇidhāya sugandhattaṃ sarīrassa dugandhino  
 Tadā jino viyākāsi sugandhatanulābhitaṃ 
  
      Yo yaṃ gandhakuṭibhūmiṃ gandhenopuñchatesakiṃ 
 Tena kammavipākena upapanno tahiṃ tahiṃ 
  
      Sugandhadeho sabbattha bhavissati ayaṃ naro 
 Guṇakandhayuto  hutvā nibbāyissatanāsavo 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Pacchime ca bhave dāni jāto vippakule ahaṃ 
 Gabbhe me vasato mātā dehenāsi sugandhikā  
  
      Yadā ca mātukucchimhā nikkhamāmi tadā purī  
 Sāvatthi sabbagandhehi vāsitā viya vāyatha 
  
      Pupphavassaṃ ca surabhi dibbagandhamanoramaṃ 
 Dhūpāni ca mahagghāni upavāyiṃsu tāvade 
  
      Devā                   ca sabbagandhehi dhūpapupphehi taṃ gharaṃ 
 Vāsayiṃsu sugandhena yasmiṃ jāto ahaṃ ghare 
  
   Mārasenāvamaddano machasaṃ 
   Vejjo machasaṃ 
   Ubbaṭṭesiṃ syā   Sarīravissagandhino machasaṃ Vigandhino sīmu 
   Guṇagandhayutto machasaṃ 
   Sugandhitā machasaṃ 
   Puraṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Yadā ca taruṇo bhaddo paṭhame yobbane ṭhito 
 Tadā selaṃ  saparisaṃ vinetvā narasārathi  
  
      Tehi sabbehi sahito  sāvatthipuramāgato 
 Tadā buddhānubhāvaṃ taṃ disvā pabbajito ahaṃ 
  
      Sīlaṃ samādhiṃ paññañca  vimuttiñca anuttaraṃ 
 Bhāvetvā caturo dhamme pāpuṇiṃ āsavakkhayaṃ 
  
      Yadā pabbajito cāhaṃ yadā ca arahā ahuṃ 
 Nibbāyissaṃ yadā cāhaṃ gandhavasso tadā ahu 
  
      Sarīragandho ca sadātiseti me 
 Mahārahaṃ candanavampakuppalaṃ 
 Tatheva gandhe itare ca sabbaso 
 Pasayha vāyāmi gato tahiṃ  tahiṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā cūḷasugandho thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Cūḷasugandhattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ 
  
 Bhaddiyavaggo pañcapaññāsamo 
  
 Uddānaṃ   
  
 Bhaddiyo revato thero mahālābhi ca sīvalī 
 Vaṅgiso nandako ceva kāḷudāyi tathābhayo 
 Lomaso vanavaccho ca sugandho dasamo kato  
 Tīṇi gāthāsanā tattha soḷasa  ca taduttariṃ 
  
 Atha vagguddānaṃ   
  
 Kaṇikāravhayo vaggo phalado tiṇadāyako 
 Kaccāno bhaddiyo vaggo gāthāyo gaṇitā cimā 
 Navagāthā                   satānīha caturāsīti eva ca 
 Sapaññāsā pañcasatā  apadānā pakāsitā 
 Saha uddānagāthāhi chasahassani hontimā 
 Dve satāni ca gāthānaṃ aṭṭhārasa taduttariṃ 
  
   Sesaṃ syā 
   Parivuto machasaṃ 
   Sīlaṃsamādhipaññañca machasaṃ 
   Yahiṃ syā 
   Sugandho cevadasamo machasaṃ 
   Soḷasāca taduttari machasaṃ 
   Sapaññāsaṃ pañcasataṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Yasattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Mahāsamuddaṃ ogayha  bhavanaṃ me sunimmitaṃ 
 Sunimmitā pokkharaṇi cakkavākupakujitā 
  
      Mandālakehi  sañchannā padumuppalakehi ca 
 Nadī ca sandate tattha supatitthā manoramā 
  
      Macchakacchapasañchannā nānādijasamākulā  
 Mayurakoñcābhirudā kokilādibhi  vaggubhi 
  
      Pārevatā ravihāsā cakkavākā nadīvarā 
 Dindibhā  sāḷikā cettha pampakā jīvaṃjīvakā 
  
      Haṃsā koñcābhinaditā kosiyā piṅgalā bahū 
 Sattaratanasampannā maṇimuttikavālikā  
  
      Sabbe soṇṇamayā rukkhā nānāgandhasameritā 
 Ujjotenti divārattiṃ bhavanaṃ sabbakālikaṃta 
  
      Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni sāyaṃ pāto pavajjare 
 Soḷasitthisahassāni parivārenti maṃ sadā 
  
      Abhinikkhamma bhavanā sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano vandayiṃ taṃ mahāyasaṃ 
  
      Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā sasaṅghaṃ taṃ nimantayiṃ 
 Adhivāsesi so dhīro sumedho lokanāyako 
  
      Mama dhammakathaṃ katvā uyyojesi mahāmuni 
 Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā bhavanaṃ me upāgamiṃ 
  
      Āmantayiṃ parijanaṃ sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā 
 Pubbanhasamayaṃ buddho bhavanaṃ āgamissati 
  
      Lābhā amhaṃ suladdhā no ye vasāma navantike 
 Mayampi buddhaseṭṭhassa pūjayissāma satthuno 
  
      Annaṃ pānaṃ paṭṭhapetvā kālaṃ ārocayiṃ ahaṃ 
 Vasīsatasahassehi upesi lokanāyako 
  
      Pañcaṅgikehi turiyehi paccuggamamakāsahaṃ 
 Sabbasoṇṇamaye pīṭhe nisīdi purisuttamo 
  
      Uparicchadanaṃ āsi sabbasoṇṇamayaṃ tadā 
 Vījaniyo pavāyanti bhikkhusaṅghaṃ anuttaraṃ 
  
   Oggayha machasaṃ 
   Mandārakehi machasaṃ 
   Nānādijasamotthaṭā machasaṃ nānāmihasamotthaṭā syā 
   Kokilādīhi machasaṃ 
   Tittirā machasaṃ 
   Maṇimuttavāḷikā machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Pahūtenannapānena  bhikkhusaṅghaṃ atappayiṃ 
 Paccekadussayugale bhikkhusaṅghassadāhaṃ 
  
      Yaṃ vadanti sumedhoti  āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Bhikkhu saṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo me annena pānena sabbe ime ca tappayi 
 Tamhaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Aṭṭhārase kappasate devaloke ramissati 
 Sahassakkhattuṃ rājāyaṃ cakkavatti bhavissati 
  
      Upagacchati yaṃ yoniṃ devattaṃ athamānusaṃ 
 Sabbasoṇṇamayaṃ tassa chadanaṃ dhārayissati 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena  satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo 
  
      Bhikkhu saṅghe nisīditvā sīhanādaṃ nadissati 
 Citake chattaṃ dhārenti heṭṭhā chattamhi ḍayhatha   
  
      Sāmaññaṃ me anuppattaṃ kilesā jhāpitā mayā 
 Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā santāse me na vijjati 
  
      Tiṃsa kappasahassamhi yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhājānāmi sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā yaso thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Yasattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ 
  
   Pahute annapānena machasaṃ 
   Sumedho so machasaṃ 
   Gottena machasaṃ 
   Mama buddhassa machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Nadīkassapattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttarassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Piṇḍacāraṃ carantassa vārato uttamaṃ yasaṃ 
 Aggaphalaṃ gahetvāna adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ 
  
      Tena kammena devindo lokajeṭṭhā narāsabho 
 Sampattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ bhitvā jayaparājayaṃ 
  
      Satasahassito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi aggadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nadīkassapo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Nadīkassapatthepadānaṃ dutiyaṃ 
  
     Gayākassapattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Ajinacammavatthohaṃ  khāribhāradharo tadā 
 Khārikaṃ hārayitvāna kolaṃ ahāsimassamaṃ 
  
      Bhagavā tasmiṃ  samaye eko adutiyo jino 
 Mamassamaṃ upaṃgañji  jotento sabbakālikaṃ 
  
      Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā abhivādetvāna subbataṃ 
 Ubhohatthehi paggayha kolaṃ buddhassadāsahaṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi koladānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
   Abhinavatthaṃ nivatthohaṃ   sī 
   Tamhi   machasaṃ   Upāgacchi   machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gayākassapo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Gayākassapattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ 
  
     Kimbilattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nibbute kakusandhasmiṃ  brāhmaṇasmiṃ  vusīmati 
 Gahetvā salalaṃ mālaṃ maṇḍapaṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Tāvatiṃsaṃ gato santo labhimha vyamhamuttamaṃ 
 Aññe devetirocāmi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Divā vā yadi vā rattiṃ caṅkamanto ṭhito cahaṃ 
 Chatto salalapupphehi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Imasmiṃ yeva kappamhi yaṃ buddhambhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kimbilo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Kimbilattherāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ 
  
   Kimila   machasaṃ 
   Kakusandhamhi   machasaṃ 
   Brāhmaṇampi   machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Vajjiputtattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Sahassaraṃsī bhagavā sayambhu aparājito 
 Vivekā vuṭṭhahitvāna govarāyābhinikkhami 
  
      Phalahattho ahaṃ disvā upagañchiṃ  narāsahaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano savaṇṭaṃ adadiṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Catunavutito  kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vajjiputto thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Vajjiputtattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ 
  
     Uttarattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Sumedho nāma sambuddho battiṃsa  varalakkhaṇo 
 Vivekakāmo bhagavā himavanta mupāgami 
  
      Ajjhogahetvā himavantaṃ aggo kāruṇiko muni 
 Pallanaṅkaṃ ābhujitvāna nisīdi purisuttamo 
  
      Vijjādharo  tadā āsiṃ antalikkhacaro ahaṃ 
 Tisūlaṃ sugataṃ gayha gacchāmi ambare tadā 
  
      Pabbatagge yathā aggi puṇṇamāyeva candimā 
 Vanaṃ obhāsate buddho sālarājāva phullito 
  
      Vanaggā nikkhamitvāna buddharaṃsī vidhāvare   
 Naḷaggivaṇṇasaṅkāsā  disvā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ 
  
      Vicinaṃ addasaṃ pupphaṃ kaṇikāraṃ devagandhikaṃ 
 Tīṇi puppāni ādāya buddhaseṭṭhamapūjayiṃ 
  
   Upagacchiṃ   machasaṃ 
   Catunanavutito   machasaṃ 
   Bāttiṃsa   machasaṃ 
   Vijjadharo   machasaṃ 
   Abhidhāvare   machasaṃ 
   Naḷagagivanasaṅkāsaṃ   sīmu 
  
                   
  
      Buddhassa ānubhāvena tīṇi pupphāni me tadā 
 Uddhavaṇṭā  adhopattā chāyaṃ kubbanti satthuno 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Tattha me sukataṃ vyamhaṃ  kaṇikārīti  ñāyate  
 Saṭṭhiyejanamubbedhaṃ tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ 
  
      Sahassakaṇḍaṃ satabheṇḍu dhajālu haritāmayaṃ 
 Satasassaniyyuhā  vyamhe pāturahaṃsu  me 
  
      Sovaṇṇamā maṇimayā lohitaṅkamayāpi ca 
 Phalikāpi ca pallaṅkā yenicchakā yadicchakā 
  
      Mahārahañca sayanaṃ tulikāvikatīyutaṃ 
 Uddhalomiñca ekantaṃ bimbohanasamāyutaṃ 
  
      Bhavanā nikkhamitvāna caranto devacārikaṃ 
 Yadā icchāmi  gamanaṃ devasaṅghapurakkhato 
  
      Pupphassa heṭṭhā tiṭṭhāmi uparicchadanaṃ mama 
 Samantā yojanasataṃ kaṇikārehi chāditaṃ 
  
      Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni sāyaṃ pātaṃ upaṭṭhahuṃ 
 Parivārenti maṃ niccaṃ rattindivamatanditā 
  
      Tattha naccehi gītehi tāḷehi  vāditehi ca 
 Ramāmi khiḍḍāratiyā modāmi kāmakāmahaṃ 
  
      Tattha bhutvā pivitvā ca modāmi tidase pure 
 Nārigaṇehi sahito modāmi vyamhamuttame 
  
      Satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñca devarajjamakārayiṃ 
 Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñca cakkavatti ahosahaṃ 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
   Uddhaṃ vaṇṭā   machasaṃ 
   Byamhaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Kaṇikāroti   sī 
   Ñāyati   machasaṃ 
   Satasahassāni byuhāni   sī 
   Pātubhaviṃsu   machasaṃ 
   Yathā gacchāmi   sī 
 Yathā icchāmi   machasaṃ 
   Tālehi   machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Bhave bhave saṃsaratto mahābhogaṃ labhāmahaṃ 
 Bhoge me ūnatā natthi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Duve bhave saṃsarāmi  devatte atha mānuse 
 Aññaṃ gatiṃ na jānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Duve kule pajāyāmi khattiye cāpi brāhmaṇe 
 Nīce kule na jānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ sivikaṃ sandamānikaṃ 
 Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Dāsigaṇaṃ dāsagaṇaṃ nāriyo samalaṅkatā 
 Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Koseyya kambaliyāni khomakappāsikāni ca 
 Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Navavatthaṃ navaphalaṃ navaggarasabhojanaṃ 
 Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Imaṃ khāda imaṃ bhuñja imasmiṃ  sayane saya 
 Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sabbattha pūjito bhomi yaso accuggato mama 
 Mahāpakkho sadā homi abhejjapariso sadā 
  
      Sītaṃ uṇhaṃ na jānāmi parilābho na vijjati 
 Atho cetasikaṃ dukkhaṃ hadaye me na vijjati 
  
      Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo hutvāna saṃsarāmi bhavābhave 
 Vevaṇṇiyaṃ na jānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Devalokā cavitvāna sukkamūlena codito 
 Sāvatthiyaṃ pure jāto mahāsālesu aḍḍhake 
  
      Pañcakāmaguṇe hitvā pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
   Yattha pacchā pajāyāmi   sīmu 
   Imambhi   machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Upasampādayī  buddho guṇamaññāya cakkhumā 
 Taruṇo pūjanīyohaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Dibbacakkhu visuddha me samādhikusalo ahaṃ 
 Abhiññāpāramippatto buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā anuppatto iddhipādesu kovido 
 Dhammesu pāramippatto buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassamhi yaṃ buddhamhipujayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā uttaro thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Uttaratherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ 
  
     Aparauttarattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nibbute lokanāthamhi siddhate lokanāyake 
 Mama ñāti samānetvā dhātupūjaṃ akāsahaṃ 
  
      Catunavutito kappe yaṃ dhātumhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dhātupūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā apara uttāratthero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Aparassa uttarattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ 
  
   Upasampadayi   machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Bhaddajīttherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Ogayha yaṃ pokkharaṇiṃ nānākuñjarasevitaṃ 
 Uddharāmi bhisaṃ tattha ghāsahetu ahaṃ tadā 
  
      Bhagavā tamhiṃ  samaye padumuttarasavhayo 
 Rattambaradharo buddho gacchate anilañjase 
  
      Dhunanto paṃsukūlāni saddaṃ assohaṃ tadā 
 Uddhaṃ nijjhāyamānohaṃ addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Nattheva ṭhitako santo āyāciṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  Madhuṃbhisehi sahitaṃ khīraṃ sappiṃ mulālikaṃ 
 Patitaṇhātu  me buddho anukampāya cakkhumā   
  
      Tato kāruṇiko satthā orohitvā mahāyaso 
 Patigaṇhī  mama bhikkhuṃ anukampāya cakkhumā 
 Paṭiggahetvā sambuddho akā me anumodanaṃ 
  
       Sukhī hotu mahāpuñña gati tuyhaṃ samijjhatu 
 Iminā bhisadānena labhassu vipulaṃ sukhaṃ  
  
      Tato bhisaṃ gahetvāna āgañjiṃ  mama assamaṃ 
 Bhisaṃ rukkhe laggetvāna mama dānaṃ anussariṃ 
  
      Mahāvāto uṭṭhahitvā sañcālesi vanaṃ tadā 
 Ākāso abhinādittha asanī ca phalī tadā 
  
      Tato me asanīpāto matthake nipatī tadā 
 Sohaṃ nisinnako santo tattha kālakato  ahaṃ 
  
      Puññakammena saññutto tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ 
 Kalevaraṃ me patitaṃ devaloke ramāmahaṃ 
  
      Chaḷāsīti  sahassāni nāriyo samalaṅkatā 
 Sāyaṃ pātaṃ upaṭṭhāhanti bhisadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
   Tasmiṃ   sīmu 
   Paṭiggaṇhātu   machasaṃ 
   Paṭigagaṇhi   machasaṃ 
   Āgacchiṃ   machasaṃ 
   Kālaṅkato   machasaṃ   Chalasīti   machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Manussayonimāgantvā sukhito bhomahaṃ tadā 
 Bhoge  me unatā natthi bhisadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Anukampitako tena devadevena tādinā 
 Sabbāsavāparikkhiṇā  natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Satasahassito kappe yaṃ bhisaṃ adadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhisadānadassiṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhaddajitthero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Bhaddajittherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ 
  
     Sīvakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Esanāya carantassa vipassissa mahesino 
 Rittakaṃ pattaṃ disvāna kummasaṃ pūrayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Ekanavutito kappe yaṃ bhikkhamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kummāsassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhā pi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sīvakatthero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Sīvakattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ 
  
 Tasasuddānaṃ 
  
 Yaso nadīkassapo ca gayākimbilavajjino 
 Dve uttarā bhaddaji ca sīvako cāpi uttamo 
  
 Yavavaggo chapaññāsatimo 
  
 Therāpadānaṃ samattaṃ 
  
  Raṭṭhapāla   upavāna ttherānaṃ apadānāni  machasaṃ  potthake yasavaggantogadhāni dissante tathāpi apadānapāḷi paṭhamabhāge dutiya tatiyavaggesu tesaṃ āgatattā idha na dassitānīti daṭṭhabbaṃ

 Suttantapiṭake khuddaka nikāye 
 Apadānapāḷi 
 Tatiyo bhāgo 
 Therī apadāna pāḷi 
  
 Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammā sambuddhassa 
  
   Sumedhāvaggo 
     Sumedhāpadānaṃ 
  
   Bhagavati koṇāgamane saṅghārāmambhi navanivesamhi   
 Sakhiyo tisso janiyo vihāradānaṃ adāsimbha 
  
   Dasakkhattuṃ satakkhattuṃ dasasatakkhattuṃ satānaṃ ca satakkhattu   
 Devesu upapajjimha ko vādo mānusake bhave 
  
   Deve mahiddhikā ahumbha mānusakamhi ko vādo 
 Sattaratanassa mahesi   itthiratanaṃ ahaṃ āsiṃ   
  
   Idha   sañcitakusalā susamiddhakulappajā 
 Dhanañajāni ca khemā ca ahmapi ca tayo janā 
  
   Ārāmaṃ sukataṃ katvā sabbāvayavamaṇḍitaṃ 
 Buddhappamukhasaṅghassa niyyādetvā pamoditā   
  
   Yattha yatthupapajjāmi tassa kammassa vāhasā 
 Devesu aggataṃ pattā manussesu tatheva ca 
  
   Imasmiyeva kappambhi brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma gottena uppajji vadataṃ varo 
  
   Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa tadā āsi narissaro 
 Kāsirājā kikī nāma bārāṇasipuruttame 
  
   Nivesanambi   simu machasaṃ   Satāni ca satakkattuṃ   syā satakkhattuṃ satānaṃ        Sattaratanamahesi   machasaṃ   Bhaviṃ   machasaṃ       Tattha   syā   Sammoditā   machasaṃ 
  
                
   Tassāsuṃ satta dhitaro rājaññā sukhedhitā   
 Buddhadhupaṭṭhānaniratā   brahmacariyaṃ cariṃsu tā 
  
    Tāsaṃ sahāyikā hutvā silesu susamāhitā 
 Datvā dānāni sakkaccaṃ agāreva vataṃ   cariṃ 
  
    Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsupagā ahaṃ 
                   
    Tato cutā yāmamagaṃ   tatohaṃ tusitaṃ gatā 
 Tato ca nimmāṇaratiṃ vasavattipuraṃ tato 
  
    Yattha yatthupapajjāmi puññakamamasamohitā   
 Ttha tattheva rājunaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
  
    Tato cutā manussatte rājunaṃ cakkavattinaṃ 
 Maṇḍalinañca rājunaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
  
    Sampattimanubhotvāna devesu mānusesu ca 
 Sabbattha sukhitā hutvā nekajātisu saṃsariṃ 
  
    So bhetu ca so pahavo taṃ mulaṃ sā ca sāsane khatti   
 Taṃ paṭhamaṃ   samodhānaṃ taṃ dhammaratāya nibbānaṃ 
  
    Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
                   
    Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
    Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ sumedhā bhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sumedhātheriyāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
   Sukhe ṭhitā   syā   Budedhāpaṭṭhānaniratā   machasaṃ   Vattaṃ   syā   Yācasagagaṃ   syā   Puññakammasamāhitā   simu   Khamaṃ   machasaṃ   Paṭhamaṃ taṃ   machasaṃ   Mama buddhassa   machasaṃ   Catasso   machasaṃ  sabbatthevaṃ  
  
                
     Mekhalādāyikāpadānaṃ 
    Siddhatthassa bhagavāte thupaṃ kārāpikā   ahuṃ 
 Mekhalikā mayā dinnā navakammāya satthuno 
  
    Niṭṭhite ca mahāthupe mekhalaṃ punadāsahaṃ 
 Lokanāthassa munino pasannā sehi pāṇihi 
  
    Catunavute ito   kappe yaṃ mekhalamadaṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhājānāmi thupakārassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
    Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
                   
    Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
    Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ mekhalādāyikā bhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Mekhalādāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
     Maṇḍapadāyikāpadānaṃ 
    Koṇāgamanassa munino maṇḍapo kārito mayā 
 Dhuvaṃ ca civaramadaṃ   buddhassa lokabandhuno 
  
    Yaṃ yaṃ janapadaṃ yāmi nigame rājadhāniyo 
 Sabbattha pujitā homi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
    Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
    Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
    Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ maṇḍapadāyākā bhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Paṇḍapadāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ tatiṃ   
  
   Thupakāraṃpikā   machasaṃ simu thupakāramakāyahaṃ   syā   Catunavutito   machasaṃ   Evaṃ ticiraṃdāsiṃ   simu machasaṃ 
  
                
     Saṅkamanatthāpadānaṃ 
    Vipassissa   bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Rathiyaṃ paṭipannassa kārayantassa pāṇino 
  
    Gharato nikkhamitvāna avakakujjā nippajjahaṃ 
 Anukampako lokanātho sisante   akkami mama   
  
    Akkamitvāna sirasi   agamā lokanāyako 
 Tena cittappasādena tusitaṃ uppajjahaṃ   
  
    Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
                   
    Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
    Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ saṅkamamanatthā bhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Saṅkamanatthātheriyāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
     Naḷamālikāpadānaṃ 
    Candabhāgānaditire ahosiṃ kintari tadā 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ 
  
    Pasannacittā sumanā vedajātā katañajali 
 Naḷamālaṃ lahetvāna sayambhuṃ abhipujayiṃ 
  
    Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā kintaridehaṃ agacchiṃ tidasaṃ gatiṃ   
  
    Chattiṃsadevarājunaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
 Dasannaṃ cakakvattaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
 Saṃvejetvāna me cittaṃ   pababajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
   Koṇḍaññassa   syā       Sirasi         Tadā         Sirasmiṃsyā   Agamāsahaṃ   machasaṃ   Gaṇaṃ  X  syā       Saṃvedayitvā kusalaṃ   syā     saṃvejayitvā me cittaṃ   sīmu 
  
                 
    Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
    Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā nathidoni punabbhavo   
  
    Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
    Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
    Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ naḷamāḷikā bhikkhunī   imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Naḷamālikātheriyāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
     Ekapiṇḍapātadāyikāpadānaṃ 
    Nagare bandhumatiyā bandhumā nāma khattiyo 
 Tassa   rañño ahuṃ bhariyā ekajjhaṃ cārayāmahaṃ   
  
    Rahogatā nisīditvā evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā 
  Adāya gamaniyaṃ hi kusalaṃ natthi me kataṃ 
                   
    Mahābhitāpaṃ kaṭukaṃ gorarūpaṃ sudāruṇaṃ 
 Nirayaṃ nūna gacchāmi ettha me natthi saṃsayo  
  
    Rājānaṃ upasaṅkamma idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  Ekaṃ me samaṇaṃ dehi bhojayissāmi khattiya  
  
    Adāsi me mahārājā samaṇaṃ bhāvitinduyaṃ 
 Tassa pattaṃ gahetvāna paramantena purayiṃ   
  
    Purayitvā paramantaṃ gandhālepamakāsahaṃ 
 Sahassagaghanakeneva   vatthayugena   chādayiṃ 
  
   Theri   simu machasaṃ   Yassa   simu   Ekaccaṃ vādayāmahaṃ   syā   Tappayiṃ   syā       Jālena pidahitvāna   machasaṃ syā       Pitacolena   syā mahānelena         simu potthakesu ayaṃ gāthā na dissate 
  
                 
    Ārammaṇaṃ mama   etaṃ sarāmi yāvajīvitaṃ 
 Tattha cintaṃ pasādetvā tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
    Tiṃsānaṃ devarājunaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
 Manasā patthitaṃ mayhaṃ nibbattati yathicchitaṃ   
  
    Visānaṃ cakkavattinaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
 Ocitattāva   hutvāna saṃsarāmi bhavesvahaṃ 
  
    Sbababandhanamuttāhaṃ apetā me upādikā 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā   natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
    Ekanavute ito kappe   yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
    Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
    Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
    Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ ekapiṇḍapātadāyikā bhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ekapiṇḍapātadāyikāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     Kaṭacchubhikkhādāyikāpadānaṃ 
    Piṇḍacāraṃ carantassa tissa nāmassa satthuno 
 Kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ paggayha buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ 
                   
    Paṭiggahetvā sambuddho tisso lokagganāyako 
 Vithiyā saṇṭhito satthā akā me anumodanaṃ 
  
     Kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ datvāna tāvatiṃsaṃ gamissasi 
 Chattiṃsadevarājunaṃ mahesittaṃ karissasi 
  
    Paññāsa   cakkavattinaṃ mahesittaṃ karissasi 
 Manasā patthitaṃ sabbaṃ paṭilacchasi sabbadā 
  
    Sampattiṃ anubhotvāna pabbajissasikikañcanā  
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissasināsavā    
  
   Mamaṃ   machasaṃ   Yathicchakaṃ   syā yadicchakaṃ         Upacitattā  syā   Sabbāsavaparikkhiṇā   machasaṃ   Paññāsaṃ   machasaṃ   Pabbajissasakiñcanā   simu   Nibbāyissasanāsavā   simu 
  
                 
    Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho tisso logganāyako 
 Nabhaṃ abbhuggami dhīro   haṃsarājāva ambare 
  
    Sudinnaṃ me dānavaraṃ suyiṭṭhā yāgasampadā 
 Kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ datvāna pattāhaṃ acalaṃ padaṃ 
  
    Dve navute ito kappe   yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhikkhāpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
    Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
    Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
    Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ kaṭacchubhikkhādāyikā bhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
  Kaṭacchubhikkhādāyikā theriyāpadānaṃ sattaṃ   
  
     Sattuppalamālikāpadānaṃ 
    Nagare aruṇavatiyā aruṇavā   nāma khattiyo 
 Tassa rañño ahuṃ bhariyā cārikaṃ cārayāmahaṃ   
  
    Sattamālā   gahetvāna uppalā devagandhikā 
 Nisajjapāsādavare evaṃ cintesi tāvade 
  
     Kiṃ me imāhi mālāhi sirasāropitāhi me 
 Varaṃ me buddhaseṭṭhassa ñāṇambhi abhiropitaṃ  
                   
    Sambuddhaṃ patimānenti dvārāsanne nisidahaṃ 
  Yadā ehiti   sambuddho pujayissaṃ mahāmuniṃ  
  
    Kakudho vilasantova migarājāva kesarī 
 Bhikkhusaṅghena sahito āgacchi vithiyaṃ jino 
  
    Buddhassa raṃsiṃ disvāna haṭṭhā saṃviggamānasā 
 Dvāraṃ avāpuritvāna   buddhaseṭṭhaṃ apūjayiṃ 
  
   Viro   machasaṃ   Aruṇo   machasaṃ   Cāritaṃ vārayāmaha   machasaṃ   Sattamālaṃ   machasaṃ   Etiha         Apāpuṇitvā   syā 
  
                 
    Sattauppalapupphāni parikiṇṇāni   ambare 
 Chadaṃ   karontā buddhassa matthake dhārayanti te 
  
    Udaggacittā sumanā vedajātā katañajali 
 Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā tāvatiṃsaṃ agañachahaṃ 
  
    Mahānelassa chadanaṃ dhārenti mama muddhani 
 Dibbagandhaṃ pavāyāmi sattuppalānidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
    Kadāci niyamānāya ñātisaṅghena me tadā 
 Yāvatā parisā mayhaṃ mahānelaṃ dhariyati 
  
    Sattati devarājunaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
 Sabbattha issarā hutvā saṃsarāmi bhavābhave 
  
    Tesaṭṭhicakkavattinaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
 Sabbe maṃ anuvattanti   ādeyyavacanā ahaṃ 
  
    Uppalasseva me vaṇṇo gandho ceva pavāyati 
 Dubbaṇṇiyaṃ na jānāmi   buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
    Iddhipādesu kusalā bojjhaṅgabhāvanāratā 
 Abhiññāpāramippatatā buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
    Satipaṭṭhānakusalā samādhijjhānagocarā 
 Sammappadhānamanuyuttā buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
    Viriyaṃ me dhuradhorayhaṃ yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā   natthidāni punabbhavo 
                   
    Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā   
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphadānassidaṃ   phalaṃ 
    Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
    Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
    Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ sattupapalamālikā bhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sattuppalamālikātheripadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
   Sucitthiṇṇāni   syā pavitthiṇṇāni         Chadiṃ   machasaṃ   Agacchahaṃ  machasaṃ   Mamanuvattanti   machasaṃ   Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi   syā       Sabbāsavaparikkhiṇā   machasaṃ   Pupphamabhipūjayiṃ   machasaṃ   Budadhapujayidaṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                 
     Pañcadipikāpadānaṃ 
    Nagare haṃsavatiyā cāriki   āsahaṃ tadā 
 Ārāmena ca ārāmaṃ carāmi kusalatthikā 
  
    Kālapakkhambhi divase addasaṃ bodhimuttamaṃ 
 Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā bodhimule nisidahaṃ 
  
    Garucittaṃ upaṭṭhapetvā sire katvāna añjaliṃ 
 Somanassaṃ pavedetvā evaṃ cintesi tāvade 
  
     Yadi budedhā amitaguṇo asamappaṭipuggalo 
 Dassetu pāṭihiraṃ me bodhi obhāsatu ayaṃ  
  
    Saha āvajjanā   mayhaṃ bodhi pajjali tāvade 
 Sabbasoṇṇamāyo   āsi disā sabbā virocayaṃ   
  
    Sattarattindivaṃ tattha bodhimule nisidahaṃ 
 Sattame divase patte dipapujaṃ akāsahaṃ 
  
    Āsanaṃ parivāretvā pañcadipāni pajjaluṃ 
 Yāva udeti suriyo dipā me pajjaluṃ tadā 
  
    Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
    Tattha me sukataṃ vyambhaṃ pañcadipiti   vuccati 
 Saṭṭhiyojanamubbedhaṃ   tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ 
  
     Asaṅkhyāni dipāni parivāre jalanti me 
 Yāvatā devabhavanaṃ dipālokena jotati   
                   
     Parammukhā nisīditvā yadi icchāmi passituṃ 
 Uddhaṃ adho ca tiriyaṃ sabbaṃ passāmi cakkhunā 
  
     Yāvatā abhikaṅkhāmi daṭṭhuṃ sugataduggate 
 Tattha āvaraṇaṃ natthi rukkhesu pabbatesu va 
  
   Cārini   syā   Āvajjite   machasaṃ syā       Sbasovaṇṇamayā   simu   Virocayi   simu machasaṃ   Pañcadipāti   machasaṃ   Satayojanamubbedhaṃ   simu syā       Jotayi   simu 
  
                 
     Asiti devarājunaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
 Satānaṃ cakakvattinaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
  
     Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Dipasatasahassāni parivāretvā jalatti maṃ   
  
     Devalokā cavitvāna uppajjiṃ mātukucchiyaṃ 
 Mātukucchigataṃ sattiṃ   akkhi me na nimilati 
  
     Dipasatasahassāni puññakammasamaṅgitā 
 Sutighare pajjalanti   pañcadipinādaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Pacchime bhave   sampanne mānasaṃ vinivaṭṭayiṃ 
 Ajarāmaraṃ   sitibhāvaṃ nibbānaṃ phassayiṃ   ahaṃ 
  
     Jātiyā sattavassāhaṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
 Upasampādayi buddho guṇamaññāya gotamo 
  
     Maṇḍape rukkhamule vā pāsādesu guhāsu vā 
 Suññāgāre ca jhāyantyā   pañcadipā jalanti me 
  
     Dibbacakkhu visuddhaṃ me samādhikusalā ahaṃ 
 Abhiññāpāramippattā pañcadipānidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Sabbavositavosānā katakiccā anāsavā 
 Pañcadipā mahāvīra pāde vandati   cakkhuma 
  
     Satasahasse ito   kappe yaṃ dipamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pañcadipānidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
                   
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ pañcadipikā bhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pañcadipikātheriyāpadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
   Paravāre jalanati me   machasaṃ   Gatā santi   machasaṃ       Jalanati sutikāgehe   machasaṃ   Pacachimabhave   simu   Ajarāmataṃ   machasaṃ   Passayiṃ   syā   Jhāyaneta   simu jhāyanatā       vachanatiyā   machasaṃ   Vandāmi   machasaṃ       Satasahassito   machasaṃ 
  
                 
      Udakadāyikāpadānaṃ 
     Nagare banadhumatiyā ahosiṃ udahārikā 
 Udahārena jivāmi tena posemi dārake 
  
     Deyyadhammo ca me natthi puññakkhette anuttare 
 Koṭṭhakaṃ upasaṅkamma udakaṃ paṭṭhapesahaṃ 
  
     Tena kammena sukatena tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
 Tattha me sukataṃ vyambhaṃ udahārena nimmitaṃ 
  
     Accharānaṃ sahassassa   ahaṃ hi pavarā tadā 
 Dasaṭṭhānehi tā sabbā abhibhomi sadā ahaṃ 
  
     Paññāsaṃ devarājunaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
 Visaticakkavattinaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
  
     Duve bhāve saṃsarāmi devatte atha mānuse 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dakadānassidaṃ   phalaṃ 
  
     Pabbatagge dumagge vā antalikkhe ca bhumiyaṃ 
 Yadā udakamicchāmi khippaṃ paṭilabhāmahaṃ 
  
     Avuṭṭhikā disā natthi santattakuthitā na ca  
 Mama saṅkappamaññāya mahāmegho pavassati 
  
     Kadāci niyamānāya ñātisaṅghena me tadā 
 Yadā icchāmahaṃ vassaṃ mahāmegho pavassati  
  
     Uṇhaṃ vā pariḷāho vā sarire me na vijjati 
 Kāye ca me rajo natthi dakadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
                   
     Visuddhamanasā ajja apetamalapāpikā  
 Sababāsavā parikkhiṇā   natthidāni punabbhāvo 
  
   Sahassānaṃ   syā   Udakadānassidaṃ   simu   Satattā kuthitāpi ca   machasaṃ   Ajāyatha   machasaṃ   Apetamanapa pikā   machasaṃ       Sababāsavaparikkhiṇā   simu machasaṃ 
  
                 
     Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ   tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dākadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ udakadāyikā bhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Udakadāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Tassuddānaṃ 
 Sumedhā mekhalādāyi maṇḍapasaṅkamaṃ dadā 
 Naḷamāli piṇḍadadā kaṭacchu uppalappadā 
  
 Dipadā dakadā ceva gāthāyo gaṇitā iha 
 Ekaṃ gāthāsataṃ ceva tiṃsati ca taduttariṃ 
   Sumedhāvaggo paṭhamo   
  
   Yamudakamadadiṃ   simu 
  
                 
   Ekuposathika vaggo 
     Ekuposathikāpadānaṃ 
     Nagare bandhumatiyā bandhumā nāma khattiyo 
 Divase puṇṇamāyaṃ   so upavasi   uposathaṃ 
  
     Ahaṃ tena samayena kumbadāsi ahuṃ tahiṃ 
 Disvā sarājikaṃ   senaṃ evāhaṃ vintayiṃ tadā 
  
      Rājāpi rajjaṃ chaḍḍhetvā upavasi   uposathaṃ 
 Saphalaṃ nūna taṃ kammaṃ janakāyo pamodito  
                   
     Yoniso pacacavekkhitvā duggaccañca daḷiddataṃ  
 Mānasaṃ saṃpahaṃsetvā   upavasiṃ uposathaṃ 
  
     Ahaṃ uposathaṃ katvā sammāsambuddhasāsane 
 Tena kammena sukatena tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ   
  
     Tattha me sukataṃ vyambhaṃ uddhaṃ   yojanamuggataṃ 
 Kuṭāgāravarūpetaṃ sayanāsabhusitaṃ   
  
     Accharā satasahassā upatiṭṭhanti maṃ sadā 
 Aññe deve atikkamma atirocāmi sabbadā 
  
     Catusaṭṭhidevarājunaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
 Tesaṭṭhicakkavattinaṃ mahesintamakārayiṃ 
  
     Suvaṇṇavaṇṇā hutvāna bhavesu saṃsarāmahaṃ 
 Sabbattha pavarā bhomi uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ rathayānañca sivikaṃ    
 Labhāmi sabbametampi uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
   Puṇamāya   machasaṃ   Upapajji   syā       Sarājakaṃ   machasaṃ   Duggatiñca   siyā   Dalidadataṃ   machasaṃ   Saṃpahaṃsitvā   machasaṃ   Tāvatiṃsamagacachahaṃ   machasaṃ   Udadha   machasaṃ   Mahāsanasubhusitaṃ   machasaṃ mahāsayana bhusitaṃ          Kevalaṃ   sīmu syā     
  
                 
     Sovaṇṇamayaṃ rūpimayaṃ athopi phalikāmayaṃ 
 Lohitaṅkamayañceva sabbaṃ paṭilabhāmahaṃ 
  
     Koseyyakambaliyāni khomakappāsikāni ca 
 Mahagghāni ca vatthāni sabbaṃ paṭilabhāmahaṃ 
  
     Annaṃ pānaṃ khādaniyaṃ vatthasenāsanāni ca 
 Sabbametaṃ paṭilabhe uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Varagandhañca mālañca cuṇṇakañca vilepanaṃ 
 Sabbametaṃ paṭilabhe uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Kūṭāgārañca pāsādaṃ maṇḍapaṃ hammiyaṃ guhaṃ 
 Sabbametaṃ paṭilabhe uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Aḍḍhamāse asampatte arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ   
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
                   
     Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ 
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ ekuposathikā bhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ekuposathikātheriyāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
   Arahattamapāpuṇiṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                 
     Salalapupphikāpadānaṃ 
     Candabhāgānaditire ahosiṃ kittari tadā addasāhaṃ devadevaṃ caṅkamantaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
  
     Ocinitvāna salalaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ 
  Upasiṅgha mahāvīra   salalaṃ devagandhikaṃ  
  
     Paṭiggahetvā sambuddho vipassī lokanāyako 
 Upasiṅghi mahāvīro pekkhamānāya me tadā 
  
     Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna vanditvā dipaduttamaṃ  
 Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā tato pabbatamārūhiṃ 
  
     Ekanavute ito   kappe yaṃ pupphamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ salalapupphikābhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Salalapupphikā theriyāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
     Modakadāyikāpadānaṃ 
     Nagare bandhumatiyā kumbhadāsi ahosahaṃ 
 Mama bhāgaṃ gahetvāna gacchiṃ udakahārikā   
  
     Santhamhi samaṇaṃ disvā santacittaṃ samahitaṃ 
 Pasannacittā sumanā modake tīṇidāsahaṃ 
                   
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Ekanavuti   kappāni vinipātaṃ na gacchahaṃ 
  
   Addasaṃ         Upasiṅghi mahāvīro   machasaṃ       Padaviduttamaṃ   machasaṃ   Ekanavutito   machasaṃ   Gacchaṃ udakahārikaṃ   simu udakahārake   syā   Ekunatiṃsa   syā 
  
                 
     Sampattiṃ   taṃ karitvāna sabbaṃ anubhavāmahaṃ  
 Modake tīṇi datvāna pattāhaṃ acalaṃ padaṃ 
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ modakadāyikā bhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Modakadāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     Ekāsanadāyikāpadānaṃ 
     Nagare haṃsavatiyā ahosiṃ bālikā   tadā 
 Mātā ca me pitā ceva kammantaṃ agamaṃsu te 
  
     Majjhantikambhi suriye addasaṃ samaṇaṃ ahaṃ 
 Vithiyaṃ   anugacchantaṃ āsanaṃ paññapesahaṃ 
  
     Goṇakacittakādihi   paññapetvāhamāsanaṃ  
 Pasannacitatā sumanā idaṃ vacanamabuviṃ 
  
      Santattā kuthitā bhumi suro majjhantike ṭhito 
 Mālutā ca na vāyanti kālo cettha upaṭṭhitā   
  
      Paññattamāsanamidaṃ tavatthāya mahāmuni 
 Anukampamupādayā nisida mama āsane  
  
     Nisīdi tattha samaṇo sudanto suddhamānaso 
 Tassa pattaṃ gahetvāna yathārandhamadāsahaṃ 
  
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
     Tattha me sukataṃ vyambhaṃ āsanena sunimmitaṃ 
 Saṭṭhiyojanamubbedhaṃ tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ 
  
   Sampatti   machasaṃ sampatiñca   syā   Anubhaviṃ ahaṃ   machasaṃ   Mālikā  syā       Vithiyā   machasaṃ   Goṇakavikatikāhi   machasaṃ       Mamāsanaṃ   machasaṃ mahāsanaṃ         Cevetthamehiti   machasaṃ cevetthameti       
  
                 
                   
     Soṇṇamayā maṇimayā athopi phalikāmayā 
 Lohitaṅkamayā ceva pallaṅkā vividhā mama 
  
     Tulikāvikatikāhi kaṭṭhissacittakāhi ca 
 Uddaekantalomihi   pallaṅkā me susatthatā   
  
     Yadā icchāmi gamanaṃ hāsakhiḍḍā samappitaṃ  
 Saha pallaṅkaseṭṭhena gacchāmi mama patthitaṃ 
  
     Asitidevarājunaṃ mahesinnamakārayiṃ 
 Sattaticakkavattinaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
  
     Bhavābhave saṃsaranti mahābhogaṃ labhāmahaṃ 
 Bhoge me ūnatā natthi ekāsanaphalaṃ Idaṃ   
  
     Duve bhave saṃsarāmi devatte atha mānuse 
 Aññe bhave na jānāmi ekāsanaphalaṃ idaṃ 
  
     Duve kule pajāyāmi khattiye cāpi brāhmaṇo 
 Uccākulinā   sabbattha ekāsanaphalaṃ idaṃ 
  
     Domanassaṃ na jānāmi cittasantāpanaṃ mama 
 Vevaṇṇiyaṃ na jānāmi ekāsanaphalaṃ idaṃ 
  
     Dhātiyo maṃ upaṭṭhanti khujjā kheḷāsākā   bahu 
 Aṅkena aṅkaṃ gacchāmi ekāsanaphalaṃ idaṃ 
  
     Aññā nahāpenti bhojenti aññā ramenti maṃ sadā 
 Aññā gandaṃ vilimpenti   ekāsanaphalaṃ idaṃ 
  
     Maṇḍape rukkhamule vā suññāgāre vasantiyā 
 Mama saṅkappamaññāya pallaṅko upatiṭṭhati 
  
     Ayaṃ pacchimako mayhaṃ carimo vattate bhavo 
 Ajjāpi rajjaṃ chaḍḍetvā pabbajaṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
     Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ekāsanaphalaṃ idalaṃ 
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ ekāsanadāyikā bhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ekāsanadāyikā theriyāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
   Udadaekanatalomi ca   machasaṃ   Susaṇṭhikā   machasaṃ syā   Hāsakhiḍaḍhasamapapitā   machasaṃ   Ekāsanasasidaṃ phalaṃ   machasaṃ   Kulikā   syā       Velāpikā   machasaṃ celāyikā syā celāvikā         Vilimpanati   machasaṃ 
  
                 
                   
     Pañcadīpadāyikāpadānaṃ 
     Nagare haṃsavatiyā cārikā   āsahaṃ tadā 
 Ārāmena ca ārāmaṃ   carāmi kusalathiko 
  
     Kālapakkhambhi divase addasaṃ bodhimuttamaṃ 
 Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā bodhimule nisidahaṃ 
  
     Garucittaṃ upaṭṭhapetvā sire katvāna añjaliṃ 
 Somanassaṃ pavedetvā evaṃ cintesiṃ tāvade 
  
      Yadi buddho amitayaso asamappaṭipuggalo 
 Dassetu pāṭihiraṃ me bodhi obhāsatu ayaṃ  
  
     Saha āvajjanā mayhaṃ bodhi pajjali tāvade 
 Sabbasoṇṇamayā asi disā sabbā rocayi  
  
     Sattarattindivaṃ tattha bodhimule nisidahaṃ 
 Sattame divase patte dipapujaṃ akāsahaṃ 
  
     Āsanaṃ parivaretvā pañcadipāni pajjaluṃ   
 Yāva udeti suriye dipā me pajjaluṃ tadā 
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
     Tattha me sukataṃ vyambhaṃ pañcadipiti   vuccati 
 Saṭṭhiyojanamubbedhaṃ tiṃsayojana vitthataṃ 
  
     Asaṅkhiyāni dipāni parivāre   jalanti me 
 Yāvatā devabhavanaṃ dipālokena jotati 
  
     Parammukhā   nisīditvā yadi icchāmi passituṃ 
 Uddhaṃ adho ca tiriyaṃ sabbaṃ passāmi cakkhunā 
  
     Yāvatā abhikaṅkhāmi daṭṭhuṃ sugataduggate   
 Tattha āvaraṇaṃ natthi rukkhesu pabbatesu vā 
  
     Asita devarānaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
 Satānaṃ cakkavattinaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
  
   Cāriki   machasaṃ   Ārāmena vihārena   syā       Virocati   syā       Pajjaliṃ   simu   Pañcadipāti   machasaṃ syā   Parivāretvā  theri   Pubbamukhā syā       Sukatadukkate   syā     theri 
                   
                 
     Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānuse 
 Dipasatasahassāni parivāre   jalatti me   
  
     Devalokā cavitvāna uppajjiṃ mātukucchiyaṃ 
 Mātukucchigataṃ sattiṃ   akkhi me na nimilati 
  
     Dipasatasahassāni puññakammasamaṅgitā 
 Jalanti sutikāgehe pañcadipinādaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Pacchime bhave sampanne mānasaṃ vinivaṭṭayiṃ  
 Ajarāmaraṃ sitibhūtaṃ   nibbānaṃ phassayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Jātiyā sattavassāhaṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
 Upasampādayi buddho guṇamaññāya gotamo 
  
     Maṇḍape rukkhamule vā suññāgāre vasantiyā 
 Sadā pajjalate dīpaṃ pañcadipānidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Dibbacakkhu visuddhaṃ me samādhikusalā ahaṃ 
 Abhiññāpāramippattā pañcadipānidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Sabbavositavosānā katakiccā anāsavā 
 Pañcadipā mahāvīra pāde vandati cakkhuma 
  
     Satasahasse ito   kappe yaṃ dipamadadiṃ tadā   
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pañcadipānidaṃ phalaṃ 
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ pañcadipayikā bhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pañcadipayikātheriyāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
   Parivāretvā   simu   Maṃ   simu   Mātukucchigataṃ sanatiṃ   simu   Vinivattayiṃ   machasaṃ   Ajarāmataṃ sitibhāvaṃ   machasaṃ   Satasahasasato   machasaṃ   Yaṃ dipamabhipujayiṃ   simu 
  
                 
     Sālamālikāpadānaṃ 
     Candābhāgānaditire ahosiṃ kintari tadā 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ 
                   
     Pasannacittā sumanā vedajātā katañajali 
 Sālamālaṃ gahetvāna sayambhuṃ abhipujayiṃ 
  
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā kinnaridehaṃ   tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
     Chattiṃsa devarājunaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
 Manasā patthitaṃ mayhaṃ nibbattati yathicchitaṃ 
  
     Dasannaṃ cakakvattinaṃ mahesintamakārayiṃ 
 Ocitattāva   hutvāna saṃsarāmi bhavesvahaṃ 
  
     Kusalaṃ vijjate mayhaṃ pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Pujārahā ahaṃ ajja   sakyaputtassa sāsane 
  
     Visuddhamanasā ajja apetamanapāpikā 
 Sabbāsavāparikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
     Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ buddhamabhipujayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi sālamālāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ sālamālikā bhikkhunī imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sālamālikātheriyāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     Mahāpāpatigotamiapadānaṃ 
     Ekadā lokapajjoto vesāliyaṃ mahāvane 
 Kūṭāgāre susālāyaṃ vasate narasārathi 
  
   Mānāsaṃ dehaṃ   simu   Sucittatāva         Ahamajaja   sīmu 
  
                 
     Tadā jinassa mātucchā mahāgotami bhikkhunī 
 Tahiṃ kate   pure ramme vasi bhikkhunupassaye 
  
     Bhikkhunīhi vimuttāhi satehi saha pañcahi 
 Rahogatāya tassevaṃ cittassāsi   vitakkitaṃ 
  
      Buddhassa parinibbāṇaṃ sāvakaggayugassa vā 
 Rāhulānandanandānaṃ nāhaṃ lacchāmi passituṃ  
                   
     Paṭigaccāyusaṅkhāre   ossajitvāna nibbutiṃ 
 Gaccheyyaṃ lokanāthena anuññātā mahesinā  
  
     Tathā pañcasatānampi bhikkhunīnaṃ vitakkitaṃ 
 Āsi khemādikānampi etadeva vitakkitaṃ 
  
     Bhūmicālo tadā āsi nāditā devadundubhi 
 Upassayādhivatthayo devatā sokapiḷitā 
 Vipalannā sakaruṇaṃ   tathessuni pavattayuṃ 
  
     Mittā   bhikkhunīyo tā hi upagantvāna gotamiṃ 
 Nipacca sirasā pade idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
      Tattha toyalavāsittā mayamayye rahogatā 
 Sācalā calitā bhumi naditā devadundubhi 
 Paridevā ca suyanti kimatthaṃ nūna gotami  
  
     Tadā avoca sā sabbaṃ yathāparivitakkitaṃ 
 Tāyopi sabbā āhaṃsu yathāparivitakkati Ṃ 
  
      Yadi te rucitaṃ ayye nibbāṇaṃ paramaṃ sivaṃ 
 Nibbāyissāma sabbāpi buddānuññāya subabate 
  
     Mayaṃ sahāva nikkhantā gharāpi va bhavāpi ca 
 Sahayeva gamissāma nibbāṇapuramuttamaṃ  
  
     Nibbānāya vajantinaṃ kiṃ vakkhāmiti  sā vadaṃ 
 Saha sabbāhi niggacchi bhikkhunīnilayā tadā 
  
   Tahiṃ yeva   syā   Citatasasāpi   machasaṃ   Paṭikacacāyusaṅkhāraṃ   machasaṃ   Visajajitvāna   machasaṃ   Sukaruṇaṃ   machasaṃ   Sababā   syā     
   Imisasā gāthāyānanajaraṃ  simu machasaṃ potthakesu  buddhassa parinibbāṇā sābakaggayugasasa ca mahākassapanandānaṃ ānandarāhulāna ca  ayampi gāthā dissate na syāma potthakesu 
  
                 
     Upassaye yādhivatthā devatā tā khamantu me 
 Bhikkhunīnilayassedaṃ pacchimaṃ dassanaṃ mama 
  
     Na jarā maccu vā yattha appiyehi samāgamo 
 Piyehi vippayogonatthi   taṃ vajissaṃ   asaṅkataṃ 
  
     Acitarāgā taṃ sutvā vacanaṃ sugatorasā 
 Sokaṭṭā parideviṃsu  aho no appapuññatā 
                   
     Bhikkhunīnilayo suñño bhūto tāhi vinā ayaṃ 
 Pabhāte viya tārāyo na dissanti jinorasā 
  
     Nibbānaṃ gotami yāti satehi saha pañcahi 
 Nadisatehiva saha gaṅgā pañcahi sāgaraṃ 
  
     Rathikāya vajantiṃ taṃ   disvā saddhā upāsikā 
 Gharā nikkhamma pādesu nipacca idamabraviṃ 
  
      Pasidassu mahābhoge anāthāyo vihāya no 
 Tayā na yutataṃ   nibbātuṃ  iccaṭṭaṃ   vilapiṃsu tā 
  
     Tāsaṃ sokapahāṇatthaṃ avoca madhuraṃ giraṃ 
  Ruditena alaṃ puttā hāsakāloyamajja vo 
  
     Pariññātaṃ mayā dukkhaṃ dukakhahetu vivajjito 
 Nirodho me sacchikato maggo cāpi subhāvito 
  Bhāṇavāraṃ paṭhamaṃ  
  
     Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
 Ohito garuko bhāro bhavanetti samuhatā 
  
     Yassatthāya pabbajitā agārasmānagāriyaṃ 
 So me attho anuppatto sabbasaññojanakkhayo 
  
     Buddho tassa ca saddhammo anuno yāva tiṭṭhati nibbātuṃ tāva kālo me mā maṃ socatha puttikā 
  
   Piyehi na viyogopi   machasaṃ   Vajajisaṃ   syā   Vajanatiyā   machasaṃ vapanatinaṃ         Yutakā   machasaṃ   Icchaṭaṭā   machasaṃ syā iccaṭṭā      
  
                 
     Koṇḍaññānandinandādī tiṭṭhanati rāhulo jino 
 Sukhito sahito saṅgho hatadappā ca titthiyā 
  
     Okkākavaṃsassa yaso usasito māramaddano 
 Nanu sampati kālo me nibbānatthāya puttikā 
  
     Cirappabhūti yaṃ mayhaṃ patthitaṃ ajja sijjhate 
 Ānandabherikāloyaṃ kiṃ vo assuhi puttikā 
  
     Save mayi dayā atthi yadi catthi kataññutā 
 Saddammaṭṭhitiyā sabbā kirotha viriyaṃ daḷhaṃ 
  
     Thinaṃ adāsi pabbajjaṃ sambuddho yācito mayā 
 Tasmā yathāhaṃ nandissaṃ tathā tamanutiṭṭhatha 
  
     Tā evamanusāsitvā bhikkhunīhi purakkhatā 
 Upecca buddhaṃ vanditvā idaṃ vacanamabravi 
                   
      Ahaṃ sugata mātā te   tvaṃ ca vīra pitā mama 
 Saddhammasukhado   nātha tayā jātambhi   gotama 
  
     Saṃvaḍḍhitoyaṃ   sugata rūpakāyo mayā tava 
 Anindiyo   dhammakāyo   mama saṃvaḍḍhito   tayā 
  
     Muhutata  taṇhāsamanaṃ khiraṃ tvaṃ pāyito mayā 
 Tayāhaṃ santamaccantaṃ dhammakhiraṃ hi   pāyitā 
  
     Vaddhanarakkhane   mayhaṃ anaṇo    tvaṃ mahāmune 
 Puttakāmā thiyo yā tā    labhantu    tādisaṃ sutaṃ 
  
     Mandhātādinarindānaṃ yā mātā sā bhavaṇṇave 
 Nimuggāhaṃ tayā putta tāritā bhavasāgarā 
  
     Rañño mātā mahesiti sulabhaṃ nāmamitthinaṃ 
 Buddamātāti yaṃ nāmaṃ etaṃ paramadullabhaṃ 
  
     Tañca laddhaṃ mayā vīra paṇidhānaṃ mamaṃ tayā 
 Anukaṃ vā mahantaṃ vā taṃ sabbaṃ puritaṃ mayā 
  
   Temātā   sabbesu   Saddhammasukhada   machasaṃ   Jātāmhi   machasaṃ   Saṃvadadhitoyaṃ   machasaṃ   Anindito   machasaṃ ānandiyo   syā   Dhamamatanu   simu       Muhuttaṃ   machasaṃ   Dhamamakhiramapi   syā   Banadhanārakkhate   machasaṃ    Aṇaṇo   machasaṃ    Yācaṃ   machasaṃ    Labhanti   machasaṃ syā theri 
  
                 
     Parinibbātumicchāmi vihāyemaṃ kalebaraṃ  
 Anujānāhi me vīra dukkhantakara nāyaka 
  
     Cakkaṅkusadhajākiṇṇe pade kamalakomale 
 Pasārehi paṇāmaṃ te karissaṃ puttapemasā   
  
     Suvaṇṇarāsisaṃkāsaṃ sariraṃ kuru pākaṭaṃ 
 Katvā dehaṃ sudiṭṭhaṃ te santiṃ gacchāmi nāyaka  
  
     Dvattiṃsalakkhaṇupetaṃ suppabhālaṅkataṃ tanuṃ 
 Sañajhāghanāva bāla kkaṃ mātucchaṃ dassayi jino 
  
     Phullāravindasaṅkāse taruṇādiccasappabhe 
 Cakkaṅkite pādatale tato sā sirasā pati 
      Paṇamāmi narādiccaṃ ādiccakulaketukaṃ 
 Pacchime maraṇe   mayhaṃ na taṃ ikkhāmahaṃ puno 
                   
     Itthiyo nāma lokagga sabbadosakarā matā 
 Yadi ko natthi doso me khamassu karuṇākara 
  
     Itthikanāñca pabbajjaṃ yamahaṃ   yāciṃ punappunaṃ 
 Tattha ce atthi doso me taṃ khamassu narāsabha  
  
     Mayā bhikkhunīyo vīra tavānuññāya sāsitā 
 Tatu ce atthi dunatitaṃ taṃ khamassu khamādhipa   
  
      Akkhante nāma khantabbaṃ kiṃ bhave guṇabhusane 
 Kimuttaraṃ te vadakkhāmi nibbānāya vajantiyā 
  
     Suddhe anune mama bhikkhusaṅghe 
 Lokā ito nisasarituṃ kamante  
 Pabhātakāle vyasanaṃ gahānaṃ  
 Disvāna niyyāti ca candalekhā 
  
     Tadetarā bhikkhunīyo jinaggaṃ 
 Tārāva candānugatā sumeruṃ ṭhitā mukhantaṃ samudikkhamānā 
  
   Kalevaraṃ   machasaṃ   Putata utatame   machasaṃ putata pemahaṃ   syā   Saraṇaṃ   syā   Yaṃ taṃ   machasaṃ   Khamāmiti   syā   Khamaneta   machasaṃ   Gatānaṃ   machasaṃ   Kacca   machasaṃ 
  
                 
      Na tittapubaṃ   tava dassanena 
 Cakkhuṃ na sotaṃ tava bhāsitena 
 Cinnaṃ mamaṃ kevalamekameca 
 Pappuyya taṃ dhammarasena tittiṃ 
  
     Nadatoparisāyaṃ te vādidappāpahārino  
 Ye te dakkhanti vadanaṃ dhaññā te narapuṅgava 
  
     Dighaṅguli tambanakhe subhe āyatapaṇahike 
 Ye pāde paṇamisasnati   tepi dhaññā guṇandhara 
                   
     Madhurāni pahaṭṭhāni dosagghāni hitāni ca 
 Ye te vākyāni sossanti   tepi dhaññā naruttama 
  
     Dhaññāhaṃ te mahāvīra pādapujanatapparā 
 Tiṇṇasaṃsārakantārā suvākyena sirimato    
  
     Tato sā anusāsetvā bhikkhusaṅghampi subbatā 
 Rāhulānandanande ca vanditvā idamabravi 
  
      Āsivisālayasame rogāvāse kalebare 
 Nibbinnā dukkhasaṃghāte   jarāmaraṇagecare 
  
     Nānākalimalākiṇṇe   parāyatte nirihake 
 Tena nibbātumicchāmi anumaññatha puttakā  
  
     Nando rāhulabhaddo ca vitasokā nirāsavā 
 Ṭhitācalaṭṭhitithirā   dhammataṃ anucintayuṃ 
  
     Dhiratthu saṅkhataṃ lolaṃ asāraṃ kadalumapamaṃ 
 Māmarivisadisaṃ ittaraṃ anavaṭṭhitaṃ 
  
     Yattha nāma jinassāyaṃ mātucchā buddhaposikā 
 Gotami nidhanaṃ yāti aniccaṃ sabbasaṅkhataṃ  
  
   Titatipubbaṃ   machasaṃ   Vāditabbapahārino   machasaṃ   Paṇamāyanati   syā   Suyyanati   machasaṃ   Sadadhammena sirimatā         Dukkhasaṅsāṭe   machasaṃ dukkhasaṅkete   syā   Kalalamākiṇṇe       kuṇapamalākiṇṇe   syā   Ṭhitācalā dhītā dhirā   syā     
  
                 
     Ānando ca tadā sekho sokaṭṭo jinavacchalo 
 Tatthassuti dharanto so karunaṃ paridevati 
  
      Hā santiṃ   gotami yāti nūna buddhopi nibbutiṃ 
 Gacchati na cireneva aggiriva nirindhano  
  
     Evaṃ vilapamānaṃ taṃ anandaṃ āha gotami 
  Sunisāgara gambhira buddhupaṭṭhānatappara 
  
     Na yuttaṃ socituṃ putta hāsakāle upaṭṭhite 
 Tava   me saraṇaṃ putta nibbānaṃ samupāgataṃ   
  
     Tayā tāta samajjhiṭṭho pabbajjaṃ anuni no 
 Mā putta vimano hohi saphalo te parissamo 
                   
     Yaṃ na diṭṭhaṃ purāṇehi titthikācariyehi pi 
 Taṃ padaṃ sukumārihi sattavassāhi veditaṃ 
  
     Buddhasāsanapāletā pacchimaṃ dassanaṃ tava 
 Tattha gacchāmahaṃ putta gato yattha na dissate  
  
     Kadāci dhammaṃ desento khipi lokagganāyako tadāhaṃ āsiṃsavacaṃ   avocaṃ anukampikā 
      Ciraṃ jiva mahāvīra kappaṃ tiṭṭha mahāmune 
 Sabbalokassa atthāya bhavassu ajarāmaro  
  
     Taṃ tathāvādinaṃ buddho mamaṃ so etadabravi 
  Na hevaṃ vandiyā buddhā yathā vandasi gotami  
  
      Kathaṃ carahi sabbaññu vanditabbā tathāgatā 
 Kathaṃ avandiyā buddhā taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito  
  
      Āraddhaviriye pahitatte niccaṃ daḷhaparakkame 
 Samagge sāvake passe   phasā buddhānavandanā   
  
   Bhāsanti   syā   Tayā   machasaṃ       Nibabāṇanatamupāgataṃ   simu   Āsiṃsavācaṃ   machasaṃ   Pasasa   machasaṃ syā       Etaṃ buddānavandanaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
                 
     Tato upassayaṃ gantvā ekikāhaṃ vicintayiṃ 
 Samaggaṃ parisaṃ nātho rocati   tihavantago 
  
     Handāhaṃ parinibbissaṃ mā vipattiṃ tamaddasaṃ   
 Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna disvāna isisattamaṃ 
  
     Parinibbānakālaṃ me   ārocesiṃ vināyakaṃ 
 Tato so samanuññāsi  kālaṃ jānāhi gotami  
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
     Thinaṃ dhammābhisamaye ye bālā vimatiṃ gātā 
 Tesaṃ diṭṭhipahānatthaṃ iddhiṃ dassehi gotami 
  
     Tadā nipacca sambuddaṃ upapatitvāna ambaraṃ 
 Iddhi anekā dassesi buddhānuñāya gotami 
  
     Ekikā bahudhā āsi bahukā cekikā tathā 
 Āvibhāvaṃ tirobhāvaṃ tirokuḍḍaṃ tironagaṃ 
                   
     Asajjamānā agamā bhumiyampi nimujjatha 
 Abhijjamāne udake agañchi mabhiyā yathā 
  
     Sakuṇiva yathākase pallaṅkena gami tadā 
 Vasaṃ vattesi kayena yāva brahmanivesanaṃ 
  
     Sineruṃ daṇḍaṃ katvāna chattaṃ katvā mahāmahiṃ 
 Samulaṃ parivattetvā dhārenti   caṅkami nabhe 
  
     Chassurodayakāleva lokañcākāsi dhumikaṃ 
 Yugante viya lokaṃ sā jālāmālākulaṃ akā 
  
   Rodhesi   machasaṃ   Vipatatitamadadasaṃ   machasaṃ   Maṃ   syā   Dhārayaṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                 
     Mucalindaṃ mahāpesalaṃ meru mandāra daddare   
 Sāsaperiva sabbāni ekenaggahi muṭṭhitā 
  
     Aṅgulaggena chādesi hākaraṃ sanisākaraṃ 
 Candasurasahasasāni āvelamiva dhārayi 
  
     Catusāgaratoyāni dhārayi ekapāṇinā 
 Yugantajaladākāraṃ mahāvassaṃ pavasayi   
  
     Cakkavattiṃ saparisaṃ māpayī sā nabhatthale 
 Garuḷaṃ dviradaṃ sihaṃ vinadantaṃ ca dassayī 
  
     Ekikā abhinimmitvāppameyyaṃ bhikkhunīgaṇaṃ 
 Puna annaradhāpetvā ekikā munimabravi 
  
      Mātucchā te mahāvīra tavasāsanakārikā 
 Anuppattā sakaṃ atthā pade vandati   cakkhuma  
  
     Dassetvā vividhā iddhī orohitvā nabhatthalā 
 Vanditvā lokapajjotaṃ ekamantaṃ nisīdi sā 
  
      Sā visaṃvassasatikā   jātiyāhaṃ mahāmune alamettāvatā vīra nibbāyisasāmi nāyaka  
  
     Tadātivimbhitā sabbā parisā sā katañajali 
 Avocayye kathaṃ āsi atuliddhiparakkamā 
                   
     Padumuttaro nāma jito sabbadhammesu cakkhumā 
 Ito satasahassambhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
  
     Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ jātāmaccakule ahuṃ 
 Sabbupakārasampanne iddhe phīte mahaddhane 
  
     Kadāci pitunā saddhiṃ dāsigaṇapurakkhatā 
 Mahatā parivārena taṃ upecca narāsabhaṃ 
  
   Merumulanadaṅkare   machasaṃ meruṃ mandāradanatare   syā   Pavassatha   machasaṃ   Vandāmi   machasaṃ syā       Visavassasatikā   machasaṃ 
  
                 
     Vasavaṃ viya vassentaṃ   dhammameghaṃ anāsavaṃ 
 Saradādiccasadisaṃ raṃsimālākulaṃ jinaṃ  
     Disvā cittaṃ pasādetvā sutvā cassa subhāsitaṃ 
 Mātucchaṃ bhikkhunīṃ agge ṭhapentaṃ naranāyakaṃ 
  
     Sutvā datvā mahādānaṃ sattāhaṃ tassa tādino 
 Sasaṅghassa naraggassa pavacayāni bahuni ca 
  
     Nipajja pādamulambhi taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃ 
 Tato mahāparisati avoca isisattamo 
  
      Yā sasaṅghaṃ abhejesi sattāhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Tamahaṃ nittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
     Satasahasse ito   kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena   satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Tassa dhammesu dāyadā orasā dhammanimmitā 
 Gotami nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvikā 
  
     Tassa buddhassa mātucchā jīvitāpādikā   ayaṃ 
 Rattaññunañca aggantaṃ bhikkhunīnaṃ labhissati  
  
     Taṃ sutvāna   pamuditā   yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ 
 Pavacayehi upaṭṭhitvā tato kālakatā ahaṃ 
  
     Tāvatiṃsesu dovesu sabbakāmasamiddhisu 
 Nibbatatā dasahaṅgehi aññe abhibhaviṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Rūpasaddehi gandhehi rasehi phusanehi ca 
 Āyunāpi ca vaṇṇena sukhena yasasāpi ca 
  
     Tathevādhipateyyena adhigayha virocahaṃ 
 Ahosiṃ amarindassa mahesi dayitā tahiṃ 
                   
     Saṃsāre saṃsarantihaṃ kammavāyusameritā 
 Kāsissa rañño visaye ajāyiṃ dāsagāmake 
  
     Pañcadāsasatānunā nivasanti tahiṃ tadā 
 Pabbesaṃ tattha yo jeṭṭho tassā jāyā abhosahaṃ 
  
   Vassantaṃ   machasaṃ   Raṃsijālasamujajalaṃ   machasaṃ syā raṃsijālakulaṃ jinaṃ         Satasahassito   machasaṃ   Nāthena   simu   Jivitepālikā   syā   Sutvāhaṃ   sīmu syā       Pamoditvā   machasaṃ 
                 
     Sayambhuno pañcasatā gāmaṃ piṇḍāya pāvisuṃ 
 Te disvāna ahaṃ tuṭṭhā saha sabbehi ñātihi   
  
     Katvā pañcasatakuṭi   catumāse upaṭṭhiya  
 Ticivarāni datvāna pasananāmbha   sasāmikā 
     Tato cutā sapatikā   tāvatiṃsagatā mayaṃ 
 Pacchime ca bhavedāni jātā devadahe pure 
  
     Pitā añajanasakko me mātā mama sulakkhaṇā 
 Tato kapilavatthūsmiṃ suddhodanagharaṃ gatā 
  
     Sesā   sakyakule jātā sakyānaṃ gharamāgamuṃ 
 Ahaṃ visiṭṭhā sabbāsaṃ jinassapādikā ahuṃ 
  
     Mama putetābhinikkhamma   buddho āsi vināyako 
 Paccāhaṃ pabbajitvāna satehi saha pañcahi 
  
     Sākiyānihi dhīrāhi saha santisukhaṃ phusiṃ 
 Ye tadā pubbajātiyaṃ ambhākaṃ ahu sāmino 
  
     Saha puññassa kattāro mahāsamayakārakā 
 Phusiṃsu arahattaṃ te sugatenānukampitā 
  
     Tadetarā bhikkhunīyo āruhiṃsu nabhatthalaṃ 
 Saṅgatā   viya tārāyo virociṃsu mahiddhikā 
  
     Iddhi anekā dassesuṃ piḷandhavikati   yathā 
 Kammaro kanakasesava kammaññassa susikkhito    
  
     Dassetvā pāṭihirāni vicitatāni    bahuni ca 
 Tosetvā vādipavaraṃ muniṃ saparisaṃ tadā 
  
     Orohitvāna gaganā vanditvā isisattamaṃ 
 Anuññātā naraggena yathāṭhane nisīdisuṃ 
  
      Ahonukampikā amhaṃ sabbāsaṃ vīra gotami 
 Vāsitā tava puññehi pattā no āsavakkhayaṃ 
  
   Sabbāhi itthihi   machasaṃ   Pagā hutvānava sabbayo   machasaṃ   Upaṭṭhahuṃ  machasaṃ   Saṃsarimhaṃ  sīmu machasaṃ   Sabbāpitā   machasaṃ   Sabbā   syā   Sa me putto   syā   Khagatā  sīmu   Piḷanadhavikatiṃ   machasaṃ    Puññakammesu sikkhitā   syā    Vividhāni   syā 
                   
                 
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
     Idadhisu ca vasi homa dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Vetopariyañāṇassa vasi homa mahāmune 
  
     Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāma dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
     Atthe ca dhamme nerutte paṭibhāne ca vijjati 
 Ñāṇaṃ ambhaṃ mahāvīra uppannaṃ tava santike 
  
     Asmāhi pariciṇṇosi mettacittāhi nāyaka 
 Anujānāhi sabbāsaṃ   nibbāsaṃ   nibbānāya mahāmune  
  
      Nibbāyissāma iccevaṃ kiṃ vakkhāmi vadantiyo   
 Yassadāni ca vo kālaṃ maññāthā ti jinobravi 
  
     Gotami ādikā tāyo tadā bhikkhunīyo jinaṃ 
 Vanditvā āsanā tamhā vuṭṭhāya agamaṃsu tā 
  
     Mahatā janakāyena saha lokagganāyako 
 Anusaṃyāsi so   viro mātucchaṃ yāva koṭṭhakaṃ 
  
     Tadā nipati pādesu gotami lokabandhuno 
 Sahetarāhi   sabbāhi pacchimaṃ pādavandanaṃ 
  
      Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ lokanāthassa dassanaṃ 
 Na puno amatākaraṃ passissāmi mukhaṃ tava 
  
     Na ca me vandanaṃ vīra tava pade sukomale 
 Samphusissāmi lokagga ajja gacchāmi nibbutiṃ 
  
   Sabbayo   syā       Vadantinaṃ   simu   Anusaṃsāvayi   syā   Sahevatāhi   machasaṃ 
  
                 
     Rūpena kiṃ tavānena diṭṭhe dhamme yathātathe 
 Sabbaṃ saṅkhatamevetaṃ anassāsitamittaraṃ  
  
     Sā tāhi saha   gantvāna bhikkhunupassayaṃ sakaṃ 
 Aḍḍhapallaṅkamābhujja nisīdi paramāsane 
  
     Tadā upāsikā tattha buddasāsanacchalā 
 Tassā pavattiṃ sutvāna upesuṃ pādavandikā 
  
     Karehi uraṃ pabhanatvā chinnamulā yathā latā 
 Rodantā karuṇaṃ rāvaṃ   sokaṭṭā bhumipātikā   
                   
      Mā no saraṇade nāthe vihāya gami nibbutiṃ 
 Nipatitvāna yācāma sabbāyo sirasā mayaṃ  
  
     Yā padānatamā tāsaṃ saddhā paññā upāsikā 
 Tassā sīsaṃ pamajjanti idaṃ vacanamabravi 
  
      Alaṃ puttā visādena mārapāsānuvattinā 
 Aniccaṃ saṅkhataṃ sabbaṃ viyogantaṃ calācalaṃ  
  
     Tato sā tā vissajjitvā paṭhamaṃ jhānamuttamaṃ 
 Dutiyaṃ tatiyaṃ cāpi samāpajji catutthakaṃ 
  
     Ākāsāyatanañceva viññāṇāyatanaṃ tathā 
 Ākiñcaññaṃ nevasaññaṃ samāpajji yathākkamaṃ 
  
     Paṭilomena jhānāni samāpajjittha gotami 
 Yāvatā paṭhamaṃ jhānaṃ tato yāva catutthakaṃ 
  
     Tato vuṭṭhāya nibbāya dipaciviva nirāsanā   
 Bhūmicālo mahā āsa nabhasā vijjutā pati 
  
     Panāditā dundubhiyo parideviṃsu devatā 
 Pupphavuṭṭhi ca gaganā abhivassatha mediniṃ 
  
     Kampito merurājāpi raṅgamajjhe yathā nāṭo 
 Sokenevātidino ca   viravo āsi sāgaro 
  
   Sā saha tāhi   machasaṃ   Ravaṃ   machasaṃ   Bhumipātitā   machasaṃ bravi pātitā        Nirāsavā   machasaṃ   Sokena cātidinova machasaṃ 
  
                 
     Devā nāgāsurā brahmā saṃviggābhaṃsu   taṅkhaṇe 
  Aniccā vata saṅkhārā yathāyaṃ vilayaṃ gatā 
  
     Yā cemaṃ parivāriṃsu satthusāsanakārikā 
 Tāyopi anuppādānā dipacci   viya nibbutā  
  
      Hā yogā vippayogantā hāniccaṃ sabbasaṅkhataṃ 
 Hā jīvitaṃ vināsantaṃ  iccāsi paridevanā 
  
     Tato devā ca brahmā ca lokadhammānuvattanaṃ 
 Kālānurūpaṃ kubbanti upetvā isisattamaṃ 
                   
     Tadā āmantayi satthā ānandaṃ sutisāgaraṃ  
  Gacchānanda nivedehi bhikkhunaṃ mātunibbutiṃ  
  
     Tadānando nirānando asasunā puṇṇalocano 
 Gaggadena sarenāha  samāgacchantu bhikkhavo 
  
     Pubbadakkiṇapaccāsu uttarāyaṃ vasanti ye 
 Suṇantu bhāsitaṃ mayhaṃ bhikkhavo sugatorasā 
  
     Yā vaḍḍhayi payattena sarīraṃ pacchimaṃ mune 
 Sā gotami gatā santiṃ tārāva suriyodaye 
  
     Budadhamātāni paññattiṃ ṭhapayitvā gatāsamaṃ 
 Na yattha pañcanettopi gataṃ   dakkhati nāyako 
  
     Yassatthi sugate saddhā yo ca piyo   mahāmune buddhamātari   sakkāraṃ karotuṃ sugatoraso  
  
     Suduraṭṭhāpi taṃ sutvā sighamāgañachu bhikkhavo 
 Keci buddhānubhāvena keci iddhisu kovidā 
  
     Kūṭāgagāravare ramme sabbasoṇaṇamaye subhe 
 Mañcakaṃ samaropesuṃ   yattha suttāsi gotami 
  
   Saṃviggahiṃsu   machasaṃ   Dipasikhā   syā   Sutasāgaraṃ   machasaṃ   Gatiṃ   machasaṃ   Yo vā sisso   sīmu   Buddamātussa   machasaṃ budadhassamātu   syā   Samāropesuṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                 
     Cattāro lokapālā te aṃsehi samadhārayuṃ 
 Sesā sakkādayo devā kūṭāgāre samaggahuṃ 
  
     Kūṭāgārāni sabbāni āsuṃ pañcasatānipi   
 Saradādiccavaṇṇāni vissakammakatāni hi 
  
     Sabbāpi tā   bhikkhunīyo āsuṃ mañcesu sāyitā 
 Devānaṃ khandhamāruḷhā niyyanti anupubbaso 
  
     Sabbaso chāditaṃ āsi vitānena nabhatthalaṃ 
 Satārā candasuriyā lañachitā kanakāmayā 
                   
     Patākā ussitā nekā vitatā pupphakañcukā 
 Ogatākāsapadumā mahiyā pupphamuggataṃ 
  
     Dissanti   candasuriyā pajjalanti ca tārakā 
 Majjhaṃgatopi cādicco na tāpeti sasi yathā 
  
     Devā dibbehi gandhehi mālehi surabhihi ca 
 Vāditehi ca nachi saṅgitihi ca pujayuṃ 
  
     Nāgā surā ca brahmāno yathāsatti   yathābalaṃ 
 Pujāyiṃsu ca niyantiṃ nibbutaṃ buddhamātaraṃ 
  
     Sbabayo purato nitā nibbutā sugatorasā 
 Gotami niyate pacchā sakkatā buddhapositā 
  
     Purato devamanujā sanāgāsurabrahmakā 
 Pacchā sasāvako buddho pujatthaṃ yāti mātuyā 
  
     Buddhassa parinibbānaṃ nedisaṃ āsi yādisaṃ 
 Gotami parinibbānaṃ ativacchariyaṃ ahu 
  
     Buddho buddhassa nibbāne   nopadissati   bhikkhavo 
 Budedhā gotaminibbāne sāriputtādikā   tathā 
  
     Citakāni karitvāna sabbagandhamayāni te 
 Gandhacuṇṇāvakiṇṇāni jhāpayiṃsu ca tā tahiṃ 
  
   Pañcasatāni hi   simu   Sabbā tāpi   machasaṃ   Dasasanti   machasaṃ   Yathāsattiṃ   simu   Na buddho buddhanibbāṇe   machasaṃ       Nopaṭiyādi   machasaṃ   Sāriputatādi   syā 
  
                 
     Sesabhāgāni ḍayahiṃsu aṭṭhisesāni sabbaso 
 Ānando ca tadāvoca saṃvegajananaṃ vaco 
  
      Gotami nidhanaṃ yātā daḍḍhaṃ vasasā   sarirakaṃ 
 Saṅke haṃ   budadhanibbānaṃ na cirena bhavisasati  
  
     Tato gotamidhātuni tassā pattagatāni so 
 Upanāmesi nāthassa ānando buddhacodito 
  
     Pāṇinā tāni paggayha avoca isighattamo 
  Māhato sāravattasasa yathā rukkhassa tiṭṭhato 
                   
     Yo so mahattaro khandho palujjeyya aniccatā 
 Tathā bhikkhunīsaṅghassa gotami parinabbutā 
  
     Aho paccariyaṃ mayhaṃ   nibbutāyapi mātuyā 
 Sariramattasesāya natthi sokapariddavo 
  
     Na sociyā paresaṃ sā tiṇṇasaṃsārasāgarā 
 Parivajjitasantāpā sitibhūtā sunibbutā 
  
     Paṇḍitāsi mahāpaññā puphupaññā tatheva ca 
 Rattaññu bhikkhunīnaṃ sā evaṃ dhāretha   bhikkhavo 
     Iddhiyā ca vasi āsi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi āsi ca gotami 
  
     Pubbenivāsaṃ aññāsi dibbacakku visodhitaṃ 
 Sabbāsavaparikkhiṇā natthi tassā punabbhavo 
  
     Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Parisuddhaṃ ahu ñāṇaṃ tasmā socaniyā na sā 
  
     Ayoghanahatasseva jalato jātavedaso 
 Anupubbupasannassa yathā na ñāyate gati 
  
     Evaṃ sammā vimuttānaṃ kāmabandhoghatārinaṃ 
 Paññāpetuṃ gati natthi pattānaṃ acalaṃ padaṃ   
  
     Attadipā tato hotha satipaṭṭhānagocarā 
 Bhāvetvā sattabojjhaṅge dukkhassantaṃ karissathāti 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ mahāpajāpati gotami imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Mahāpajāpati gotami theriyāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
   Ḍayyāñcassā   machasaṃ   Saṅketaṃ   machasaṃ syā       Ānandapassa buddhassa   syā   Jānātha       viññātha   syā   Sukhaṃ   simu machasaṃ 
  
                 
    Khemāpadānaṃ 
     Padumuttaranāmajino sabbadhammesu cakkhumā 
 Ito satasahassambhi kappe uppajaji nāyako 
  
     Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ jātā seṭṭhikule ahuṃ 
 Nānāratanapajjete mahāsukhasamappitā 
                   
     Upetvā taṃ mahāvīraṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ 
 Tato jātappasādāhaṃ upesiṃ saraṇaṃ jinaṃ 
  
     Mātaraṃ pitaraṃ cāpi āyācitvā vināyakaṃ 
 Nimantayitvā sattāhaṃ bhojayiṃ sahasāvakaṃ 
  
     Atikkante ca santāhe mahāpaññānamuttamaṃ 
 Bhikkhunīṃ etadaggambhi ṭhapesi narasārathi 
  
     Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā puno tassa mahesino 
 Kāraṃ katvāna taṃ ṭhānaṃ paṇipacca paṇidahiṃ 
  
     Tato maṃ sa   jino āha  sijjhataṃ paṇidhi tava sasaṃghe me kataṃ kāraṃ appameyyaphalaṃ tayā 
  
     Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena   satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Tassa dhammesu dāyāda orasā dhammanimmitā 
 Ekadadaggaṃ anuppattā khemā nāma bhavissasi  
  
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhiha ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsupagā ahaṃ 
  
     Tato cutā yāmamagaṃ tatohaṃ tusitaṃ gatā 
 Tato ca nimamāṇaratiṃ vasavattipuraṃ tato 
  
     Yattha yatthuppajjāmi tassa kammassa vāhasā 
 Tattha tattheva rājunaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
  
     Tato cutā manussatte rājunaṃ cakkavattinaṃ 
 Maṇḍalinañca rājunaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
  
   Tato mama   simu machasaṃ   Nāmena   simu 
  
                 
     Sampattiṃ anubhotvāna dese manujesu ca 
 Sabbattha sukhitā hutvā nekakāppesu saṃsiriṃ 
  
     Ekanavute ito   kappe vipasasi lokanāyako 
 Uppajji cārunayano   sabbadhammavipassako 
                   
     Tamahaṃ lokanāyakaṃ upetvā narasārathiṃ 
 Dhammaṃ paṇitaṃ sutvāna pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
     Dasavassahassāni tassa virassa sāsane 
 Brahmacariyaṃ caritvāna yuttayogā bahussutā 
  
     Paccayākārakusalā catusaccavisāradā 
 Nipuṇā cittakathikā satthusāsanakārikā 
  
     Tato cutāhaṃ tusitaṃ upapannā yasassini abhibhosiṃ tahiṃ aññe brahmacariyaphalenahaṃ 
  
     Yattha yanthupapannāhaṃ mahābhogā mahaddhanā 
 Medhāvini rupavati   vinitaparisāpi ca 
  
     Bhavāmi tena kammena yogena jinasāsane 
 Sabbā sampattiyo mayhaṃ sulabhā manaso piyā 
  
     Yopi me bhavate bhattā yattha yattha gatāyapi 
 Vimāneti na maṃ koci paṭipattiphalena me 
  
     Imasmiṃ   bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Nāmena koṇāgamano uppajji vadataṃ varo 
  
     Tadāhaṃ   bārāṇasiyaṃ susamiddha   kulapapajā 
 Dhanañajāni sumedhā ca ahampi ca tayo janā 
  
     Saṅghārāmamadāsimbha dānasahāyikā pure   
 Saṅghassa ca vihārampi   udadissa kārikā   mayaṃ
