   Ekanavutito   machasaṃ   Cārudassanā   machasaṃ   Silavati   Imamabhi  machasaṃ   Tadā hi   machasaṃ   Susamidadhi   syā   Nekasahāyikā mune   syā dānaṃ sahāyikā mune        Sasaṅghasasa vihāraṃhi   syā       Dāyikā       
  
                 
     Tato cutā mayaṃ sabbā tāvatiṃsupagā ahuṃ 
 Yasasā aggataṃ pattā manussesu tatheva ca 
  
     Imasmiṃ yeva kappambhi brahmabandhu mahāyeso 
 Kasasapo nāma gottena   uppajji vadataṃ varo 
  
     Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa tadā āsi narissaro 
 Kāsirājā kiki nāma bārāṇasipuruttame 
  
     Tassāsiṃ jeṭṭhikā ṭhitā samaṇi iti vissutā 
 Dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ 
                   
     Anujāni na no tāto akāreva tadā mayaṃ 
 Visavassasahassāni vicarimha atanditā 
  
     Komāribrahmacariyaṃ rājakaññā sukhedhita 
 Khuddhupaṭṭhānaniratā muditā satta dhitaro 
  
     Samaṇi samaṇaguttā ca bhikkhunī bhikkhudāsikā   
 Dhammā ceva sudhammā ca sattami saṅghadāsikā   
  
     Ahaṃ uppalavaṇṇā ca paṭācārā ca kuṇḍalā 
 Kisāgotami dhammadinnā visākhā hoti sattami 
  
     Kadāci so narādicecā dhammaṃ deseti abbhatuṃ 
 Mahānidānasuttantaṃ sutvā taṃ pariyāpuṇiṃ 
  
     Tebhi kammehi sukatehi cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
     Pacchime ca bhavedāni sāgalāyaṃ puruttame 
 Rañño madadassa dhītāmhi manāpā dayitā piyā 
  
     Saha me jātamattamhi khemaṃ tamhi pure ahu 
 Tato khemāti nāmaṃ me guṇato upapajjatha   
  
     Yadāhaṃ yobbanaṃ pattā rūpalāvaññabhusitā   
 Tadā adāsi maṃ tāto bimbisārassa rājino 
  
   Nāthena   sīmu   Bhikkhudāyikā   machasaṃ       Saṅghadāyikā   machasaṃ       Guṇitaṃ upapajjatha         Rūpalāvaṇaṇa vibhusitā   syā rūpavantā vibhusitā       
  
                 
     Tassāhaṃ suppiyā āsiṃ rūpakelāyane ratā 
 Rūpānaṃ dosavāditi na upesiṃ mahādayaṃ 
  
     Bimbisāro tadā rājā mamānuggahabuddhiyā 
 Vaṇaṇayitvā veḷuvanaṃ gāyake gāpayi mamaṃ 
  
      Rammaṃ veḷuvanaṃ yena na diṭṭhaṃ sugatālayaṃ 
 Na tenana nandanaṃ diṭṭhaṃ iti maññāmase mayaṃ 
  
     Yena veḷuvanaṃ diṭṭhaṃ naranandananandanaṃ 
 Sudiṭṭhaṃ nandinaṃ tena amarindasunandanaṃ 
                   
     Vihāya nandanaṃ devā otaritvā mahitalaṃ   
 Rammaṃ veḷuvaṃ disvā na tappatti suvimhitā 
  
     Rājapuññena nibbattaṃ buddhapuññena bhusitaṃ 
 Ko vattā tassa nissesaṃ vanassa guṇasañcayaṃ  
  
     Taṃ sutvā vanasamiddhaṃ mama sotamanoharaṃ 
 Daṭṭhukāmā tamuyyānaṃ rañño ārocayiṃ tadā 
  
     Mahatā parivārena tadā ca   so mahipati 
 Maṃ pesesi   tamuyyānaṃ dassanāya samussukaṃ 
  
      Gaccha passa mahābhoge vanaṃ nettarasāyanaṃ 
 Yaṃ sadā bhāti siriyā sugatābhānurañajitaṃ  
  
     Yadā ca piṇḍāya muni giribbajapuruttame 
 Paviṭṭhohaṃ tadāyeva vanaṃ daṭṭhumupāgamiṃ 
  
     Tadāhaṃ phullavipinaṃ nānāhamarakujitaṃ 
 Kokilāgitasahitaṃ mayuragaṇanacatitataṃ 
  
     Appasaddamanākiṇṇaṃ nānācaṅkamabhusitaṃ 
 Kuṭimaṇḍapasaṅkiṇaṇaṃ yogivaracirājitaṃ 
  
     Vicaranti amaññissaṃ saphalaṃ nayanaṃ mama 
 Tatthāpi taruṇaṃ bhikkhuṃ yuttaṃ disvā vicintayiṃ 
  
   Mahitale   syā       Maṃ   syā       Sampesesi   syā sama pāpesi       
  
                 
     Īrisepi vane   ramme ṭhitatoyaṃ navayobbane 
 Vasantamiva kantena rūpena ca samanacito 
  
     Nisitto rukkhamulambhi muṇḍo saṅghāṭipāruto 
 Jhāyate vatayaṃ bhikkhu hitvā visayajaṃ ratiṃ 
  
     Nanu nāma gahaṭṭhena kāmaṃ bhutvā yathāsukhaṃ 
 Pacchā jiṇeṇana dhammoyaṃ caritabebā subhaddako 
                   
     Suññakatti viditvāna gandhagehaṃ jinālayaṃ 
 Upetvā jinamaddakkhiṃ udayantaṃva bhākaraṃ 
  
     Ekakaṃ sukhamāsinaṃ vijamānā   varitthiyā 
 Disvānevaṃ vicintesiṃ nāyaṃ lukho narāsabho 
  
     Sā kaññā kanakāhāsā padumānanalocanā 
 Bimboṭṭhi kundadasanā manonettarasāyanā 
  
     Hemadolāhasavanā kalasākāra   sutthati 
 Tanumajjhā ca sussoṇi   rambhoru   cārubhusanā 
  
     Rattaṃsukupasabyānā   nilamaṭṭhanivāsanā 
 Atappaneyyarūpena   hāvabhāvasamanavitā   
  
     Disvā tamevaṃ cintesi  ahoyaṃ abirupini 
 Na mayātena nettena diṭṭhapubbā kudācanaṃ  
  
     Tato jarābhubhūtā sā vivaṇaṇā vitatānanā 
 Bhinnadantā setasirā salālavadanāsuci 
  
     Saṅkhittakaṇṇā setakkhi lambāsubhapayodharā 
 Vicitatasabbaṅgi sirāvitatadehini 
  
     Nataṅgā daṇḍadutiyā uppaṇḍuppaṇḍukā   kisā 
 Pavedhamānā patitā nissasanti muhuṃ muhuṃ 
  
   Īdise vipine   machasaṃ   Vijamānaṃ   machasaṃ   Kalikākāra   machasaṃ   Vedimajjhāva sussoṇi   machasaṃ vedimajjhā varasoṇi   syā       Ramemāru   syā       Ratataṃsakasusaṃvitā         Anappaneyyarūpena  sīmu   Sabbābharaṇabhusitā   syā   Uppāsulikatā   machasaṃ 
  
                 
     Tato me āsi saṃvego abbhuto lomahaṃsano 
 Dhiratthu rūpaṃ asuciṃ ramante yattha bālisā 
  
     Tadā mahākāruṇiko disvā saṃviggamānasaṃ 
 Udaggacitto sugato   imā gāthā abhāsatha 
                   
      Āturaṃ asuciṃ putiṃ passa kheme samussayaṃ 
 Uggharantaṃ paggharantaṃ bālānaṃ abhinanditaṃ 
  
     Asubhāya cittaṃ bhāvehi ekaggaṃ susamāhitaṃ 
 Sati kāyagatā tyatthu nibbidābahulā bhava 
  
     Yathā idaṃ tathā etaṃ yathā etaṃ tathā idaṃ 
 Ajjhattiñca bahiddhā ca kāye chandaṃ virājaya 
  
     Animittañca bhāvetha mānānusayamujjaha 
 Tato mānābhisamayā upasantā carissasi 
  
     Ye rāgarattānupatanti sotaṃ 
 Sayaṃ kataṃ makkaṭakova jālaṃ 
 Etampi chetvāna paribbajanti 
 Anapekkhino   kāmasukhaṃ pahāya  
  
     Tato kallitacittaṃ   maṃ ñatvāna narasārathi 
 Mahānidānaṃ desesi suttantaṃ vinayāya me 
  
     Sutvā suttantaseṭṭhaṃ taṃ pubbasaññamanussariṃ 
 Tattha ṭhitāvahaṃ satti dhammacakkhuṃ visodhayiṃ 
  
     Nipatitvā mahesissa pādamulamhi tāvade 
 Accayaṃ desanatthāya idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
      Nāmo te sabbadassāvi namo te karuṇākara 
 Namo te tiṇṇasaṃsāra namo te amataṃdada 
  
   Sumano   syā   Na pekkhino   machasaṃ   Kallikacattaṃ   syā kalika citataṃ       
  
                 
     Diṭṭhigahanapakkhantā   kāmarāgavimohitā 
 Tayā sammā upāyena vinitā cinaye ratā 
  
     Adassanena vibbhogā tādisānaṃ mahesinaṃ 
 Anubhonti mahādukkhaṃ sattā saṃsārasāgare 
  
     Yadāhaṃ lokasaraṇaṃ araṇaṃ maraṇantaguṃ   
 Nāddasāsimaduraṭṭhaṃ desayāmi   tamaccayaṃ 
  
     Mahāhitaṃ varadadaṃ ahitoti visaṅkitaṃ 
 Nopesiṃ rūpaniratā desayāmi tamaccayaṃ  
                   
     Tadā madhuraniggoso mahākāruṇiko jino 
 Avoca tiṭṭha khemetati siñcanto amatena maṃ 
  
     Tadā paṇamya sirasā katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃ 
 Gantvā disvā narapatiṃ idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
      Aho sammāupāyo te cintitoyamarindama 
 Vanadassanakāmāya diṭṭho nibbānedo muni 
  
     Yadi te ruccate rāja   sāne tassa tādino 
 Pabbajissāmi rūpehaṃ nibbintā munivāṇinā   
   Bhāṇavāraṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
     Añajali paggahetvāna tadāha sa mahipati 
  Anujānāmi te bhadde pabbajjā tava sijjhatu  
  
     Pabbajitvā tadācāhaṃ addhamāse   upaṭṭhite 
 Dipodaya ñña bhedañca disvā saṃviggamānasā 
  
     Nibbittā sabbasaṅkhāre paccayākārakovidā 
 Caturoghe atikkamma arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
     Iddhiyā ca vasi āsiṃ dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi cāpi bhavāmahaṃ 
  
   Pakkhandā   machasaṃ   Maraṇanatagaṃ   syā   Desessāmi   syā   Rājā   syā   Munibhāṇinā   syā       Satatamāse   syā     
  
                 
     Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
     Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Parisuddhaṃ mama ñāṇaṃ uppannaṃ buddhasāsane 
  
     Kusalāhaṃ visuddhisu kathāvatthu visāradā 
 Abhidhammanayaññu ca vasippattāmbhi sāsane 
  
     Tato bhojanavatthusamiṃ   raññā kosasāminā 
 Pucchitā nipuṇe pañhe vyākaronti yathātathaṃ 
  
     Tadā sa rājā sugataṃ upasaṅkamma pucchatha 
 Tatheva buddho vyākāsi yathā te vākatā mayā 
  
     Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  Mahāpaññānamaggāti bhikkhunīnaṃ naruttamo 
                   
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ khemā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Khemātheriyāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
    Uppalavaṇṇāpadānaṃ 
     Bhikkhunī uppalavaṇṇā iddhiyā pāramiṅgatā 
 Vanditvā satthuno pāde idaṃ vacanamabravi 
  
     Nittiṇṇā jātisaṃsāraṃ   pattāhaṃ acalaṃ padaṃ 
 Sabbadukkhaṃ mayā khiṇaṃ arocemi mahāmuni 
  
     Yāvatā parisā atthi pasannā jānasāsane 
 Yesañca   meparadhotthi khamantu jānasammukhā 
  
     Saṃsāre saṃsarantāya   khalitaṃ me sace bhave 
 Ārocemi vahāvira aparādhaṃ khamassu taṃ   
  
   Toraṇavatthusaciṃ   machasaṃ sya       Jātisaṃsārā   machasaṃ   Yasā ca   machasaṃ   Saṃsaranatiyā   machasaṃ saṃsaranatā me   syā   Me   syā 
  
                 
      Iddhiṃ cāpi nidassehi mama sāsanakārike 
 Catasso parisā ajja kaṃkhaṃ jindāhi yāvatā  
  
      Dhitu   tuyahaṃ mahāvīra paññāvanta jutijhara 
 Bahuṃ ca dukkaraṃ kammaṃ kataṃ me atidukkaraṃ 
  
     Uppalasseva me vaṇṇo nāmenuppalanāmikā 
 Sāvikā te mahāvīra pade vandati cakkhuma 
  
     Rāhulo ca ahañceva nekajātisate bahu 
 Ekasmiṃ sambhave jātā samānacchandamānasā 
  
     Nibbatti ekato hoti jātisu bahuso mama   
 Pacchimabhave   sampatte ubhopi nānāsambhāvā 
  
     Putto ca rāhulo nāma dhītā uppalasavhayā 
 passa vira mamaṃ iddhiṃ balaṃ dassemi satthuno 
                   
     Mahāsamudde caturo pakkhipi hathepātiyaṃ 
 Telaṃ hatthagataṃ   ceva vejjo   komārako yathā 
  
     Ubbattayitvā paṭhaviṃ pakkhipi hatthapātiyaṃ 
 Cittamuñajaṃ   yathā nāma luñci komārako yuvā 
  
     Cakakavāḷasamaṃ pāṇiṃ chādayitvāna matthake 
 Vassāpetvāna phusitaṃ nānāvaṇaṇaṃ punappunaṃ 
  
     Bhumiṃ udukkhalaṃ katvā dhaññaṃ katvāna sakkharaṃ 
 Sineru musalaṃ katvā maddi komārikā yathā 
  
      Dhitāhaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa nāmenuppalasavahayā 
 Abhiññāsu vasibhūtā tava sāsanakārikā 
  
     Nānā vikubbaṇaṃ katvā dassetvā lokanāyakaṃ 
 Nāmagottañca sāvetvā   pāde vandāmi vakkhuma 
  
   Dhītā   machasaṃ   Jātiyāpi ca ekato   machasaṃ syā       Pacchime bhave   machasaṃ   Vatthigataṃ   simu   Khiḍḍo   machasaṃ   Cittaṃ muñajaṃ  machasaṃ   Pakāsetvā   syā 
  
                 
     Iddhiyā ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi homi mahāmune 
  
     Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā   natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
     Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ me vimalaṃ suddhaṃ pabhāvena mahesino 
  
     Purimānaṃ jinaggānaṃ sammukhā ca parammukhā   
 Adhikāraṃ bahuṃ mayhaṃ tuyhatthāya mahāmuni 
  
     Yaṃ mayā puritaṃ   kammaṃ kusalaṃ sara me   muni 
 Tavatthāya mahāvīra puññaṃ upacitaṃ mayā 
  
     Abhabbaṭṭhāne vajjetvā parivajjenti   anācāraṃ   
 Tavatthāya mahāvīra cattaṃ jīvitamuttamaṃ 
  
     Asakoṭisahassāni adāsiṃ mama   jīvitaṃ 
 Pariccantaṃ   ca me hoti   tavatthāya mahāmuni  
  
     Tadātivimhitā sabbā sirasāva katañajali 
 Avocayye kathaṃ āsi atuliddhiparakkamā 
                   
     Satasahasse ito    kappe nāgakaññā ahuṃ    tadā 
 Vimalā namā nāmena kaññānaṃ sādhusammatā 
  
     Mahorago mahānāgo pasanto jinasāsane 
 Padumuttaraṃ mahātejaṃ nimantesi sasāvakaṃ 
  
     Ratanāmayaṃ    maṇḍapañca pallaṅkaṃ ratanāmayaṃ 
 Ratana    vālukākiṇṇaṃ upabhogaṃ ratanāmayaṃ 
  
     Maggaṃ ca paṭiyādesi ratanaddhajabhusitaṃ 
 Paccuggantvāna sambuddhaṃ vajjanto turiyehi    so 
  
   Sabbāsavaparikkhiṇā   machasaṃ   saṅgamaṃ te nidassitaṃ   machasaṃ   Purimaṃ   syā       Saṃsāre         Vāranto   machasaṃ paripācento   syā   Anācaraṃ   machasaṃ syā   Mayhaṃ   simu   Pariccattā   machasaṃ   Homi   machasaṃ    Satasahasasito   machasaṃ    Ahaṃ   machasaṃ    Ratanamayaṃ  machasaṃ    Ratanaṃ   machasaṃ    Turiyehi   machasaṃ 
  
                 
     Parisāhi catūhi   sahito   lokanāyako 
 Mahoragassa bhavane nisīdi paramāsane 
  
     Annaṃ pānaṃ khādaniyaṃ bhojaniyaṃ   mahārahaṃ 
 Varaṃ varañca pādāsi nāgarājā mahāyaso  
  
     Bhuñjitvāna sambuddho pattaṃ dhoviya   yoniso 
 Anumodaniyaṃkāsi nāgarañño mahiddhino   
  
     Sabbaññuṃ phullitaṃ   disvā nāgakaññā mahāyasā   
 Pasannā   satthuno cittaṃ sunibaddhañca mānasaṃ 
  
     Mamañca ñcittamaññāya jalajuttamanāyako 
 Tasmiṃ khāṇe mahāvīro bhikkhunīṃ dassayiddhiyā 
  
     Iddhi anekā dasessi bhikkhunī sā visāradā 
 Pameditā vedajātā sathoraṃ idamabraviṃ     
  
     Addasāhaṃ imaṃ iddhiṃ sumanāyitarāyapi    
 Kathaṃ ahosi sā vīra iddhiyā suvisāradā  
  
      Orasā mukhato jātā dhītā mama mahiddhikā 
 Mamānusāsanikarā iddhiyā suvisāradā  
  
     Buddhassa vacanaṃ sutvā evaṃ patthesahaṃ tadā   
  Ampi tādisā homi iddhiyā suvisāradā  
                   
     Pameditāhaṃ sumanā pattauttamamānasā   
 Anāgatamhi addhāne īdisā homi nāyaka 
     Maṇimayamhi pallaṅke maṇḍapasmiṃ pabhaṅkare 
 Annapānena tappetvā sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
   Parisāhi ca catūhi   machasaṃ parisāhi ca tasesāhi         Parivuto   machasaṃpharito   syā pareto         Bhojanañca   machasaṃ   Mahāyasaṃ   machasaṃ   Dhovitvā   machasaṃ       Nāgakaññā mahiddhikā   machasaṃ   syā       Sabbañakaduphullitaṃ   simu   Sahāyasaṃ machasaṃ   Pasannaṃ   machasaṃ    Idamabravi   machasaṃ    Sumanaṃ itarāyapi   machasaṃ    Tuṭeṭhā evaṃ avocahaṃ   syā    Patte uttama mānasā   machasaṃ 
  
                 
     Nāgānaṃ pavaraṃ pupphaṃ aruṇaṃ nāma uppalaṃ 
 Vaṇaṇaṃ me īdisaṃ hota pujesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
     Tato cutāhaṃ manuje upapannā sayambhuno 
 Uppalehi paṭicchannaṃ piṇḍapātamadāhaṃ 
  
     Ekanavute ito kappe vipassī nāma nāyako 
 Uppajji cāru nayano sabbadhammesu cakkhumā 
  
     Seṭṭhi dhītā tadā hutvā bārāṇasipuruttame 
 Nimantetvāna sambuddhaṃ sasaṅghaṃ lonāyakaṃ 
  
     Mahādānaṃ daditvāna uppalehi vināyakaṃ 
 Pujayitvā cetasāva   vaṇṇasohaṃ apatthayaṃ 
  
     Imasmiṃ bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma gottena   uppajji vacataṃ varo 
  
     Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa tadā āsi narissaro 
 Kāsirājā kikī nāma bārāṇasipuruttame 
  
     Tassāsiṃ dutiyā dhītā samaṇaguttasamavhayā 
 Dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ 
  
     Anujāni na no tāto agāreva tadā mayaṃ 
 Visaṃ vassasahassāni vicarimbha atanditā 
  
     Komāribuhmacariyaṃ rājakaññā sukhedhitā 
 Buddhupaṭṭhānaniratā muditā sattadhitaro 
  
     Samaṇi samaṇaguttā ca bhikkhunī bhikkhudāsikā   
 Dhammā ceva sudhammā ca sattami saṅghadāsikā  
  
     Ahaṃ khemā ca sappaññā paṭācārā ca kuṇḍalā 
 Kisāgotami dhammadinnā visākhā hoti tassamī 
  
   Ca tebheva   syā       Nāmena   simu   Dāyikā   machasaṃ     
                   
                 
     Tehi kammehi sukatehi cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
     Tato cutā manusessu upapannā mahākule 
 Pītamaṭṭhaṃ   varaṃ dusasaṃ adaṃ arahato ahaṃ 
  
     Tato cutāriṭṭhapure jātā vippakule ahaṃ 
 Dhitā tiriṭavacchassa   ummādanti   manoharā 
  
     Tato cutā janapade kule aññatare ahaṃ 
 Pasutā nātiphitambhi sāliṃ gopemahaṃ tadā 
  
     Disvā paccekasambuddhaṃ pañcalājāsatānahaṃ 
 Datvā padumachantāni pañcaputtasatānipi 
  
     Patthesiṃ tepi patthesuṃ madhuṃ datvā sayambhuno 
 Tato cutā araññehaṃ ajāyiṃ padumodare 
  
     Kāsirañño mahesihaṃ hutvā sakkatapujitā 
 Ajaniṃ rājaputtānaṃ anunaṃ satapañcakaṃ 
  
     Yadā te yobbatappattā kiḷantā jalakiḷitaṃ 
 Disvā opattapadumaṃ āsuṃ paccekanāyakā 
  
     Sāhaṃ tehi vinābhūtā sutavarehi sokini 
 Cutā isigilipasse gāmakambhi ajāyisaṃ 
  
     Yadā cuddhā sutamati sutānaṃ bhattunopi ca 
 Yāgumādāya gacchanti aṭṭhapaccekanāyake 
  
     Bhikkhāya gāmaṃ gacchante disvā putte anussariṃ 
 Dhiradhārā viniggacchi tadā me puttapemasā 
  
     Tato tesaṃ adaṃ yāguṃ pasannā sehi pāṇihi 
 To vutāhaṃ tidase nandanaṃ upapajjahaṃ 
  
     Anubhotvā sukhaṃ dukkhaṃ saṃsaritvā bhavābhave 
 Tavatthāya mahāvīra pariccattañca jīvitaṃ 
                   
     Evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ dukkhaṃ sampatti ca bahubbidhā 
 Pacchime bhave sampatte jātā sāvatthiyaṃ pure 
  
   Pitaṃ maṭṭhaṃ   machasaṃ   Tiriṭivacchassa   machasaṃ   Ummādenti   simu 
  
                 
     Mahādhane seṭṭhikule sukhite sajjite tathā 
 Nānāratanapajjote sabbakāmesamiddhiti 
  
     Sakkatā pujitā āsiṃ mānitāpacitā tathā 
 Rūpasobhaggasampannā kulesu abhisammatā 
  
     Ativa patthitā cāsiṃ rūpabhoga sirihi ca 
 Patthitā seṭṭhiputtehi anekehi satehi ca 
  
     Agāraṃ pajahitvāna pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Aḍḍhamāse asampatte arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
     Iddhiyā abhinimmitvā caturassarathaṃ ahaṃ 
 Buddhassa pade vandissa lokanāthassa sirimato 
  
     Supupphitaggaṃ upagamma bhikkhunī ekā tuvaṃ tiṭṭhasi sālamule 
 Na catthi te dutiyā vaṇṇadhātu bale na tvaṃ bhāyasi dhuttakānaṃ 
  
     Sataṃ sahassānapi dhuttakānaṃ idhāgatā tādisakā bhaveyyuṃ 
 Lomaṃ na icajāmi na santasāmi na māra bhāyāmi 
  
     Phasā antaradhāyāmi kucchiṃ vā pavisāmi te 
 Pakhumantarikāyempi tiṭṭhantiṃ maṃ na dakkhasi 
  
     Vittasmiṃ vasibhūtambhi iddhipādā subhāvitā 
 Sabbabandhanamuttāmbhi na taṃ bhāyāmi āvuso 
  
     Sattisulupamā kāmā khandhāsaṃ adhikuṭṭanā 
 Yaṃ tvaṃ kāmaratiṃ brūsi aratidāni sā mama 
                   
     Sabbattha vihatā nandi tamondho padāḷito 
 Evaṃ jānāhi pāpima nihato tvamasi antaka 
  
                   
     Jino tamhi guṇe tuṭṭho etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
 Aggā iddhimatinanti parisāsu vināyako 
  
     Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
 Ohito garuko bhāro bhavanetti samuhatā 
  
     Yassatthāya pabbajitā agārasmānagāriyaṃ 
 So me attho anuppatto sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo 
  
     Civaraṃ piṇḍapātaṃ ca paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ 
 Khaṇena upanāmenti sahassāni samantato 
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ uppalavaṇṇā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Uppalavaṇṇā theriyāpadānaṃ navamaṃ 
  
    Paṭācārāpadānaṃ 
     Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragu 
 Ito satasahassambhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
  
     Tadāhaṃ saṃsavatiyaṃ jātā seṭṭhikule ahuṃ 
 Nānāratanapajjote mahāsukhasamappitā 
  
     Upevo taṃ mahāvīraṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ 
 Tato jātappasādāhaṃ upesiṃ saraṇaṃ jinaṃ 
  
     Tato vinayadhārinaṃ aggaṃ vaṇeṇasi nāyako 
 Bhikkhunīṃ lajjaniṃ tādiṃ kappākappavisāradaṃ 
  
     Tadā muditacittāhaṃ taṃ ṭhānamabhikaṅkhini 
 Nimantetvā dasabalaṃ sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
     Bhojayitvāna sattāhaṃ daditvā ca ticivaraṃ   
 Nipacaca sirasā pade idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
   Daditvāna ticivaraṃ   machasaṃ daditvā pattacivaraṃ   syā 
  
                   
      Yā tayā vaṇṇitā vīra ito aṭṭhamakehani   
 Tādisāhaṃ bhavissāmi yadi sijjhati nāyaka  
                   
     Tadā avoca maṃ satthā  bhadde mā bhāyi assasa 
 Anāgatambhi addhāne lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ 
  
     Satasahasse ito kappe okakākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gotattena   satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Tassa dhammesu dāyādā orasā dhammanimmitā 
 Paṭācārāti nāmana hessisa satthusāvākā  
  
     Tadāhaṃ muditā hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tato   jinaṃ 
 Menannacittā paricaraṃ sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatisaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
     Imasmiṃ bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma gottena   uppajji vadataṃ varo 
  
     Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa tadā āsi narissaro 
 Kāsirājā kiki nāma bārāṇasisuparuttame 
  
     Tassāsiṃ tatiyā dhītā bhikkhunī iti vissutā 
 Dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ 
  
     Anujāni na no tāto agāreva tadā mayaṃ 
 Visaṃ vassasahassāni vicarimha atanditā 
  
     Komāribrahmacariyaṃ rājakaññā sukhadhitā 
 Buddhupaṭṭhāna niratā muditā satta dhitaro 
  
     Samaṇi samaṇaguttā ca bhikkhunī bhikkhudāsikā 
 Dhammā ceva sudhammā ca sattami saṅghadāsikā 
  
     Ahaṃ uplavaṇṇā ca khemā bhaddā ca bhikkhunī 
 Kisāgotami dhammadinnā visākhā hoti sattami 
  
   Muni   machasaṃ syā   Nāmena   simu   Tadā   machasaṃ   Kāmena   simu 
  
                   
     Tehi kammehi sukatehi cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
     Pacchime ca bhavedāni jātā seṭṭhikule ahaṃ 
 Sāvatthiyaṃ puravare iddhe phīte mahaddhane 
  
     Yadā ca yobbanupetā vitakkavasagā ahaṃ 
 Naraṃ jātapadaṃ   disvā tena saddhiṃ agacchahaṃ 
                   
     Ekaputtappasutāhaṃ dutiyo kucchiyaṃ mama 
 Tadāhaṃ mātāpitaro dakkhāmiti   sunicchitā 
  
     Na rocesi pati   mayhaṃ tadā tamhi pavāsite 
 Ekikā niggatā gehā gantuṃ sāvatthimuttamaṃ 
  
     Tato me sāmi āgantvā sambhāvesi pathe mamaṃ 
 Tadā me kammajā vāta uppannā atidāruṇā 
  
     Uṭṭhito ca mahāmegho pasutisamaye mama 
 Dabbatthāya tadā gantvā sāmi sappena mārito 
  
     Tadā vijātadukkhena anāthā kapaṇā ahaṃ 
 Kunnadiṃ puritaṃ disvā gacchanti sakulālayaṃ 
  
     Bālaṃ ādāya atariṃ parakule ca ekakaṃ 
 Sāyetvā bālakaṃ puttaṃ itaraṃ tāraṇāyahaṃ 
  
     Nivattā ukkusohāsi taruṇaṃ vilapantakaṃ 
 Itarañca vahī soto sāhaṃ sokasamappitā 
  
     Sāvathinegaraṃ gantvā assosiṃ sajane mate 
 Tadā avocaṃ sokaṭṭā mahāsokasamappitā 
  
      Ubho puttā kālakatā panthe mayhaṃ pati mato 
 Mātā pitā ca hātā ca ekacitakasmiṃ ḍayhara  
  
     Tadā kisā ca paṇḍu ca anāthā dinamānasā 
 Ito tato hamantihaṃ   addasaṃ narasārathiṃ 
  
   Sārapatiṃ   machasaṃ   Okkhāmi   machasaṃ     icchāmi   syā   Nārocesiṃ patiṃ   machasaṃ syā   Gacchanatihaṃ   syā 
  
                   
     Tato avoca maṃ satthā  putto mā soci assasa 
 Attānaṃ tvaṃ   gavesassu kiṃ niratthaṃ vihaññasi 
  
     Na satti puttā tāṇāya na pitā napi bandhavā 
 Antakenādhipannassa natthi ñātisu tāṇatā  
  
     Taṃ sutvā munino vākyaṃ paṭhamaṃ phalamajjhagaṃ 
 Pabbajitvāna na ciraṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
                   
     Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Paracittāni jānāmi satthusāsanakārikā 
  
     Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Khepetvā āseve sabbe visuddhāmhi satimmalā 
  
     Tatohaṃ vinayaṃ sabbaṃ santike sabbadassino 
 Uggaṇhaṃ sabbavitthāraṃ vyāhariṃ yathātathaṃ 
  
     Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  Aggā vinayadhārinaṃ paṭācārāva ekikā  
  
     Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
 Ohito garuko bhāro bhavanetti samuhatā 
  
     Yassatthāya pabbajitā agārasmānagāriyaṃ 
 So me attho anuppatto sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo 
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ paṭācārā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Paṭācārātheriyāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ 
  
   Te   sabbattha 
  
                   
                   
    Kuṇḍalakesāpadānaṃ 
     Padamuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragu 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
  
     Tadāhaṃ saṃsavatiyaṃ jātā seṭṭhikule ahuṃ 
 Nānāratanapajjote mahāsukhasamappite 
                   
     Upetvā taṃ mahāvīraṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ 
 Tato jātappasādāhaṃ upesiṃ saraṇaṃ jinaṃ 
  
     Tadā mahākāruṇiko padumuttaranāmako 
 Khippabhiññānamaggatte ṭhapesi bhikkhunīṃ subhaṃ 
  
     Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā dānaṃ datvā mahesino 
 Nipajja sirasā pāde taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃ 
  
     Anumodi mahāvīro bhadde yaṃ tebhipatthitaṃ 
 Samijjhissati taṃ sabbaṃ sukhini bhogi nibbutā 
  
     Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena   satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Tassa dhammesu dāyādā orasā dhammanimmitā 
 Bhadadā kuṇḍakesāti hessasi satthusāvikā 
  
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
     Tato cutā yāmamagā tatohaṃ tusitaṃ gatā 
 Tato ca nimamāṇaratiṃ vasavattipuraṃ tato 
  
     Yattha yatthupapajjāmi tassa kammassa vābhasā 
 Tattha tattheva rājunaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
  
   Nāmena   simu 
  
                   
     Tato cutā manussesu rājunaṃ vasavattinaṃ 
 Maṇḍapinañca rājunaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
  
     Sampattiṃ anubotvāna devesu mānusesu ca 
 Sabbattha sukhinā hutvā nekakappesu saṃsariṃ 
  
     Imasmiṃ bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma gottena   uppajji vadataṃ varo 
     Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa tadā āsi narissaro 
 Kāsirājā kiki nāma bārāṇasi puruttame 
  
     Tassādhitā catutthāsiṃ bhikkhudāsiti vissutā 
 Dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ 
  
     Anujāni na no tāto agāreva tadā mayaṃ 
 Visaṃ vassasahassāni vicarimha atanditā 
  
     Komāribrahmacariyaṃ rājakaññā sukhedhitā 
 Buddhupaṭṭhāna niratā muditā satta dhitaro 
  
     Samaṇi samaṇaguttā ca bhikkhunī bhikkhudāsikā 
 Dhammā ceva sudhammā ca sattami saṅghadāsikā 
                   
     Khemā uplavaṇṇā ca paṭācārā ahaṃ tathā 
 Kisāgotami dhammadinnā visākhā hoti sattami 
  
     Tehi kammehi sukatehi cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
     Pacchime ca bhavedāni giribbajapuruttame 
 Jātā seṭṭhikule phīte yadāhaṃ yobbane phitā 
  
     Coraṃ vadhatthaṃ niyantaṃ disvā rattā tahiṃ ahaṃ 
 Pitā me taṃ sahasseta mocayitvā vadhā tato 
  
     Adāsi tassa maṃ tāto viditvāna manaṃ mama 
 Tassāhamāsiṃ vissatthā   ativa dayitā hitā 
  
     So me bhusanalobhena khalitajjhāsayo   diso 
 Corappapātaṃ netvāna pabbataṃ cetayī vadhaṃ 
  
   Nāmena   simu   Visasaṭṭhā   machasaṃ   Khalimajjhāsayo   machasaṃkhaliṃ paccārahaṃ   syā mālapacchāhataṃ       
  
                    
     Tadāhaṃ paṇamitvāna bhattukaṃ sukatañjali 
 Rakkhanti attano pāṇaṃ idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
      Idaṃ suvaṇṇaṃ keyuraṃ muttā veḷuriyā bahu 
 Sabbaṃ harassu bhaddante mañca dāsiti sāvaya  
  
     Oropayassu kalyāṇi mā bāḷhaṃ paridevasi 
 Na cāhaṃ abhijānāmi ahanatvā dhanamābhataṃ  
  
     Yato sarāmi attānaṃ yato pattasmi viññataṃ 
 Na cāhaṃ abhijānāmi aññaṃ piyataraṃ tayā 
  
     Ehi taṃ upaguhissaṃ kassañca   taṃ padakkhiṇaṃ 
 Na vadāni puno atthi   mama tuyhañca saṅgamo 
  
     Na hi   sabbesu ṭhānesu puriso hoti paṇḍito 
 Itthipi paṇḍitā hoti tattha tattha vivakkhaṇā 
  
     Na hi   sabbesu ṭhānesu puriso hoti paṇḍito 
 Itthipi paṇḍitā hoti lahuṃ atthavicintakā   
                   
     Lahuñca vata khippañca nikiṭṭhe samacetayiṃ 
 Migamuṇaṇā   yathā evaṃ   tadāhaṃ sattukaṃ vadhiṃ 
  
     Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ na khippamanukhujjhati 
 So bhaññate mandamati corova girigabbhare 
  
     Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ khippameva nibodhati 
 Muccate sattusambadhā tadāhaṃ sattukā yathā 
  
     Tadā taṃ pātayitvāna giriduggamhi sattukaṃ 
 Sattikaṃ setavatthānaṃ upetvā pabbajiṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Saṇḍāsena ca kese me luñcitvā sabbaso tadā 
 Pabbājetvā sasamayaṃ ācikkhiṃsu nirantaraṃ 
  
   Katvāna   sīmu machasaṃ   Taṃ vadāmi puna natthi   syā   So   mano   Muhutatamapi cintaye   mano   Nikaṭṭhe   si      nekatthe   simu   Migaṃ uṇaṇā   machasaṃ   Citatapuṇaṇāyatāneva   syā migaṃ puṇaṇāya teneva       
  
                   
     Tato taṃ uggahetvāna nisīditvāna ekikā 
 Samayaṃ taṃ vicintesiṃ suvāno mānusaṃ karaṃ 
  
     Chinnaṃ gayha samipe me pātayitvā apakkami 
 Disvā nimittamalabhiṃ hatthaṃ taṃ puḷavākulaṃ 
  
     Tato vuṭṭhāya saṃviggā apucchiṃ sahadhammike 
 Te avocuṃ vijānanti tamatthaṃ   sakyabhikkhavo 
  
     Sāhaṃ tamatthaṃ pucchissaṃ upetvā buddhasāvake 
 Te mamādāya gacchiṃsu buddhaseṭṭhassa santikaṃ 
  
     So me dhammamadesesi khandāyatanadhātuyo 
 Asubhāniccā dukkhāti   anattāti ca nāyako 
  
     Tassa dhammaṃ suṇitvāhaṃ dhammacakkhuṃ   visodhayiṃ 
 Tato viññātasaddhammā pabbajjaṃ upasampadaṃ 
  
     Āyāciṃ so   tadā āha ehi bhaddeti nāyako 
 Tadāhaṃ upasampanannā parittaṃ   toyamaddasaṃ 
                   
     Pādapakkhālanenāhaṃ ñatvā saudayaṃ vayaṃ   
 Tathā sabbepi saṅkhārā iti saṃvintayiṃ   tadā 
  
     Tato cittaṃ vimucci me anupādāya sabbaso 
 Khippābhiññānamaggaṃ maṃ tadā paññāpayi   jino 
  
     Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Khepetvā jānāmi santhusāsanakārikā 
  
     Pubbanivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhuvisodhitaṃ 
 Khepetvā āsave sabbe visuddhāsiṃ sunimmalā 
  
     Pariciṇeṇā mayā satthā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
 Ohito garuko bhāro bhavanettisamuhatā 
  
   Taṃ atthaṃ   machasaṃ   Asubhāniccadukkhāti   machasaṃ   Dhammacakkhu   machasaṃ   Āyācito   machasaṃ   Gacchanti   si   Saudayabbayaṃ   machasaṃ   Saṅkhāre īdisaṃ cintayiṃ   machasaṃ   Tadā ca ṭhapayi   si 
  
                   
     Yassatthāya pabbajitā agārasamānagāriyaṃ 
 So me attho anupapatto sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo 
  
     Athedhammaniruttisu paṭibhāṇe tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ me vipulaṃ suddhaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa sāsane    
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ bhaddā kuṇḍalakesā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kuṇḍalakesātheriyāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
    Kisāgotami apādānaṃ 
     Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragu 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
  
     Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ jātā aññatare kule 
 Upetvā taṃ naravaraṃ saraṇaṃ samupāgamiṃ 
  
     Dhammañca tassa assosiṃ vatusaccupasaṃhitaṃ 
 Madhuraṃ paramassādaṃ vaṭṭasanti   sukhāvahaṃ 
  
     Tadā ca   bhikkhunīṃ viro lukacivaradhāriniṃ 
 Ṭhapento etaggamhi vaṇaṇayi purisuttamo 
                   
     Janetvānappakaṃ pitiṃ sutvā bhikkhuṇiyā guṇaṃ 
 Kāraṃ katvāna buddhassa yathāsatti yathābalaṃ 
  
     Nipacca municiraṃ taṃ taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ 
 Tādānumodi sambuddho ṭhānalābhāya nāyako 
  
   Vāhasā        Mama buddhassa sāsane   machasaṃ   Catasso   machasaṃ   Citatasanati   syā   Kacāci       
  
                   
     Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādā orasā dhammanimmitā 
 Gotami nāma nāmena   hessasi satthu sāvikā  
  
     Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ 
 Mennacittā paricariṃ paccayehi vināyakaṃ 
  
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
     Imasmiṃ bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma gottena uppajji vadataṃ varo 
     Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa tadā āsi narissaro 
 Kāsirājā kiki nāma bārāṇasi puruttame 
  
     Pañcami tassa dhītāsiṃ dhammā nāmena vissutā 
 Dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ 
  
     Anujāni na no tāto agāreva tadā mayaṃ 
 Visaṃ vassasahassāni vicarimha atanditā 
  
     Komāribrahmacariyaṃ rājakaññā sukhedhitā 
 Buddhupaṭṭhāna niratā muditā satta dhitaro 
  
     Samaṇi samaṇaguttā ca bhikkhunī bhikkhudāsikā 
 Dhammā ceva sudhammā ca sattami saṅghadāsikā 
  
     Khemā uplavaṇṇā ca paṭācārā ca kuṇḍalā 
 Ahaṃ ceva dhammadinnā visākhā hoti sattami 
  
     Tehi kammehi sukatehi cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃgacchahaṃ 
  
     Pacchime ca bhavedāni jātā seṭṭhikule ahaṃ 
 Duggate adhane naṭṭhe   gatā ca sadhanaṃ kulaṃ 
  
     Patiṃ ṭhapetvā sesā disanti   adhanā iti 
 Yadā ca sasutā   āsiṃ sabbesaṃ dayitā tadā 
  
   Kisāgotami nāmena   machasaṃ   Nica   syā nidedha         Desasanati   machasaṃ   Pasutā   machasaṃ 
                   
                   
     Yadā so taruṇo bhado komalaṅgo   sukhedhito 
 Sapāṇamiva kanto me tadā yamacasaṃ gato 
  
     Sokaṭṭā dinavadanā assunettā rudammukhā 
 Mataṃ kuṇapamādāya vilapanti bhamāmahaṃ 
  
     Tadā ekena sandiṭṭhā upetvā bhisajuttamaṃ   
 Avocaṃ  dehi bhesajjaṃ puttasañajivananti bho  
  
      Na vijjante matā yasamiṃ gehe siddhathekaṃ tato 
 Āharā ti jino āha vinayopāyakovido 
  
     Tadā gamitvāna sāvatthiyaṃ na labhiṃ tādisaṃ gharaṃ 
 Kuto siddhatthakaṃ kasmā tato laddhā satiṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Kuṇapaṃ chaḍḍhayitvāna upesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Duratova mamaṃ disvā avoca madhurassaro 
  
      Yoca vassasataṃ jive apassaṃ udayabbayaṃ 
 Ekāhaṃ jīvitaṃ seyyo passato udayabbayaṃ 
  
     Na gāmadhammo no nigamassa dhammo 
 Nacāpayaṃ ekakulassa dhammo 
 Sabbassa lokassa sadevakassa 
 Esova dhammo yadidaṃ aniccatā  
  
     Sāhaṃ sutvānimā gāthā dhammacakkhuṃ visodhayiṃ 
 Tato viññātasaddhammā pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
     Tathā pabbajitā santi yuñajanti jinasāsane 
 Na cireneva kālena arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
     Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Paracittāni jānāmi satthusāsanakārikā 
  
     Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhuṃ visodhitaṃ 
 Khepetvā āsave sabbe visuddhāsiṃ sunimmalā 
  
   Putto   simu   Komalako   machasaṃ komārako   syā   Bhisakakunatamaṃ   machasaṃ bhisagutatamaṃ   simu 
  
                   
     Pariciṇeṇā mayā satthā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
 Ohito garuko bhāro bhavanettisamuhatā 
                   
     Yassatthāya pabbajitā agārasamānagāriyaṃ 
 So me attho anupapatto sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo 
  
     Athedhammaniruttisu paṭibhāṇe tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ me vimalaṃ suddhaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa vāhasā 
  
     Saṅkārakuṭā āhatvā susānā rathiyāpi ca 
 Tato saṅghāṭikaṃ katvā lukhaṃ dharemi civaraṃ 
  
     Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho lukhavicaradhāraṇe 
 Ṭhapesi etadaggamhi parisāsu vināyako 
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ bhaddā kisāgotami bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kisāgotamitheriyāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
    Dhammadinnāpādānaṃ 
     Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragu 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
  
     Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ kule aññatare ahuṃ 
 Parakammakari āsiṃ nipakā silasaṃvutā 
  
     Padumuttara buddhassa sujāto aggasāvako 
 Vihārā abhinikkhamma piṇḍapātāya gacchati 
  
     Ghaṭaṃ gahetvā gacchanti tadā udakahārikā 
 Taṃ disvā adadiṃ   puvaṃ   pasannā sehi pāṇihi 
  
   Adadaṃ   machasaṃ   Supaṃ       
  
                   
     Paṭiggahetvā tattheva nisinno paribhuñaji so 
 Tato netvāna taṃ gehaṃ adāsiṃ tassa bhojanaṃ 
  
     Tato me ayyako tuṭṭho akari suṇisaṃ sakaṃ 
 Sassuyā saha gantvāna sambuddhaṃ abhivādayiṃ 
  
     Tadā so dhammakathikaṃ bhikkhunīṃ parikittayaṃ 
 Ṭhapesi etadaggasmiṃ taṃ sutvā muditā ahaṃ 
                   
     Nimantayitvā sugataṃ sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Mahādānaṃ daditvāna taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃ 
  
     Tato maṃ sugato āha ghananinnādasussaro 
  Mamupaṭṭhānanirate sasaṅghaṃ parivesike 
  
     Saddhammasamaṇe yutte guṇavaḍḍhitamānase 
 Bhadde bhavassu muditā lacchase paṇiḍhiphalaṃ 
  
     Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Tassa dhammesu dāyādā orasā dhammanimmitā 
 Dhammadinnāti nāmena hessasi satthu sāvikā  
  
     Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā yāvajīvaṃ mahāmuniṃ 
 Mennacittā paricariṃ paccayehi vināyakaṃ 
  
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
     Imasmiṃ bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma gottena uppajji vadataṃ varo 
     Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa tadā āsi narissaro 
 Kāsirājā kiki nāma bārāṇasi puruttame 
  
     Chaṭṭhā tassāsahaṃ ṭhitā sudhammā iti vissutā 
 Dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggagassa pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ 
  
                   
     Nānujānāsi   maṃ tāto agārenālayā   mayaṃ 
 Visaṃ vassasahassāni vicarimbha atanditā 
   Bhāṇavāraṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     Komāribrahmacariyaṃ rājakaññā sukhedhitā 
 Buddhupaṭṭhāna niratā muditā satta dhitaro 
  
     Samaṇi samaṇaguttā ca bhikkhunī bhikkhudāsikā 
 Dhammā ceva sudhammā ca sattami saṅghadāsikā 
  
     Khemā uplavaṇṇā ca paṭācārā ca kuṇḍalā 
 Gotami ca ahaṃ ceva visākhā hoti sattami 
  
     Tehi kammehi sukatehi cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃgacchahaṃ 
                   
     Pacchime ca bhavedāni giribbajapuruttame 
 Jātā seṭṭhikule phīte sabbakāmasamiddhake   
  
     Yadā rūpaguṇopetā paṭhame yobbate ṭhitā 
 Tadā parakulaṃ gantvā vasiṃ sukhasamappitā 
  
     Upetvā lokasaraṇaṃ suṇitvā dhammadesanaṃ 
 Anāgāmiphalaṃ patto sāmiko me sukhuddhimā 
  
     Tadā taṃ anujānetvā pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Na cireneva kālena arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
     Tadā upāsako so maṃ upagantvā apucchatha 
 Gambhire nipuṇe paññe te sabbe vyākariṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
 Bhikkhunīṃ dhamammakathikaṃ nāññaṃ passāmi edisaṃ 
  
     Dhammadinnā yathā dhīrā evaṃ dhāretha bhikkhavo 
 Evāhaṃ paṇḍatā jātā nāyakenānukampitā 
  
     Pariciṇeṇā mayā satthā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
 Ohito garuko bhāro bhavanettisamuhatā 
  
     Yassatthāya pabbajitā agārasamānagāriyaṃ 
 So me attho anupapatto sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo 
  
   Anujāni no   machasaṃ   Samidadhine   machasaṃ   Sabbakāmisamiddhane 
  
                   
     Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Paracittāni jānāmi satthu sāsanakārikā 
  
     Pubbanivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Khepetvā āsave sabbe visuddhāmhi sunimmalā 
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ dhammadinnā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Dhammadinnātheriyāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
    Sakulāpadānaṃ 
     Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragu 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
     Hitāya sabbasattānaṃ sukhāya vadataṃ varo 
 Atthāya purisājañño paṭipanno sadevake 
                   
     Yasaggappatto simā vaṇṇakittibhattā jino 
 Pujito sabbalokassa disā sabbāsu vissuto 
  
     Uttiṇṇavicikiccho so vitivattakathaṃkatho 
 Sampuṇaṇamanasaṅkappo patto sambodhimuttamaṃ 
  
     Anuppantassa maggassa uppādetā naruttamo 
 Anakkhātañca akkhāsi asasañajātañca sañajati 
  
     Maggañcu ca maggavidu maggakkhāyi nanarāsabho 
 Maggassa kusalo satthā sārathinaṃ varuttamo 
  
     Mahākaruṇiko satthā   dhammaṃ desesi nāyako 
 Nimugge kāmapaṅkambhi samuddharati pāṇino 
  
   Kittivaṇaṇagato   machasaṃ   Tadā mahākāruṇiko   simu 
  
                   
     Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ jātā khattinandanā 
 Surūpā sadhanā cāsiṃ dayitā ca sirimati 
  
     Ānandassa mahārañño dhītā paramasobhanā 
 Vemātu  bhagini cāpi padumuttaranāmino 
  
     Rājakaññāhi sahitā sabbabharaṇabhusitā 
 Upagamma   mahāvīraṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ 
  
     Tadā hi so lokagaru bhikkhunīṃ dibbacakkhukaṃ 
 Kittayaṃ parisāmajjhe   aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapesi taṃ 
  
     Suṇitvā tamahaṃ haṭṭhā dānaṃ datvāna santhuno 
 Pujetvāna   ca sambuddhaṃ dibbacakkhuṃ apatthayiṃ 
  
     Tato   avoca maṃ satthā  nande lacchasi patthitaṃ 
 Padipadhammadānānaṃ phalametaṃ sunicchitaṃ 
  
     Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Tassa dhammesu dāyādā orasā dhammanimmitā 
 Sakulā nāma   hessasi satthusāvikā  
                   
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
     Imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma gottena uppajji vadataṃ varo 
     Paribbājakini āsiṃ tadāhaṃ ekacārini 
 Bhikkhāya vicaritvāna alabhiṃ telamattakaṃ 
  
     Tena dīpaṃ padipetvā upaṭṭhiṃ sabbasaṃvariṃ 
 Cetiyaṃ dipadaggassa   vippasannena cetasā 
  
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
   Vemātā   machasaṃ   Upāgamma   machasaṃ   Catuparisāya majjhe   syā 
   Pujitvāna   machasaṃ   Tadā   simu   Sakulāti ca   syā   Davipadagagasasa   machasaṃ 
  
                   
     Yattha yatthupapajjāmi tassa kammassa vāhasā 
 Pajjalanti   mahādipā tattha tattha gatāya me 
  
     Tirokuḍḍaṃ tiroselaṃ samatiggayha pabbataṃ 
 Passāmahaṃ   yadiccāmi dipadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Visuddhanayanā homi yasasā ca jalāmahaṃ 
 Saddhāpaññāvati ceva dipadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Paccime ca havedāni jātā vippakule ahaṃ 
 Pahutadhanadhaññamhi mudite rājapujite 
  
     Ahuṃ   sabbaṅgasampannā sabbābharaṇabhusitā 
 Purappavese sugataṃ vātapāne ṭhitā ahaṃ 
  
     Disvā jalantaṃ yasasā devamānusa   sakkataṃ 
 Anubyañajana   sampannaṃ lakkhaṇehi vibhusitaṃ 
  
     Udaggacittā sumanā pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ 
 Na cireneva kālena arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
     Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Paracittāni jānāmi satthusāsanakārikā 
  
     Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Khepetvā āsave sabbe visuddhāsiṃ sunimmalā 
  
     Pariciṇṇo mahā satthā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
 Ohito garukobhāro bhavanetti samuhatā 
                   
     Yassatthāya pabbajitā agārasmānagāriyaṃ 
 So me attho anuppatto tibbasaṃyojanakkhayo 
  
     Tato mahākāruṇino etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  Dibbacakkhukinaṃ aggā sakulā ti naruttamo 
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ sakulā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sakulātheriyāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
   Saṃjalanti   syā saṃvaranti         Pasāyāmihaṃ   simu   Ahaṃ   machasaṃ   Devamanusasa   machasaṃ   Anuvyañajana   simu 
  
                   
    Nandājanapadakalyāṇi apadānaṃ 
  
     Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragu 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
     Ovādako viññāpako kārako sabbajāṇinaṃ 
 Desanākusalo buddho tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ 
  
     Anukampako kāruṇiko hitesi sabbapāṇinaṃ 
 Sampatte titthiye sabbe pañcasile patiṭṭhahi 
  
     Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi suññakaṃ titthiyehi ca 
 Vicinnaṃ arahantehi vasibhutehi tādihi 
  
     Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ uggato so mahāmuni 
 Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso khattiṃsavaralakkhaṇo 
  
     Vassasatasahassāni āyu vijjati tāvade 
 Tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ 
     Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ jātā seṭṭhikule ahuṃ 
 Nānāratatapajjota mahāsukhasamappite 
  
     Upetvā taṃ mahāvīraṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ 
 Amataṃ paramassādaṃ paramatthanivedakaṃ 
  
     Tadā nimantayitvāna sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ   
 Datvā tassa mahādānaṃ pasantā sehi pāṇihi 
                   
     Jhāyininaṃ bhikkhunīnaṃ aggaṭṭhānaṃ apatthayiṃ 
 Nipacca sirasā viraṃ sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
     Tadā adantadamako tilokasaraṇo pabhu 
 Vyākāsi narasaddulo   lacchase taṃ pasupatthitaṃ 
  
     Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
   Tibhavatatagaṃ         Byākāsi narasārathi   machasaṃ   sārathi     
  
 Piṭuva     
     Tassa dhammesu dāyādā orasā dhammanimmitā 
 Nandāti nāma hessasi satthusāvikā  
  
     Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ 
 Mettacittā paricariṃ paccayehi vināyakaṃ 
  
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
     Tato cutā yāmamagaṃ tatohaṃ tusitaṃ agaṃ   
 Tato ca nimmāṇaratiṃ vasavattipuraṃ tato   
  
     Yattha yatthupapajjāmi tassa kammassa vāhasā 
 Tattha tattheva rājānaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
  
     Tato cutā manussatte rājānaṃ cakkavattinaṃ 
 Maṇḍalinañca rājānaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
  
     Sampattiṃ anubhotvāna devesu manujesu ca 
 Sabbattha sukhitā hutvā nekakappesu saṃsariṃ 
  
     Pacchime bhave sampatte purambhi   kapilavhaye 
 Rañño suddhodanassāhaṃ dhītā āsiṃ aninditā 
  
     Siriṃva   rūpiniṃ disvā nanditaṃ āsi taṃ kulaṃ 
 Tena nandati me nāmaṃ sundaropapadaṃ   ahu 
  
     Yuvatinañca sabbāsaṃ kalyāṇiti ca vissutā 
 Tasmimpi nagare ramme ṭhapetvā ca   yasodharā 
  
     Jeṭṭho hātā tilokaggo pacchimo   arahā tathā 
 Ekānini gahaṭṭhāhaṃ mātarā paricoditā 
                   
      Sākiyamhi kule jātā putte buddhānujā tuvaṃ 
 Nandenapi vinā bhūtā agāre kinnu vacchasi  
   Gatā   machasaṃ   Gatā   syā   Suramme   simu machasaṃ   Siriyā  machasaṃ   Sundaraṃ pavaraṃ   machasaṃ     sundarā pavarā   syā   Ṭhapetvā taṃ   machasaṃ   Majjhimo   si     
  
                   
     Jarāvasānaṃ yobbaññaṃ rūpaṃ asuvisammataṃ 
 Rogantampi ca ārogyaṃ jīvitaṃ maraṇantikaṃ 
  
     Idampi te subhaṃ rūpaṃ sasikantaṃ manoharaṃ 
 Bhusanānamalaṅkāraṃ sirisaṅghātasantanibhaṃ 
  
     Piṇḍitaṃ   lokasāraṃva nayanānaṃ rasāyanaṃ 
 Puññānaṃ kittijananaṃ okkākakula   nandanaṃ 
  
     Na cireneva kālena jarā samatibhossati   
 Vihāya gehaṃ tāruññe   cara dhammamanindite 
  
     Sutvāhaṃ mātuvacanaṃ pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Dehena natu cittena rūpayobbanalālitā   
  
     Mahatā ca payantena jhānajjhenaparaṃ mamaṃ   
 Kātuṃ ca vadate mātā na cāhaṃ tattha ussukā 
  
     Tato mahākāruṇiko disvā maṃ kāmalālasaṃ   
 Nibbindanatheṃ rūpasmiṃ mama cakkhupathe jino 
  
     Sakena anubhāvena   itthiṃ māpesi sobhaniṃ 
 Dassaniyaṃ suruciraṃ mamatopi surūpiniṃ 
  
     Tamahaṃ vimhitā disvā ativimhitadehiniṃ 
 Cittahayiṃ saphalaṃ meti nettalābhañca mānusaṃ 
  
     Tamahaṃ ehi subhage yenatthā taṃ vadehi me 
 Kulaṃ te nāmagottañca vada me yadi te piyaṃ 
  
     Na pañcakālo   subhage ucchaṅge maṃ nivesaya    
 Sidantiva    mamaṅgāni supasuppaya muhuttakaṃ 
  
     Tato sisaṃ mamaṅke sā katvā sayi sulocanā 
 Tassā nalāṭe patitā lutā    paramadāruṇā 
  
   Puñajitaṃ   si machasaṃ       Ukkākaka   machasaṃ   Samadhisessati   machasaṃ       Kāruññe   si machasaṃ       Lāḷitā   machasaṃ   Mama   machasaṃ   Kamalānanaṃ   syā   Ānubhāvena   machasaṃ   Cañcakālo   machasaṃ    Nivāsaya   machasaṃ    Nisidanti   si        Luddhā   machasaṃ 
  
                   
     Saha tassā nipātena siḷakā uppajjatha 
 Pagghariṃsu pahittā ca kuṇapā pubbalohitā 
  
     Pabhinnaṃ vadanaṃ cāsi kuṇapaṃ putigandhikaṃ   
 Udadhumātaṃ vinilañca vipubbañca   sarirakaṃ 
  
     Sā pavedhitasabbaṅgi nissasanti muhuṃ muhuṃ 
 Vedayanti sakaṃ dukkhaṃ karuṇaṃ paridevayi 
  
      Dukkhena dukkhitā homi phusayanti ca vedanā 
 Mahādukkhe nimuggāmhi saraṇaṃ hohi me sakhi  
  
      Kuhiṃ vadanasohā te kuhiṃ te tuṅganāsikā 
 Tambabimbavaroṭṭhaṃ te vadanaṃ te kuhiṃ gataṃ 
  
     Kuhiṃ sasinibhaṃ vantaṃ   kambugivā kuhiṃ gatā 
 Doḷālālā ca   te kaṇaṇā vevaṇṇaṃ samupāgatā 
  
     Makuḷamburuhākārā   kalasāva   payodharā 
 Pabhinnā putikuṇapā duggandhittamāgatā 
  
     Tanumajjhā puthussoṇi   sunā vaṇitakibbisā   
 Jātā amejjhaharitā aho rūpaṃ asassataṃ 
  
     Sabbaṃ sarirasañajātaṃ putigandhaṃ bhayānakaṃ 
 Susānamiva bibhacchaṃ ramante yattha bālisā   
                   
     Tadā mahākāruṇiko bhātā me lokanāyako 
 Disvā saṃviggacittaṃ maṃ imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
      Āturaṃ asuciṃ passa nande samussayaṃ 
 Asubhāya cittaṃ bhāvehi ekaggaṃ susamāhitaṃ 
  
     Yathā idaṃ tathā etaṃ yathā etaṃ tathā idaṃ 
 Duggandhaṃ putikaṃ vāpi bālānaṃ abhinanditaṃ 
  
   Putigandhanaṃ   machasaṃ   Pubbañcāpi   machasaṃ sabbañcāpi         Vaṇaṇaṃ  machasaṃ   Doḷālolāva   machasaṃ dāmāmālañca   syā   Makuḷakārakākārā  machasaṃ makuḷapadumākārā   syā   Kalikā ca   machasaṃ   Vedibajjhāva sussoṇi   machasaṃ vedimajjhā puthusessāṇi         Yunāva nitakibbisā   machasaṃ   Bāliyā   simu 
  
                   
     Evametaṃ acekkhanti rattindivamatanditā 
 Tato satāya paññāya abhinibbijja dakkhasi  
  
     Tatohaṃ atisaṃviggā   sutvā gāthā subhāsitā 
 Tatuṭṭhitā vipassanti   arahattamapāpuṇaṃ 
  
     Yattha yattha nisinnāhaṃ sadā jhānaparāyanā 
 Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ nandā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Nandātheriyāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
    Soṇāpadānaṃ 
     Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragu 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
     Tadā seṭṭhikule jātā sukhitā pujitā piyā 
 Upetvā taṃ munivaraṃ assosiṃ madhuraṃ vacaṃ 
  
     Āraddhaviriyānagga vaṇeṇasi   bhikkhunīṃ jino 
 Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā kāraṃ katvāna satthuno 
  
     Abhivādetvā sambuddhaṃ taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayiṃ tadā 
 Anumodi mahāvīro  sijjhataṃ paṇidhi tava 
  
     Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
                   
     Tassa dhammesu dāyādā orasā dhammanimmitā 
 Nandāti nāma hessasi satthusāvikā  
  
     Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ 
 Mettacittā paricariṃ paccayehi vināyakaṃ 
  
   Tatohamāsiṃ saṃviggā   syā       Tatuṭṭhitāvahaṃ santi   machasaṃ   Vaṇeṇati   syā 
  
                   
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
     Pacchime ca bhavedāni jātā saṭṭhikele ahaṃ 
 Sāvatthiyaṃ puravare iddhe phīte mahaddhane 
  
     Yadā ca yobbanappattā gantvā patikulaṃ ahaṃ 
 Dasaputtāni ajaniṃ surūpāni visasato 
  
     Sukhedhitā ca te sabbe jananettamanoharā 
 Amitatānampi te rucitā mamaṃ sageva   te piyā 
  
     Tato mayhaṃ akāmāya dasapuntapurakkhato 
 Pabbajittha sa me bhattā devadevassa sāsane 
  
     Tadekikā vicintesuṃ jivitenālamatthu me 
 Cattāya   patiputtehi vuṭṭhāya ca varākiyā 
  
     Ahmapi tattha gacchissaṃ sampatto yattha me pati  
 Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
     Tato ca maṃ bhikkhunīyo evaṃ bhikkhunupassaye 
 Vihāya gacchumovādaṃ  tāpehi udakaṃ  iti 
  
     Tadā udakāhitvā okiritvā kumhiyā 
 Cullyaṃ   ṭhapetvā āsinā tato cittaṃ samādahiṃ 
  
     Khandhe aniccato disvā dukkhato ca antatato 
 Chenvāna   āsave sabbe arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
     Tadāgantvā bhikkhunīyo uṇhodakamapucchisuṃ 
 Tejodhātuṃ adhiṭā khippaṃ santāpayiṃ jalaṃ 
                   
     Vimhitā tā jinavaraṃ etamatthamasāvayuṃ 
 Taṃ sutvā mudito nātho imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha 
  
   Paṇehi   si   Jināya   si syā       Culle   si machasaṃ syā       Khepetvā   syā     
  
                   
     Yo ce   vassasataṃ jive kusito hinaviriyo 
 Ekāhaṃ jīvitaṃ seyyo viriyamārabhato daḷahaṃ  
  
     Ārādhito mahāvīro mama   suppaṭipattiyā 
 Āraddhaviriyānaggaṃ mamāha sa   mahāmuni 
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ soṇā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Soṇātheriyāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
    Bhaddākāpilāni apadānaṃ 
     Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragu 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako 
     Tadāhu haṃsavatiyaṃ videho nāma nāmato   
 Seṭṭhi pahutaratano tassa jāyā ahosahaṃ 
  
     Kadāci so narādiccaṃ upecca saparijjano   
 Dhammamassosi buddhassa sabbadukkhakkhayāvahaṃ   
  
     Sāvakaṃ dhutavādānaṃ aggaṃ kittesi nāyako 
 Sutvā sattāhitaṃ dānaṃ datvā buddhassa tādino 
  
     Nipacca sirasā pāde taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayi 
 Sa hāsayanto parisaṃ tadā hi narapuṅgavo 
  
     Seṭṭhino anukampāya imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  Lacchase patthitaṃ ṭhānaṃ nibbuto hohi puttaka 
                   
     Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
   Ca   simu machasaṃ   Mayā   sīmu machasaṃ   Mamaṃ bhāsi   simu   Sabbadhammānapāragu  machasaṃ   Nāmako   syā     nāyako   thea   Sapari jano   thea   Sabbadukkhabhayappahaṃ   simu machasaṃ 
  
                   
     Tassa dhammesu dāyādā orasā dhammanimmitā 
 Kassapo nāma nāmena hessasi satthusāvikā  
  
     Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ 
 Mettacittā paricariṃ paccayehi vināyakaṃ 
  
     Sāsanaṃ jotayitvāna   madaditvā ca kutithiye 
 Veneyye   vinayitvā ca nibbuto so sasāvako 
  
     Nibbute tamahi lokagge pujanatthāya satthuno 
 Ñātimitte samānetvā saha tehi akārayi 
  
     Sattaṭojanikaṃ thupaṃ ubbiddhaṃ ratanāmayaṃ 
 Jalantaṃ sataraṃsiva sālarājavaṃva phullitaṃ 
  
     Sattasatasahassāni pātiyo   tattha kārayi 
 Naḷaggi viya jotanti   rataneheva sattahi 
  
     Gandhatelena puretvā dipānujālayi tahiṃ 
 Pujatthāya   mahesissa sabbabhūtānukampino 
  
     Santa satasahassāni puṇaṇakumbhāni kārayī 
 Rataneheva puṇṇāni pujatthāya mahesino 
  
     Majjhe aṭṭhaṭṭha kumbhinaṃ ussitā kañcanagghiyā 
 Atirocanti vaṇeṇana saradeva divākaro 
  
     Catudvāresu sobhanti toraṇā ratanāmayā 
 Ussitā phalakā rammā sobhanti ratanāmayā 
  
     Virocanti parikkhittā avataṃsā   sunimmitā 
 Ussitāni paṭākāni ratanāni virocare 
  
     Surattaṃ sukataṃ cetaṃ   cetiyaṃ ratanāmayaṃ 
 Atirocati vaṇeṇana sasañejhāva   divākare 
  
   Jotayitvā so   simu thea   Veneyyaṃ   machasaṃ   Cātiyo   syā   Jotante   syā       Pujanatthāya   machasaṃ pujāya   syā   Avaṭaṃsā   machasaṃ   Vitakaṃ   machasaṃ   Sasañjhāva   syā 
  
                   
                   
     Thupassa vediyo tisso   haritālena purayi 
 Ekaṃ manosilāyekaṃ añajanena ca ekikaṃ 
  
     Pujāmetādisaṃ rammaṃ kāretvā varavādino 
 Adāsi dānaṃ saṅghassa yāvajīvaṃ yathābalaṃ 
  
     Sahāhaṃ seṭṭhinā tena tāni puññāni sabbaso 
 Yāvajīvaṃ karitvāna sahāva sugatiṃ gatā 
  
     Sampattiyonubhotvāna devatte atha mānuse 
 Chāyā viya sarirena saha teneva saṃsariṃ 
  
     Ekanavute ito kappe vipassi nāma nāyako 
 Uppajji cārunayano   sabbadhammavipasasako 
  
     Tadāyaṃ bandhumatiyaṃ brāhmaṇo sādhusammato 
 Aḍḍho satthāgamenāsi   dhanena ca suduggato 
  
     Tadāpi tassahaṃ āsiṃ brahmaṇi samacetasā 
 Kadāci so dijavaro saṃgamesi mahāmuniṃ 
  
     Nisinnaṃ janakāyasmiṃ desentaṃ amataṃ padaṃ 
 Sutvā dhammaṃ pamudito adāsi ekasāṭakaṃ 
  
     Gharamekena vatthenāgatvānetaṃ   mamabraviṃ   
 Anumoda mahāññe   dinnaṃ buddhassa sāṭakaṃ 
  
     Tadāhaṃ añjaliṃ katvā anumodiṃ supiṇitā   
 Suditto sāṭako sāmi buddhaseṭṭhassa tādino 
  
     Sukhito sajjito hutvā saṃsaranto bhavābhāvo 
 Bārāṇasipure ramme rā āsi mahipati 
                   
     Tadā tassa mahesihaṃ itthigumbassa uttamā 
 Tassātidayitā āsiṃ pubbasenahena hatatuno   
  
   Thupassimā disā tisso   si syā thupassima dipādiyo   thea   Aḍḍho santo guṇenāpi   machasaṃ   Vatthena gantvānetaṃ   machasaṃ syā   Sa mabravi  machasaṃ   Mahāpuññe   thea mahāpuññaṃ   machasaṃ       Supitiyā   the a   Cuttari   syā     bhattari   the a 
  
                   
     Piṇḍāya vicarante so   aṭṭha paccekanāyake 
 Disvā pamudito hutvā datvā piṇḍaṃ mahārahaṃ 
  
     Pano nimantayitvāna katvā ratanamaṇḍapaṃ 
 Kammārehi kataṃ chatataṃ   sovaṇṇaṃ satahatthakaṃ   
  
     Samānetvāna te sabbe tesaṃ dānamadāsi so 
 Soṇaṇāsanopaviṭṭhānaṃ   pasanno sehi pāṇihi 
  
     Tampi dānaṃ sahādāsiṃ kāsirājenahaṃ tadā 
 Punāhaṃ bārāṇasiyaṃ ajāyiṃ dvāragāmake   
  
     Kuṭumbikakule phīte sukhito so sabhātuko 
 Jeṭṭhassa bhātuno jāyā ahosiṃ supatibbatā 
  
     Paccekabuddhaṃ disvāna mama bhattu kaniyasi   
 Bhāgannaṃ tassa datvāna āgate tambhi pāvadi   
  
     Nābhinandittha so dānaṃ tato tassa adāsahaṃ 
 Ūkhā āniya taṃ annaṃ puno tasseva so adā 
  
     Tadantaṃ chaḍḍhayitvāna duṭṭhā buddhassahaṃ tadā 
 Pattaṃ kalalapuṇaṇaṃ taṃ adāsiṃ tassa tādino 
  
     Dāne ca gahaṇe ceva amejjhe padume yathā   
 Samacittamukhaṃ disvā tadāhaṃ saṃvijiṃ bhusaṃ 
                   
     Puno pantaṃ gahetvāna sodhayitvā sugandhinā 
 Pasannacittā puretvā saghataṃ sakkharaṃ adaṃ 
  
     Yattha yatthupapajjāmi surūpā homi dānato 
 Buddhassa apakārena   duggandhā vadanena ca 
  
     Puna kassapacirassa niṭṭhāyantamhi    cetiye 
 Sovaṇaṇaḍaṭṭhakavaraṃ adāsiṃ muditā ahaṃ 
  
   Te   machasaṃ the a   Pattaṃ   machasaṃ     katamaṭṭhaṃ   syā   Vata tattakaṃ   machasaṃ   Soṇaṇāsane paṭiṭṭhānaṃ   machasaṃ senāsane paṭiṭṭhānaṃ   syā senāsano paviṭṭhānaṃ   the a   Jātā kāsikagāmake   machasaṃ syā   Kaṇiyassa mama bhatatuno   simu machasaṃ kaṇiyaso   syā       Pāvadiṃ   simu machasaṃ   Apace padusepi ca   machasaṃ syā     majjhatatamanaso ahu   the a   Apasādena   the a    Niṭṭhāpentampi   the a 
  
                   
     Catujjāttena gandhena nivayitvā   tamiṭṭhakaṃ 
 Muttā duggandhadosambhā sabbaṅgasusamāgatā 
  
     Sattapānisahassāni rataneheva sattihi 
 Kāretvā ghatapurāni vaṭṭiyo   ca sahassaso 
  
     Pakkhipitvā padipetvā ṭhapayi   sattapantiyo 
 Pujatthaṃ   lokanāthassa vippasannena cetasā 
  
     Tadāpi tamhi puññamhi bhāginihaṃ visesato 
 Puna kāsisu sañajāto sumitto iti vissuto 
  
     Tassāhaṃ bhariyā sukhitā sajjitā piyā 
 Tadāpi paccekamunino adāsi   ghanaceṭhanaṃ 
  
     Tassāpi bhāgini āsiṃ moditvā dānamuttamaṃ 
 Punāpi kāsiraṭṭhambhi jāto koliyajātiyā 
  
     Tadā koliyaputtānaṃ satehi saha pañcahi 
 Pañca paccekabuddhānaṃ satānisamupaṭṭhahi 
  
     Temāsaṃ tappayitvāna   adāsi ca ticivaraṃ   
 Jāyā tassatadā āsiṃ puññakammapathānugāta 
                   
     Tato cuto ahu rājā nando nāma mahāyaso 
 Tassāpi mahesi āsiṃ sabbakāmasamiddhini 
  
     Tadā ca so   bhavitvāna brahmadatto mahipati 
 Padumavatiputtānaṃ paccekamuninaṃ tadā 
  
     Satānipañcanunāni yāvajīvaṃ upaṭṭhahi 
 Rājuyyāne nivāsetvā nibbutāni ca pujayi 
  
     Cetiyāni ca kāretvā pabbajitvā ubho mayaṃ 
 Bhāvevo appamaññāyo brahmalokaṃ aggambhase 
  
     Tato cuto mahātitthe sujāto pipphalāyano 
 Mātā sumanadeviti kosiyagotto dijo pitā 
  
   Temayitvā   syā the a   Vaṭṭini   machasaṃ the a   Ṭhapayiṃ   machasaṃ   Pujanatthaṃ   machasaṃ   Adāsiṃ   machasaṃ   Vāsayitvāna   syā       Pattacivare   the a   Tadā rājā   machasaṃ tato cuto   simu 
  
                   
     Ahaṃ maddajanapade sāgalāya puruttame 
 Kapilassa dijassāsiṃ dhītā mātā sucimati 
  
     Ghanakañcanabambena nimmiṇitvāna maṃ pitā 
 Adā kassapadhirassa kāmāsāvajjitassa   maṃ 
  
     Kadāci so kāruṇiko gantvā kammantapekkhanaṃ   
 Kākādikehi khajjante pāṇe disvāna saṃviji 
  
     Ghare cāhaṃ tile jāte disvānāpatāpane 
 Kimi kākehi khajjante saṃvegamalabhiṃ tadā 
  
     Tadā so pabbaji dhīro ahaṃ tamanupabbajiṃ 
 Pañca vassāni nivasiṃ paribbājavate   ahaṃ 
  
     Yadā pabbajitā āsi gotami jinaposikā 
 Tadāhaṃ tamupāgantvā buddhena anusāsitā 
  
     Na cireneva kālena arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
 Aho kalaṇāṇamittattaṃ kassapassa sirimato 
  
     Suto buddhassa dāyado kassapo susamāhito 
 Pubbanivasāṃ yo vedi saggāpāyañca passati 
                   
     Atho jātikkhayaṃ patto abhiññāvosito muni 
 Etāhi tihi vijjahi tevijjo hoti brāhmaṇo 
  
     Tatheva bhaddā kāpilāni tevijjā maccubhāyini 
 Dhāreti antimaṃ dehaṃ jetvā māraṃ savāhiniṃ 
  
     Disvā ādinavaṃ loke ubho pabbajitā mayaṃ 
 Tyambhā khiṇāsavā dantā sitibhūtāmha nibbutā 
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ bhaddākāpilāni bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Bhaddākāpilāni theriyāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
   Kāmehi   vajjitassa   machasaṃ syā the a   Pekkhako   machasaṃ syā       Paribbājapathe   syā     
  
                   
    Yasodharāpadānaṃ 
     Ekasmiṃ samaye ramma iddhe rājagahe pure 
 Pabbhārambhi varekasmiṃ vasante naranāyake 
  
     Vasantiyā tamhi nagare ramme bhikkhunupassaye 
 Yasodharā bhikkhunīyā evaṃ āsi vitakkitaṃ  
  
      Nando rāhulabhaddo ca sāvakaggā tatheva ca 
 Suddhodano mahārājā gotami ca pajāpati 
  
     Abhiññātā ca mahātherā theriyo ca mahiddhikā 
 Sattiṃ gatāva āsuṃ te dipacciva nirāsavā 
  
     Lokanāthe dharanteva ahampi ca sivaṃ padaṃ 
 Gamissāmi ti cintetvā passanti āyumattano 
     Passitvā āyusaṅkhāraṃ tadaheva khayaṃ gataṃ 
 Pattacivaramādāya nikkhamitvā sakassamā 
     Purakkhatā bhikkhunīhi satehi sahassehi sā   
 Mahiddhikā mahāpaññā sambuddhaṃ upasaṅkami 
  
     Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā satthuno cakkalakkhino 
 Nisinnā ekamantamhi idaṃ vacanamabravi 
  
      Aṭṭhasattativassāhaṃ pacchimo vattate vayo   
 Pabbhāraṃ hi   anupapattā ārocemi mahāmune 
  
     Paripakko vayo mayhaṃ pararittaṃ mama jīvitaṃ 
 Pahāya vo gamissāmi kataṃ me saraṇamatta 
  
     Vayaṃ hi   pacchime kāle maraṇaṃ uparundhati   
 Ajja rattiṃ mahāvīra pāpuṇissāmi nibbutiṃ 
  
   Satehi saha pañcahi   simu       Masasāmahi   simu   Pacchimā vattati vayā   syā   Pabbhāramahi   machasaṃ   Vayamhi   machasaṃ   Uparuddhati   machasaṃ uparujjhati   pujā 
  
                   
     Natthi jāti jarā vyādhi maraṇañca yahiṃ mune   
 Tattha gacchāmahaṃ vīra gato yattha na dissati   
  
     Yāvatā parisā ettha   samupāsanti satthuno 
 Aparādhaṃ pajānanti   khamantaṃ sammukhā mune 
                   
     Saṃsaritvā ca saṃsāre khalitaṃ ce mamaṃ tayi 
 Ārocemi mahāvīra aparādhaṃ khamassu me 
  
     Sutvāna tassā vacanaṃ munindo idamabravi 
 Kimuttaraṃ te cakkhāmi nibbānāya vajantiyā 
  
     Iddhiṃ cāpi nidassehi mama sāsanakārike 
 Parisānañca sabbāsaṃ kaṅkhaṃ chindassu sāne 
  
     Sutvā taṃ munino vācaṃ bhikkhunī sā yasodharā 
 Vanditvā munirājaṃ taṃ idaṃ vacanamabravi 
  
      Yasodharā ahaṃ vīra agāre te pajāpati 
 Sākiyambhi kule jātā itthiyaṅge patiṭṭhitā 
  
     Thinaṃ satahasassānaṃ navutinaṃ chaḷuttari   
 Agāre te ahaṃ vīra pāmokkhā sabbaisasarā 
  
     Rūpācāraguṇupetā yobbanaṭṭhā piyaṃvadā 
 Sabbā maṃ apacāyanti devatā viya mānusā 
  
     Kaññāsahassappamuṇā sakyaputtanivesane 
 Samānasukhadukkhā tā devatā viya nandane 
  
     Kāmadhātumatikkantā  saṇṭhitā rūpadhātuyā 
 Rūpena sadisā natthi ṭhapetvā lokanāyakaṃ  
  
     Evamādini vatvāna uppatitvāna ambaraṃ 
 Iddhi anekā dasessi buddhānuññā yasodharā   
  
   Mahāmune   machasaṃ   Ajarāmaṃ santipuraṃ gamissāmi asaṅkhataṃ   simu ajarāmaṃpuraṃ   machasaṃ   Nāma   simu machasaṃ   Sace metthi   simu aparādhamajānanti   machasaṃ   Chaduttari   machasaṃ   Kāmādhātumatikkamma   machasaṃ   machasaṃ   phasā gāthā na disasate apica ayaṃ gāthā dissate  sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā iddhiṃ dasessi satthuno nekā nānāvidhākārā mahāiddhipi dassayi  
  
                   
     Cakkavāḷasamaṃ kāyaṃ sīsaṃ uttarato kuru 
 Ubho pakkhā duve dipā jambudipo   sarirato 
  
     Dakkhiṇañca saraṃ piñajaṃ nānāsākhā tu pattakā 
 Cando ca suriyo akkhi   merupabbatato sikhā   
  
     Cakkavāḷagiri   tuṇḍaṃ   jamburukkhaṃ samulakaṃ 
 Vijamānā upāgantvā vandate lokanāyakaṃ 
  
     Hatthivaṇaṇaṃ tathevassaṃ pabbataṃ jaladhiṃ tathā 
 Vandimaṃ suriyaṃ meruṃ   sakkavaṇaṇañca dassayi 
                   
      Yasodharā ahaṃ cira pāde vandāmi cakkhuma  
 Sahassaṃ lokadhātunaṃ phullapadmena   chādayi 
  
     Brahmavaṇaṇañca māpetvā dhammaṃ desesi suññataṃ 
  Yasodharā ahaṃ cira pade vandāmi cakkhuma 
  
     Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi homi mahāmuni 
  
     Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sabbesavā parikkhiṇā nanthidāni punabbhavo 
  
     Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ mayhaṃ mahāvīra uppannaṃ tava santike 
  
     Buddhānaṃ lokanāthānaṃ saṅgamaṃ te   sudassitaṃ   
 Adhikāraṃ bahuṃ mayhaṃ tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
  
     Yaṃ mayhaṃ purimaṃ kammaṃ kusalaṃ sarase mune 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra puññaṃ upacitaṃ mayā 
  
     Abhabbaṭṭhāne vajjetvā vārayitvā anācaraṃ 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra sañcattaṃ jīvitaṃ mayā 
  
   Jamabudipā   sabbesuṃ   Vandañca suriyañcakkhi   machasaṃ si syā candasuriyavisālakkhi   pujā   Sikhaṃ   machasaṃ pujā   Giriṃ   machasaṃ   Tuṇḍā   pujā   Vandasuriyamahaṃmeruṃ   pujā   Thullapādena   pujā   Saṅgamanetasu   sima   Nidassitā   machasaṃ 
  
                   
     Nekakoṭisahassānaṃ bhariyathoyadāsi maṃ 
 Na tattha vimanā homi tuyhatthāya mahāmuni 
  
     Nekakoṭisahassānaṃ   upakārāyadāsi maṃ 
 Na tattha vimanā homi tuyhatthāya mahāmuni 
  
     Nekakoṭisahassānaṃ bhojanatthāyadāsi maṃ 
 Na tattha vimanā homi tuyhatthāya mahāmuni 
  
     Nekakoṭisahassāni jīvitāni pariccachiṃ 
 Bhayamokkhaṃ karissaṃ ti cajāmi   mama jīvitaṃ 
  
     Aṅgagate alaṅkāre vatthe nānāvidhe bahu itthimaṇḍe na guhāmi tuyhattāya mahāmuni 
                   
     Dhanadhaññapariccāgaṃ gāmāna nagamāni ca 
 Khetatā   puttā ca dhītā ca pariccattā mahumune 
  
     Hatthi assā gavā cāpi dāsiyo paricārikā 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra pariccattā asaṅkhiyā 
  
     Yaṃ mayhaṃ paṭimantesi   dānaṃ dassāmi yācake 
 Vimanaṃ me na passāmi dadato dānamuttamaṃ 
  
     Nānāvidhaṃ bahuṃ dukkhaṃ saṃsāre ca bahubbidhe 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra anubhuttaṃ asaṅkhiyā 
  
     Sukhappattā na modāmi na ca dukkhesu dummanā 
 Sabbattha tulitā homi tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
  
     Anumaggena sambuddho yaṃ dhammaṃ abhinihari 
 Anubhutvā sukhaṃ dukkhaṃ patto bodhiṃ mahāmuni 
  
     Buhmadevañca sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Aññesaṃ lokanāthānaṃ saṅgamā te bahu mayā 
  
   Sahasasāni   machasaṃ pujā   Dadāmi   machasaṃ   Khettaṃ   machasaṃ   Patimattesi   simu 
  
                   
     Adhikāraṃ bahuṃ mayhaṃ tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
 Gavesato buddhadhamme ahaṃ te paricārikā 
                   
      Kappe satasahasse ca caturo ca asaṅkhiye 
 Dipaṅkaro mahāvīro uppajji lokanāyako 
  
      Paccantadesaviseye nimantetvā tathāgataṃ 
 Tassa āgamana ṃmaggaṃ sodhenti tuṭṭhamānasā 
  
      Tena kālena so āsi sumedho nāma brāhmaṇo 
 Maggañca paṭiyādesi āyato   sabbadassino 
  
      Tena kālenahaṃ āsiṃ kaññā brāhmaṇasambhavā 
 Sumittā nāma nāmena upagañachiṃ samāgamaṃ 
  
      Aṭṭha uppalahatthāni pujanatthāya satthuno 
 Ādāya janasammejjha   addasaṃ isimugagataṃ 
                   
      Cirānupari āsinaṃ   atikantaṃ manoharaṃ 
 Disvā tadā amaññissaṃ  saphalaṃ jīvitaṃ mama  
  
      Parakkamaṃ taṃ saphalaṃ addasaṃ isino tadā 
 Pubbakammena sambuddhe vittañcāpi pasidi me 
  
      Bhiyyo cittaṃ pasādesiṃ ise uggatamānase   
 Deyyaṃ aññaṃ na passāmi demi pupphāni te ise 
  
      Pañca hatthā tava hontu tayo hontu mamaṃ ise 
 Tena siddhi   samā hotu   bodhatthāya tavaṃ ise 
   Bhāṇavāraṃ catutthaṃ   
  
      Isi gahetvā pupphāni āgacchantaṃ mahāyasaṃ 
 Pujesi janasammajjhe   bodhatthāya mahāisiṃ   
  
      Passitvā janasammajjhe dipaṅkaro mahāmuni 
 Viyākāsi mahāvīro isiṃ uggatamānasaṃ   
  
   Āyataṃ   simu   Janatāmajjhe   simu   Virānugataṃ dayitaṃ   machasaṃ syā   Isimahuggatamānase   simu   Saddhiṃ   machasaṃ syā   Hontu   machasaṃ   Janatāmajjhe   simu   Mahāisi   simu machasaṃ   imissānantaraṃ simu machasaṃ potthakesu ayaṃ gāthā dissate na tu pujāvaliyaṃ  aparimeyye ito kappe dipaṅkaro mahāmuni mama kammaṃ viyākāsi ujubhāvaṃ mahāmuni  
  
                   
      Samacittā samakammā samakāri bhavisasti 
 Piyā hessati kammenana tuyhatthāya mahāise   
  
      Sudassanā suppiyā   ca manāpā piyavādini 
 Tassa dhammesu dāyadā piyā hessati   itthikā 
  
      Yathāpi bhaṇḍasāmuggaṃ anurakkhanti   sāmino 
 Evaṃ kusaladhammānaṃ anurakkhissate ayaṃ 
  
      Tassa te   anukampanti purayissati pārami 
 Sihova pañajaraṃ hetvā   pāpuṇissati bodhiyaṃ 
  
      Aparimeyye ito kappe yaṃ maṃ buddho viyākari 
 Taṃ vācaṃ anumodanti evaṃkāri bhaviṃ ahaṃ 
                   
      Tassa kammassa sukatassa tattha cittaṃ pasādayiṃ 
 Devamānusakaṃ yoniṃ upapajja   asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
      Anubhotvā sukhaṃ dukkhaṃ devesu mānusesu ca 
 Pacchime bhave sampatte ajāyiṃ sākiye kule 
  
      Rūpavati bhogavati yasasilavati tathā 
 Sabbaṅgasampadā homi kusalesu atisakkatā 
  
      Lābhaṃ silokaṃ sakakāraṃ lokadhammasamāgamaṃ 
 Cittañca dukkhitaṃ natthi vasāmi akutobhayā 
  
      Nibbinditvāna saṃsāre pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Sahassaparivārena pabbajitvā akiñcanā 
  
      Agāraṃ vijahitvāna pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Addhamāse asampatte catusaccaṃ apāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Civaraṃ piṇḍapātaṃ ca paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ 
 Upanenti bahu teke sāgarasseva ūmiyo 
  
   Mahāisi   simu   Supiyā   machasaṃ   Viharissati   machasaṃ   Anurakkhati   machasaṃ   Maṃ   syā   Hitvā   si syā hetvā         Anubhotvā  simu machasaṃ 
  
                   
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ dukkhaṃ sampatti ca bahubbidhā 
 Visuddhabhāvaṃ sampattā labhāmi sabbasampadā 
  
      Sā dadāti sakattānaṃ puññatthāya mahesino 
 Sahāyasampadā honti nibbānapadamasaṅkhataṃ 
  
      Parikkhiṇaṃ atitaṃ ca pacacuppannaṃ anāgataṃ 
 Sabbaṃ kammaṃ mamaṃ khiṇaṃ pāde vandāmi cakkhumaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ yasodharā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sayodharātheriyāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
                   
      Dasabhikkhunīsahassāpadānaṃ 
      Kappe ca satasahasse caturo ca asaṅkhiye 
 Dīpaṅkaro nāma jino uppajji lokanāyako 
  
      Dipaṅkaro mahāvīro viyākāsi vināyako 
 Sumedhaṃ ca sumittaṃ ca samānasukhadukkhaṃ 
  
      Sadevakaṃ ca passantā civarantā sadevakaṃ 
 Tesaṃ pakittane amhe upagamma samāgamamaṃ   
  
      Amhaṃ sabbapati hohi   anāgatasamāgame 
 Sabbāva tuyahaṃ bhariyā manāpā piyavādikā 
  
      Dānasilamayaṃ sabbaṃ bhāvanā ca subhāvitā   
 Dīgharattaṃ ca no   sabbaṃ pariccatataṃ mahāmune 
  
   Sadevake   simu   Sabbā patibhonti         Bhāvanaṃ ca subhāvitaṃ         Mayaṃ       
  
                   
      Gandhaṃ vilepanaṃ mālaṃ dipaṃ ca ratanāmayaṃ 
 Yaṃ kiñci patthitaṃ sabbaṃ pariccattaṃ mahāmune 
  
      Aññaṃ cāpi kataṃ kammaṃ paribhogaṃ ca mānusaṃ 
 Dīgharattaṃ hi no sabbaṃ pariccattaṃ mahāmune 
  
      Anekajātisaṃsāraṃ bahuṃ puññaṃ hi no kataṃ 
 Issaramanubhotvāna saṃsaritvā bhavābhave 
  
      Pacchimahave sampatte sakyaputtanivesane 
 Nānākuluppanānāyo accharākāmavaṇaṇini 
  
      Lābhaggena yasaṃ pattā pujitā sabbasakkatā 
 Bābhiyo annapānānaṃ sadā sammānitā mayaṃ 
  
      Agāraṃ pajahitvāna pabbajitvāgāriyaṃ 
 Aḍḍhamāse asampatte sabbā pattāmaha nibbutiṃ 
  
      Lābhiyo annapānānaṃ vatthasenāsanāni ca 
 Upenti paccayā sabbe sadā sakkatapujitā 
                   
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ yasodharāpamukhāni dasabhikkhunīsahassāni bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Dasahibhikkhunīsahassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
                   
        Aṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahassāpadānaṃ 
      Aṭṭhārasasahassāni bhikkhunī sakyasambhavā 
 Yasodharāpamukhāti sambuddhaṃ upasaṅkamuṃ 
  
      Aṭṭhārasasahassāni sabbā honti mahiddhikā 
 Vandanti munino pāde ārocenti yathābalaṃ 
  
      Jāti khiṇā jarā vyādhi maranaṃ ca mahāmuni 
 Anāsavaṃ padaṃ santaṃ amataṃ yāma nāyaka 
  
      Khalitaṃ ce pure atthi sabbāsampi mahāmuni 
 Aparādhamajānanti   khama amhaṃ vināyaka 
  
       Iddhiṃ cāpi nidassetha mama sāsanakārikā 
 Parisānaṃ ca sabbāsaṃ kaṅkhaṃ chindatha yācatā  
  
      Yasodhari mahāvīra manāpā piyadassanā 
 Sabbā tuyhaṃ mahāvīra agārasmiṃ pajāpati 
  
      Thinaṃ satasahassānaṃ navutina chaḷuttari 
 Agāre te mayaṃ vīra pāmokkhā sabbaissarā 
  
      Rūpācāraguṇupetā yobbanaṭṭhā piyaṃvadā 
 Sabbāyo apacāyanti devatā viya mānusā 
  
      Aṭṭhārasasahassāni sabbā sākiyasambhavā 
 Yasodarā   sahassāni pāmokkhā issarā tadā 
                   
      Kāmadhātumatikkanattā saṇṭhitā rūpadhatuyā 
 Rūpena sadisā natthi sahassānaṃ 
      Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā iddhiṃ dassesu satthuno 
 Nekā   nānāvidhākārā mahāiddhipi dassayuṃ 
  
      Cakkavāḷasamaṃ kāyaṃ sisaṃ uttarato kuru 
 Ubho pakkhā duve dipā jambudipaṃ sarirato 
  
      Dakkhiṇaṃ ca saraṃ piñajaṃ nānāsākhā tu pattakā 
 Candasuravisālakkhā   merupabbatato sikhā 
  
   Aparādhaṃ pajānanti         Yasovati   si       Loke   simu   Candaṃ ca suriyaṃ vakkhi   machasaṃ     
  
                   
      Cakkavāḷagirituṇḍā jamburukkhaṃ samulakaṃ 
 Vijamānā upagantvā vandanti lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Hatthivaṇṇaṃ tathevassaṃ pabbataṃ jaladhiṃ tathā 
 Canda ca suriyaṃ meruṃ sakkavaṇṇaṃ ca dassayuṃ 
  
      Yasodharā mayaṃ vīra pāde candāma cakkhuma 
 Tava vīra pabhāvane nipphantā naranāyaka 
  
      Buddhisu ca vasi homa dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetoparāyañāṇassa vasi homa mahāmune 
  
      Pubbe nivāsaṃ jānāma dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sababāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ amhaṃ mahāvīra uppannaṃ tava sattike 
  
      Subbānaṃ lokanāthānaṃ saṅgamaṃ no nidassitaṃ 
 Adhikārā bahu ambhaṃ tumhatthāya mahāmune 
  
      Yaṃ amhaṃ purimaṃ kammaṃ kusalaṃ sarase mune 
 Tumhatthāya mahāvīra puññānupacitāni no 
  
      Abhabbaṭṭhāne vajjetvā vārayimaha anācaraṃ 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra cattāni jīvitāni no 
                   
      Nekakoṭisahassānaṃ bhariyatthāyadāsi no 
 Na tattha vimanā homa tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
  
      Nekakoṭisahassānaṃ upakārāyadāsi no 
 Na tattha vimanā homa tuyhatthā mahāmune 
  
      Nekakoṭisahassānaṃ bhojanatthāyadāsi no 
 Na tattha vimanā homa tuyhatthā mahāmune 
  
      Nekakoṭisahassāni jīvitāni vajimbha no 
 Bhayamokkhaṃ karissāma jīvitāni cajimha se 
  
      Aṅgagate alaṅkāre vatthe nānāvidhe bahu 
 Itthibhaṇḍe na guhāma tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
  
                   
      Dhanadhaññapariccāgaṃ gāmāni nigamāni ca 
 Khettā puttā ca dhītā ca pariccattā   mahāmune 
  
      Hatthi assā gavā cāpi   dāsiyo paricārikā 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra pariccatatā asaṅkhiyā   
  
      Yaṃ amhe paṭimantesi dānaṃ dassāma yācake 
 Vimanaṃ no na passāma dadato dānamuttamaṃ 
  
      Nānāvidhaṃ bahuṃ dukkhaṃ saṃsāre ca bahubadhe 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra anubhuttaṃ asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
      Sukhappattā na modāma   na ca dukkhesu dummanā 
 Sabbattha tulitā homa tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
  
      Anumaggena sambuddho yaṃ dhammaṃ abhinihari 
 Anubhutvā sukhaṃ dukkhaṃ patto bodhiṃ mahāmuni 
  
      Brahmadevaṃ ca sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Aññesaṃ lokanāthānaṃ saṅgamā tehi no bahu 
  
      Adhikārā bahu amhaṃ   tuyhatthā mahāmune 
 Gavesato buddhadhamme mayaṃ te paricārikā 
  
      Kappe ca sahatahasse caturo ca asaṅkhiye 
 Dipaṅkaro mahāvīro uppajji lokanāyako 
  
      Paccantadesavisaye nimantetvā tathāgataṃ 
 Tassa āgamanaṃ maggaṃ sodhenti tuṭṭhamānasā 
  
      Tena kālena so āsi sumodho nāma brāhmaṇo 
 Maggeṃ ca paṭiyādesi āyataṃ   sabbadasisano 
                   
      Tena kālena āsimbha sabbā brāhmaṇasambhavā 
 Thaludajāni pupphāni āharimbha samāgamaṃ 
  
      Tasmiṃ so samaye buddho dipaṅkaro mahāyaso 
 Viyākāsi mahāvaro isimuggatamānasaṃ 
  
   Khettaṃ putataṃ ca dhitaṃ ca pariccattaṃ         Hatthiassaṃgavaṃ cāpi         Pariccattaṃ asaṃkhiyaṃ         Numodāma   machasaṃ   Adhikāraṃ bahuṃ ameha         Āyato   machasaṃ     
  
                   
      Calati racati paṭhavi saṅkampati sadevakaṃ 
 Tassa kammaṃ pakittente isinuggatamānaso   
  
      Devakaññā manussā ca mayaṃ cāpi sadevakā 
 Nānāpujaniyaṃ bhaṇḍaṃ pujayitvāna patthayuṃ 
  
      Tesaṃ buddho viyākāsi jotidipasanāmako 
  Ajja ye patthitā atthi te bhavissanti sammukhā  
  
      Aparimeyye ito kappe yaṃ no buddho viyākari 
 Taṃ vācamanumodanti evaṅkāri ahumha no 
  
      Tassa kammassa sukatassa tattha cittaṃ pasādiya   
 Devamānusakaṃ yoni anubhotvā asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
      Sukhadukkhenubhotvāna devesu mānusesu ca 
 Pacchimabhave sampatte jātāmbha sākiye kule 
  
      Rūpati bhogavati yasasilavati tato 
 Sabbaṅgasampadā homa kulesu atisakkatā 
  
      Lābhaṃ silokaṃ sakkāraṃ lokadhammasamāgamaṃ 
 Cittaṃ ca dukkhitaṃ natthi vasāma akutobhayā 
  
      Vuttaṃ hetaṃ bhagavatā rañño antepare tadā 
 Khattiyānaṃ pure viro upakāraṃ ca niddasi 
  
      Upakārā ca yā nāri yā ca nāri sukhe dukhe 
 Atthakkhāyi ca yā nāri yā ca nārinukampikā 
                   
      Dhammaṃ care sucaritaṃ na naṃ duccaritaṃ care 
 Dhammacāri sukhaṃ seti asmiṃ loke parambhi ca 
  
      Agāraṃ vijahitvāna pabbajimbhanagāriyaṃ 
 Aḍḍhamāse asampatte catusaccaṃ phusimbha no 
  
      Civaraṃ piṇḍapātaṃ ca paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ 
 Upanenti bahuṃ ambhe sāgarasseva ūmiyo 
  
   Isimuggata mānasaṃ   machasaṃ       Pasādayuṃ   simu 
  
                   
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ dukkhaṃ sampatti ca bahubbidhā 
 Visuddhabhāvaṃ sampannā labhāma sabbasampadā 
  
      Yā dadanti sakattānaṃ puññatthāya mahesino 
 Sahāyasampadā honti nibbānapadamasaṅkhataṃ 
  
      Parikkhiṇaṃ atitaṃ ca pacacuppannaṃ anāgataṃ 
 Sabbaṃ kammampi no khiṇaṃ pāde candāma cakkhuma 
  
      Nibbānāya vajantinaṃ kiṃ vo cakkhāma uttariṃ 
 Santasaṅkhatadosaṃ hi pappotha amataṃ padaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ yasodharāpamukhāni aṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahassāni bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Yasodharāpamukhaaṭṭhārasabhikukhunisahassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
 Kuṇḍalakesivaggo tatiyo 
  
 Tatthuddānaṃ 
 Kuṇḍalā gotami ceva dhammadinnā ca sakulā 
 Caranandā soṇā ca kāpilāni yasodharā 
 Dasasahassabhikkhunī aṭṭhārasasahassakā 
 Gāthāsatāni cattāri cha ca sattani meva ca 
                   
                   
       Yasavatipamukhabhikkhunīnaṃ apadānaṃ 
      Bhavā sabbe parikkhiṇā bhavasandhi vimocitā 
 Sabbāsavā ca no natthi ārocema mahāmune 
  
      Purimaṃ kusalaṃ kammaṃ yaṃ kiñci sādhu patthitaṃ 
 Paribhogamayaṃ dinnaṃ tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
  
      Buddhapaccekabuddhānaṃ buddhānaṃ sāvakānana ca 
 Paribhogamayaṃ dinnaṃ tuyahatthāya mahāmune 
  
      Uccanicamayaṃ kammaṃ bhikkhunaṃ sādhu patthitaṃ 
 Uccākulaparikamamaṃ katametaṃ mahāmune 
  
      Teneva sukkamūlena coditā kammasampadā 
 Mānusikamatikkantā jāyiṃsu khattiye kule 
  
      Uppatte ca kate kamme jātiyā cāpi ekato 
 Paccime ekato jātā khattiyā kulasambhavā 
  
      Rūpavati bhogavati lābhasakkārapujitā 
 Antepure māvira devānaṃ viya nandane 
  
      Nibbinditvā agārambhā pabbajimhanagāriyaṃ 
 Katipāhaṃ upādāya sababā pattāmha nibbuti 
  
      Civaraṃ paṇḍapātaṃ ca paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ 
 Upanenti bahu ambe sadā sakkatapujitā 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ yasavatipamukhāni aṭṭhāsakhattiyakaññā bhikkhunīssāni bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Yasavatipumukhaaṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahasāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
                   
                   
       Brahmaṇakaññābhikkhunīnaṃ apadānaṃ 
      Cullāsitisahassāni brahmaññakulasambhavā 
 Sukhumālahatthapādā pure tuyhaṃ mahāmune 
  
      Vessasuddakule jātā devā nāgā ca kintarā 
 Cātuddipā bahu kaññā pure tuyahaṃ mahāmune 
  
      Keci pabbajitā atthi saccadassāvino bahu 
 Devā ca kintarā nāgā khujjhissanti anāgate 
  
      Anubhotvā yasaṃ sabbaṃ satvāna sabbasampadā 
 Tvasi pasādaṃ paṭiladdhā bujjhissanti anāgate 
  
      Ambhe brāhmaṇadhitā tu brahmaññakulasambhavā 
 Pekkhato no mahāvīra pāde vandama cakkhuma 
  
      Upahatā bhavā sabbe mulataṇhā samuhatā 
 Samucchinnā anusayā puññasaṅkhārā dālitā 
  
      Samādhigocarā sabbā samāpattivasi tathā 
 Jhānena dhammaratiyā viharissāma no sadā 
  
      Bhavanetti avijjā ca saṅkhārāpi ca khepitā 
 Sududdasaṃ padaṃ gantuṃ anujānātha nāyaka 
  
      Upakārā mamaṃ tumbhe digharattaṃ katāvino 
 Bahuttaṃ saṃsayaṃ chetvā sabbā gacchantu   nibbutiṃ 
  
      Vanditvā munino pāde katvā iddhivikubbaṇaṃ 
 Kāci dassenti ālokaṃ andhakāramathāparā 
  
      Dassenti candasuriye sāgaraṃ ca samacchakaṃ 
 Sineruparibhaṇḍaṃ ca dassenti pārichattakaṃ 
  
   Gacchata       
  
                   
      Tāvatiṃsaṃ ca bhavanaṃ yāmaṃ dassenti iddhiyā 
 Tusitaṃ nimmite deve vasavatti mahissare 
      Buhmāno kāci dassenti caṅkamaṃ ca mahārahaṃ 
 Brahmavaṇṇaṃ ca māpetvā dhammaṃ desenti suññataṃ 
  
      Nānāvikubbaṇaṃ katvā iddhiṃ dasasiya patthuno 
 Dassāyiṃsu khalaṃ sabbā pade vandiṃsu satthuno 
                   
      Iddhisu ca vasi homa dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi homa mahāmune 
  
      Iddhisu ca vasi homa dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā nathidoni punabbhavo 
  
      Atthadhamamaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ ambhaṃ mahāvīra uppannaṃ tava santike 
  
      Pubbānaṃ lokanāthānaṃ saṅgamaṃ no nidassitaṃ 
 Adhikārā bahu ambhaṃ tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
  
      Yaṃ ambhehi kataṃ kammaṃ kusalaṃ sarataṃ mune 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra puññānupacitāni no 
  
      Yaṃ ambhehi kataṃ kammaṃ kusalaṃ sarataṃ mune 
 Puraṃ haṃsavati nāma sambuddhassa kulāsayaṃ 
  
      Dvārena haṃsavatiyā gaṅgā sandati sababadā 
 Ubbāḷha nadiyā bhikkhu gamanaṃ na labhantite 
  
      Divasaṃ dve tayo ceva sattāhaṃ māsakaṃ tato
